
-----title
成都 (出生地)
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年7月</a>　秋闱中举。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='39752157395141d389282be03db5fbe2_label'><a href='javascript: gray;'>▪</span>年初，在成都，知府张涛离任，作诗送之。作品：《送张涛景元》<div id='poem_502690' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_502690' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/502690?labeling=true' "poem_title_502690")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_502690_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_502690'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_502690'>方域提权重，朝廷择士尊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_502690_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_502690'>纲疏因正纪，流洁为澄源。<div id='poem_sentence_1_502690_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_502690'>寒日风威静，熙阳气序温。<div id='poem_sentence_2_502690_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_502690'>人知廉使体，物荷圣皇恩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_502690_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_502690'>清辔才周境，归途已驾辕。<div id='poem_sentence_4_502690_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_502690'>光华三节瑞，邃密九重阍。<div id='poem_sentence_5_502690_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_502690'>韶集丹山凤，云升北海鲲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_502690_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_502690'>闻公难避让，天下尽元元。<div id='poem_sentence_7_502690_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_502690'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_502690_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>作《送张子公》诗。<div id='poem_502610' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_502610' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/502610?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送张子公</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_502610")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_502610_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_502610'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_502610'>康定用兵日，府谷尤孤危。<div id='poem_sentence_0_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_502610'>属当治安久，多事尽废隳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_502610'>三面枕贼境，平易如通逵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_502610'>重城辄议葺，浮论多背驰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_502610'>贤哉光禄公，定虑先本基。<div id='poem_sentence_4_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_502610'>百堵大兴作，据险成藩篱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_502610'>城完贼已至，善守莫敢窥。<div id='poem_sentence_6_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_502610'>泉源众所汲，公为亲解围。<div id='poem_sentence_7_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_502610'>兵势弱不振，公能屡张威。<div id='poem_sentence_8_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_502610'>贼退城可处，生聚始有归。<div id='poem_sentence_9_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_502610'>于今三十年，功勋书鼎彝。<div id='poem_sentence_10_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_502610'>边人每记忆，言者感涕挥。<div id='poem_sentence_11_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_502610'>近日羽书至，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_502610", 502610, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>讨伐</span>加羌夷。<div id='poem_sentence_12_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_502610'>庙算出帷幄，王师整熊罴。<div id='poem_sentence_13_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_502610'>壮夫思报国，志士窃忧时。<div id='poem_sentence_14_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_502610'>寒日朝惨淡，凄风夜号悲。<div id='poem_sentence_15_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_502610'>昔人何卓荦，往事可追维。<div id='poem_sentence_16_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_502610'>夫君实贤嗣，仕宦图奋飞。<div id='poem_sentence_17_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_502610'>家声贵不坠，儒学当有为。<div id='poem_sentence_18_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_502610'>归欤自磨砺，门阀增光辉。<div id='poem_sentence_19_502610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年4月</a>　朝廷令吕陶往成都府与转运司议定役法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年5月</a>　论劾张璪、李琮、王子韶等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年5月</a>　奏苏缄子苏子元换武官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年9月</a>　苏轼为翰林学士，作启贺之。作品：《贺苏内翰启》<div id='poem_1181044' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181044' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181044?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺苏内翰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181044")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181044_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181044'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181044'>伏审光膺制命，进直禁林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181044_comment'></div>盖朝廷以斯文为难，必咨间杰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181044_comment'></div>而天下知公议所属，共激欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181044_comment'></div>恭惟某官道造本元，才周<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1181044", 1181044, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>贯变</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181044_comment'></div>语默系时之休戚，出处为国之重轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181044_comment'></div>密告嘉猷，务引君而当道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181044_comment'></div>总司大计，期节用以裕民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181044_comment'></div>远业寖施，贵名增重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181044_comment'></div>深被中宸之遇，延登内相之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181044_comment'></div>惟仁经义纬之成文，庶几同于三代；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181044_comment'></div>况前兄后弟之接武，盛事萃于一门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181044_comment'></div>将倚全谟，共敷元化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181044_comment'></div>某远从吏役，恭听恩俞，趋庆莫缘，瞻风载抃。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1181044_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='5ad8aa11f4f440a9a11fe5210901cc0b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5ad8aa11f4f440a9a11fe5210901cc0b");'><span id='5ad8aa11f4f440a9a11fe5210901cc0b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1091')">1090-1091年</a>，63-64岁</div><div id='5ad8aa11f4f440a9a11fe5210901cc0b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年1月28日</a>　改任成都府路转运副使。有谢表。作品：《上谢成都府路转运副使表》<div id='poem_1180990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢成都府路转运副使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1090年1月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180990")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180990_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180990'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180990'>臣陶言：进奏院递到告命一道，伏蒙圣恩，就差臣权成都府路转运副使，已于今月七日到任讫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180990_comment'></div>转输淮甸，既受命以之官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180990_comment'></div>廉按坤维，遽叨恩而易地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180990_comment'></div>宠章特异，感涕交流<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180990_comment'></div>伏念臣早以疏凡，误蒙役使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180990_comment'></div>备员台省，预闻国论之几微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180990_comment'></div>赐对帘帷，屡奉德音之奖训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180990_comment'></div>一违朝缀，四涉年华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180990_comment'></div>甘簿领之沉迷，事道途之奔走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180990_comment'></div>抗章宸戾，少希恻怛之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180990_comment'></div>得请乡邦，极享便安之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180990_comment'></div>此盖太皇太后陛下德由坤载，道济离明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180990_comment'></div>有任贤使能之心，愿登至治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180990_comment'></div>无泄迩忘远之意，昭示大公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180990_comment'></div>终赐矜怜，俾尘寄任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180990_comment'></div>况岷峨之列壤，乃桑梓之旧封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180990_comment'></div>入境观风，情伪同于指掌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180990_comment'></div>过家上冢，岁时得以荐诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180990_comment'></div>恩实光华，力难报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1180990_comment'></div>臣敢不致勤夙夜，积虑简书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1180990_comment'></div>有以澄清，虽愧古人之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1180990_comment'></div>近于忠厚，敢忘君子之风？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1180990_comment'></div>庶集涓劳，仰酬化力。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1180990_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年1月</a>　再上谢表。作品：《又谢成都府路转运副使表》<div id='poem_1180991' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180991' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180991?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又谢成都府路转运副使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1090年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180991")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180991_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180991'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180991'>王事言私，盖犯辞难之义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180991_comment'></div>天心垂宥，特推从欲之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180991_comment'></div>就畀漕符，即居乡闬，深惭委任，俯切兢惶<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180991_comment'></div>伏念臣生长寒乡，栖迟冗路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180991_comment'></div>虽曰为贫而愿仕，曷尝枉己以求容？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180991_comment'></div>亲逢纳谏之朝，屡伸狂瞽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180991_comment'></div>深体裕民之意，久莅输将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180991_comment'></div>何补涓尘，仅逃罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180991_comment'></div>辄露由衷之请，茍希恤隐之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180991_comment'></div>亟奉诏谕，仍叨使领，罢淮壖之奔走，遂井络之便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180991_comment'></div>自省孤根，极知幸会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180991_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下尧仁天覆，汤德日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180991_comment'></div>以四海为一家，视兆民如赤子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180991_comment'></div>敷施大信，役驭万官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180991_comment'></div>付臣以故里之行，责臣以远方之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180991_comment'></div>地产之盈虚可度，物情之美恶粗知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180991_comment'></div>郡邑相望，如在户庭之内；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180991_comment'></div>松楸密迩，每宽霜露之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180991_comment'></div>窃禄于兹，厚颜已甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1180991_comment'></div>臣敢不布宣惠泽，申饬教条，勤恤疲氓，力绳慢吏，期得富饶之实，预防废弛之端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1180991_comment'></div>倘于父母之邦，可安其职，则报君亲之赐，无愧此生。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1180991_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年6月</a>　苏辙荐陶等为谏官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年8月</a>　贾易劾苏轼、苏辙结吕陶等为党与。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　任成都府路转运副使。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ab03c3120d854466af4aa3c3deed0d1e_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　致仕，有谢表。作品：《谢致仕表》<div id='poem_1181012' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181012' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181012?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢致仕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181012")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181012_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181012'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181012'>齿发衰残，义当告老；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181012_comment'></div>丝纶焕赫，恩许归休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181012_comment'></div>荷君父之始终，全臣子之进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181012_comment'></div>敬承俞命，感激危心<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181012_comment'></div>伏念臣起迹至寒，逢辰过幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181012_comment'></div>早竭簿书之力，徒自沉迷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181012_comment'></div>晚叨侍从之班，讫无补报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181012_comment'></div>侵寻暮境，眷恋故乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181012_comment'></div>辄申谢事之诚，觊遂乞骸之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181012_comment'></div>仰烦睿鉴，俯察愚衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181012_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下舜道用中，尧仁济众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181012_comment'></div>如天地阴阳之造，不间于微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181012_comment'></div>虽虫鱼草木之生，亦从其欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181012_comment'></div>因而衰朽，得遂休閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181012_comment'></div>臣即解郡章，言旋故里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181012_comment'></div>想天颜之睟穆，难睹清光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181012_comment'></div>咏化日之舒长，敢忘帝力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181012_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1181012_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　有答启。作品：《答简州知郡杨朝请启》<div id='poem_1181060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181060?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答简州知郡杨朝请启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181060")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181060'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181060'>比者起于发放，贲以宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181060_comment'></div>得郡还家，难补邦人之徯望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181060_comment'></div>胜笺讲好，过烦才哲之抚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181060_comment'></div>观礼意之勤隆，异世途之流薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181060_comment'></div>第增感服，奚极叙畅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181060_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1181060_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　有贺启。作品：《贺简州知郡杨朝请启》<div id='poem_1181061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺简州知郡杨朝请启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181061")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181061'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181061'>伏审考绩推先，颁恩示劝，陟郎曹之前列，沸郡境之欢声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181061_comment'></div>恭惟某官茂器承家，远材适治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181061_comment'></div>要涂更践，惟娴循吏之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181061_comment'></div>华步超迁，允被盛朝之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181061_comment'></div>行期异日，自陟迩联。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1181061_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　诸友贺致仕，有谢启。作品：《谢诸公贺致仕启》<div id='poem_1181062' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181062' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181062?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢诸公贺致仕启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181062")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181062_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181062'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181062'>齿发衰残，义当避退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181062_comment'></div>名勋焕赫，恩许归休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181062_comment'></div>于君臣之际，幸而有终；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181062_comment'></div>于朋友之功，岂为无助？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181062_comment'></div>此盖某官至诚嗟恤，雅度并包。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181062_comment'></div>知其勉强不前，未尝深责；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181062_comment'></div>使之安完而去，可乐馀生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181062_comment'></div>重委笺修，曲存轸念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181062_comment'></div>且引年谢事，庶几免贤者之诮，义所宜然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181062_comment'></div>而杜门养疾，聊以待终焉之期，礼无足贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181062_comment'></div>褒嘉所及，愧惧莫胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181062_comment'></div>方羸疹之缠绵，想门庭之阻邈，欣闻所教，书不尽言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1181062_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　致仕居家。作《回成都监司启》<div id='poem_1181063' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181063' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181063?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回成都监司启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181063")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181063_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181063'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181063'>隆恩遣使，朝廷委宪度之成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181063_comment'></div>清辔戒涂，郡邑仰光华之远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181063_comment'></div>式钦茂业，良抃下悰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181063_comment'></div>夙觌风徽，尝亲诲语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181063_comment'></div>方幸退藏于里巷，未由趋集于宾除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181063_comment'></div>向望实勤，叙扬奚悉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181063_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1181063_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　致仕居家。作《代贺范相公启》<div id='poem_1181064' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181064' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181064?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代贺范相公启<span class='inlineComment2'>（尧夫）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181064")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181064_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181064'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181064'>器兼文武，道备天人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181064_comment'></div>始列周行，绰有栋梁之器；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181064_comment'></div>及参大政，蔚为社稷之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181064_comment'></div>果振家声，遂当国相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181064_comment'></div>昔韦、平嗣兴于西汉，袁、杨继起于东京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181064_comment'></div>张公锡延赏之名，陆氏取象先之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181064_comment'></div>虽云华族，未必熙朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181064_comment'></div>然犹前史以为美谈，当世谓之荣事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181064_comment'></div>固未有百年遇太平之运，四时膺爰立之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181064_comment'></div>以今言之，一何盛也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181064_comment'></div>某夙登门仞，尝颂威容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181064_comment'></div>念班谒以无由，第承风而窃抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181064_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1181064_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　作杜诲求墓志铭。作品：《朝请郎潼川府路提点刑狱杜诲求公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181136' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181136' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181136?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝请郎潼川府路提点刑狱杜公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181136")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181136_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181136'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181136'>吾友杜公，讳敏求，字趣翁，其先出于唐杜氏，历世有显人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181136_comment'></div>盖西汉御史大夫曰周，东汉谏议大夫曰穰，晋有恕、有预，皆名臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181136_comment'></div>洎唐之盛，为宰相者十一人，子孙又以文章显者，有曰审言，审言生闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181136_comment'></div>闲生甫，字子美，肃宗时以右拾遗论事忤旨，出为华州司功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181136_comment'></div>会关、陕凶歉，弃官流落剑南，居成都西郊，严武待之甚厚，表为节度参谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181136_comment'></div>久之，崔旰乱，甫往来二蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181136_comment'></div>至大历初，南下沅、湘，卒于耒阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181136_comment'></div>甫初娶司农少卿杨怡女，生二子，及下江陵，留二子守成都籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181136_comment'></div>杨子琳之乱，避患奔眉之东山大垭，因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181136_comment'></div>其后族属蕃衍，遂为郡大姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181136_comment'></div>后有葬青神者，遂为青神人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181136_comment'></div>公之曾大父光期，隐晦不仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181136_comment'></div>大父允升，以文行推高于众，为乡先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181136_comment'></div>父万，静默守道，笃好经史，由公贵，赠朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181136_comment'></div>妣宋氏，赠昌国县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181136_comment'></div>公幼禀颖秀，不与群儿类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181136_comment'></div>在襁褓时，每见字书，辄喜动于色，或指而道之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181136_comment'></div>幼教以班固史，遂能记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181136_comment'></div>七岁尝赋《闵雨诗》，有「农夫苦相问，燮理是何人」之句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181136_comment'></div>年十八，问学该赡，尝应进士试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181136_comment'></div>眉素多士，试者二千人，能合于式度中选者，数止二十，由是人人竞衒所蕴，以争能决胜于一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181136_comment'></div>有司深慎去取，莫不搜索隐奥，标而为题，明经中选，或于题有所不知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181136_comment'></div>公凡两试，每临为一词，则详尽意谓，贲以辞藻，选在甲乙，乃登嘉祐六年进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181136_comment'></div>授简州司理参军，徙绵州西昌，判州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181136_comment'></div>寻而丁大夫公忧，除服，知汉州什邡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181136_comment'></div>嘉州犍为泺骤激入江，有罗护滩据险奔激，屡为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181136_comment'></div>公导而通之，至今民赖以济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181136_comment'></div>赖田寨控羌夷，率以武弁领之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181136_comment'></div>公至未期月，主者数以夷人相侵扰为告，意在开边隙以要赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181136_comment'></div>公揣知其情，不答，而告至不已，公曰：「某虽不肖，来临此邦，羌人未必我欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181136_comment'></div>他日茍有患，吾自任其责」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181136_comment'></div>已而终公之去，竟无他警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181136_comment'></div>邑人孙熙祖险猾慢上，县官稍不假借，辄造作飞语，欲中伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1181136_comment'></div>前后来者，往往悦以美言，幸无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1181136_comment'></div>公将抉剔其恶而诛锄之，终公之去，更不敢涉县境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1181136_comment'></div>以昌国君忧去职，既除丧，屏处里舍，悢然有不愿仕之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1181136_comment'></div>部使荐之，就监成都商税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1181136_comment'></div>成都市征，岁多羡入，至者往往苛敛以觊赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1181136_comment'></div>公独不然，务职举以办事，耻削民以希进，于是上下两得，民甚乐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1181136_comment'></div>元祐中，以十科进擢天下士，命近臣荐而后用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1181136_comment'></div>时荐公者十数人，既还阙，未尝一言闻于人，乃诣吏部，拟润州通判以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1181136_comment'></div>或告之曰：「公德望之重，十科所荐尤多，傥诣丞相，当得美仕，何不审为计，而遽归乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1181136_comment'></div>公曰：「富贵穷达，固有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1181136_comment'></div>吾读书闻道踰四十年，未尝求知于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1181136_comment'></div>茍有知者，皆自相知耳，何暇修辞令，俛颜色，汲汲自媒以取辱哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1181136_comment'></div>执政惜其所守如此，不得已，除公成都府教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1181136_comment'></div>公闻命，喜甚，促装而西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1181136_comment'></div>官满，执政见其姓名，问同列，曰：「是尝除成都学官，欣然而去，而未尝识之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1181136_comment'></div>若人安恬静退，岂须识其面目而后用之乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1181136_comment'></div>即日除太学博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1181136_comment'></div>自熙宁、元丰以来，士专一经，或略去文学，及委公撰堂试策目，乃条析班、马之学以询之，自是诸生稍稍习史传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1181136_comment'></div>未几，罢词赋，复以经术取士，公曰：「吾昔以诗赋举进士，故在此选，今用非所长，安能屑屑务向背以徇合于人乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1181136_comment'></div>即请于朝，求罢去，改差通判定州，在韩公师朴幕府，事无巨细，多以委公，公率以仁恕忠厚补之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1181136_comment'></div>韩公尝谓同僚曰：「吾与治中君性相若，气相投，无异兄弟，但姓不同耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1181136_comment'></div>有掾曹以母疾赴官淹缓，众皆难之，公为出力必争，毅然不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1181136_comment'></div>徐诘之，乃故右辖胡公婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1181136_comment'></div>公告韩公曰：「万里从官，以母疾后期，不失为孝子，又况胡公婿乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1181136_comment'></div>某素受胡公之知深，傥不一言，他日泉下何面目见之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1181136_comment'></div>竟使就职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1181136_comment'></div>韩公叹曰：「笃于风义至如此，可为薄俗戒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1181136_comment'></div>元符初，除广汉太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1181136_comment'></div>京居仅二年，掩关读书，未尝妄与人交一言，士论伟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1181136_comment'></div>今上即位覃霈，迁朝请郎，除梓州路转运判官，就移提点刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1181136_comment'></div>识者谓朝廷将大用，俄感疾，乞致仕，卒于官，享年六十有三，实建中靖国元年八月二十日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1181136_comment'></div>公初娶太原王氏，崇德县君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1181136_comment'></div>再娶郭氏，旌德县君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1181136_comment'></div>又娶郭氏，长安县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1181136_comment'></div>二子：长曰端方，博学孝友，公笃爱之，先公十五年卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1181136_comment'></div>次曰续，今才六岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1181136_comment'></div>女三人：长适进士孙燮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1181136_comment'></div>次适新授成都郫县主簿张澈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1181136_comment'></div>季适进士郭琛，而先亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1181136_comment'></div>孙男一人，曰嗣老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1181136_comment'></div>将以崇宁某年二月二十三日葬于玉台乡敦教里，举长安君及端方之丧而祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1181136_comment'></div>有文集三十卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1181136_comment'></div>公仕宦四十年，未尝殖产，或劝之，则曰：「君独不闻萧相国所谓『令后世贤，师吾俭』乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1181136_comment'></div>使没于利者闻之，当足以自警，故今西南指士大夫廉洁者，必推以为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1181136_comment'></div>既丧，梓人哀其贫，赒以赗赠，孀妇诸孤号且诉曰：「先君子昔以礼义自持，终身未尝一毫取于人，今不幸至大故，虽贫甚，宁寒饿以死，敢纳人之遗，以累其清白耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1181136_comment'></div>辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1181136_comment'></div>闻者深嘉之，以为非公廉洁自处，素信于其家，安能至是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1181136_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1181136_comment'></div>予从公最久，知公最详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1181136_comment'></div>方少时学有原本，文辞纯明博赡，谓其可以标范后来，故爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1181136_comment'></div>既壮而仕，则闻其治有体要，重民贵义，谓其可以扩而充之，以及远大，非特区区郡县耳，故畏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1181136_comment'></div>及见其信道守己，愈老益坚，不以一毫屈于物，而觊尺寸之茍获，然亦竟不为时用，故惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1181136_comment'></div>又悲其平生患难，死亡憔悴，岁月相继，将卒而子尚幼，已死而家尤贫，诸孤尚不忍茍得，以累其素履，可谓贤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1181136_comment'></div>天地之报施善人吉士，果可知邪，果不可知邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1181136_comment'></div>予又闻，昔者孔子论死生之际，则曰：「知生而不知死，吊而不伤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1181136_comment'></div>知死而不知生，伤而不吊」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1181136_comment'></div>至「朋友之丧，则亦吊于寝门之外」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1181136_comment'></div>斯皆要以恩义而归诸礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1181136_comment'></div>予于公既吊而又伤之，哭于寝门之外，而又铭之，孰谓非礼欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1181136_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1181136'>终始从公，可得而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1181136_comment'></div>义操于我，从容典彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1181136_comment'></div>德爱在物，涵濡咏嘻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1181136_comment'></div>吊且伤矣，曷穷予悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1181136_comment'></div>大山之垭，青江之湄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1181136_comment'></div>著信以铭，云乎庶几。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1181136_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　向新知成都府胡资政上贺启。作品：《贺新知成都府胡资政启 》<div id='poem_1181065' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181065' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181065?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新知成都胡资政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181065")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181065_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181065'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181065'>伏审法扆畴庸，制函申命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181065_comment'></div>易宛丘之巨镇，领全蜀之要权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181065_comment'></div>一发宠章，交流欢颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181065_comment'></div>恭惟某官至诚自任，大节不欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181065_comment'></div>以道德文章为经国之远猷，以法度纪纲为致君之先务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181065_comment'></div>四邻作辅，独高治世之典刑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181065_comment'></div>九命出藩，尤重远方之形势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181065_comment'></div>即闻温綍，复秉洪钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181065_comment'></div>某早拜下风，宿闻馀教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181065_comment'></div>仰朝廷之图任，窃幸依仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181065_comment'></div>知乡党之蒙休，敢先致庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181065_comment'></div>愿言欣咏，奚极叙扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181065_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1181065_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　作《答家朝请谢转官启》<div id='poem_1181066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181066?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答家朝请谢转官启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181066")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181066'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181066'>伏审天官考绩，法扆霈恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181066_comment'></div>循格有常，迁官示宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181066_comment'></div>恭惟某官内崇德本，旁贯治源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181066_comment'></div>贤业周施，宜坦云霄之步；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181066_comment'></div>禄阶叙进，荣酬日月之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181066_comment'></div>仰承君命之光华，聊助亲闱之喜乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181066_comment'></div>遽烦隆礼，特贶珍题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181066_comment'></div>感抃交深，布宣奚极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181066_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1181066_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年9月</a>　九月，入元祐党籍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年9月29日</a>　九月二十九日，罢职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　卒于家。<br /></div>

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　寓居开封，吕诲罢知等州，作诗送之。作品：《三黜》<div id='poem_502601' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_502601' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/502601?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三黜诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（己酉岁送吕公出守南阳也　有序）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_502601")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_502601_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_502601'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_502601'>下惠为士师，子文乃令尹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_502601'>仕也固不喜，黜之何尝愠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_502601'>直道宜少合，高风谅难泯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_502601'>大抵君子心，惟义素藏韫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_502601'>进非为私谋，退亦为道隐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_502601'>顾彼荣与辱，于吾不加损。<div id='poem_sentence_5_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_502601'>我公天下贤，许国以诚悃。<div id='poem_sentence_6_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_502601'>危言屡启纳，大事费量忖。<div id='poem_sentence_7_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_502601'>审如秦和医，良剂起疾疢。<div id='poem_sentence_8_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_502601'>工如鲁匠斲，钜木赴绳准。<div id='poem_sentence_9_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_502601'>昔尝迁九江，谁谓去途窘。<div id='poem_sentence_10_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_502601'>又尝谪蕲水，恬然泛惊濆。<div id='poem_sentence_11_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_502601'>于今已三黜，去就决不混。<div id='poem_sentence_12_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_502601'>远视前世贤，并驱而齐轸。<div id='poem_sentence_13_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_502601'>大敌众所畏，未战势自殒。<div id='poem_sentence_14_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_502601'>惟公鼓而前，万旅悚兵楯。<div id='poem_sentence_15_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_502601'>晚节人所重，半道或凋陨。<div id='poem_sentence_16_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_502601'>惟公久益壮，千古激忠愤。<div id='poem_sentence_17_502601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_502601'>大明方乘离，元老反遇遁。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　寓居开封，唐介荐其应熙宁制科。有谢启。作品：《谢荐举启》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　寓居开封，备应熙宁制科。有谢诸官启。作品：《答诸官谢荐举启》<div id='poem_1181037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答诸官谢荐举启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181037")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181037'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181037'>比闻治最，辄露奏封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181037_comment'></div>盖为公朝之荐才，敢言私室之专惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181037_comment'></div>遽烦厚眷，特贶珍题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181037_comment'></div>仰荷谦光，徒增感怍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181037_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1181037_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　寓居开封，一作应制举上诸公书。作品：《应制举上诸公书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　寓居开封，又作应制举上诸公书。作品：《又应制举上诸公书》<div id='poem_1181028' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181028' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181028?labeling=true' target='_blank'>应制举上诸公书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181028")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181028_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181028'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181028'>陶闻之，圣人之所谓道者，以简易为宗，以该天下之理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181028_comment'></div>以仁义为用，以成天下之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181028_comment'></div>非幽远而难明，阔疏而难施，汗漫而不可考信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181028_comment'></div>自微言既息，章句之学，随流而兴，百家异骛，众说殊骋，各习其师，忘失统要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181028_comment'></div>故为《易》者不穷天地之本始、变化之至神，以推迹于人事，而务言上下无二经之异，《系辞》非仲尼之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181028_comment'></div>为《诗》者不究风俗之代变，王道之初终，以参验于治体，而好议《商》、《鲁》二颂之不同，毛、郑两解之小异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181028_comment'></div>为《春秋》者不考赏刑之大原，权制善否，一归皇极，而争辨日月之为例，五始七等之成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181028_comment'></div>为《书》者不取君臣上下、都俞告戒之义，号令施设之体要，而竞论《武成》之不可尽信，《秦》、《费》二誓之不当作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181028_comment'></div>有释数字之文至数十万言而是非无所处正，求以援世率民、乂天下国家之大略，盖阙如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181028_comment'></div>昔者尧舜之盛，崇冠百王，而《书》称其德乃曰：「顺考古道而行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181028_comment'></div>傅说戒于商宗，则亦曰：「师古以克永世」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181028_comment'></div>孟轲皇皇战国，开说诸侯，然非二帝三王仁义之语，未尝辄道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181028_comment'></div>摭此而论，则君臣之际，舍斯文要道，安所稽法，以全适治之具哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181028_comment'></div>是以二汉硕儒若董仲舒、儿宽、公孙弘、夏侯胜、隽不疑、伏湛、侯霸、鲁恭、郑兴、桓荣之徒，皆以经术博彊，果于适用，其辅导世主，推明治统，建大议，施远业，率有考据，不悖于三纲五常之分义，若持权衡、按绳墨，以审万物之轻重曲直，而毫忽莫敢欺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181028_comment'></div>永惟圣人立教贻训之心则既如彼，君臣之际师经式道则又宜如此，而学不执六经之用，以酬世务之变，乃放肆纷纭，乐为衍说，而滋破碎之害，深足惜焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181028_comment'></div>抑又闻哲人志士之所存，不以离俗为高，求全于世而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181028_comment'></div>盖仁以为任，远而逾励，大则欲恢隆先务，以跻至治之极；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181028_comment'></div>小则欲举偏补弊，以便安于一时故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181028_comment'></div>然三代之盛时，皆出于圣人经营创业之法，足以维持百世，是故井地以授民，什一以定赋，而天下之食足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181028_comment'></div>九赋以待用，九式以均节，而天下之财丰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181028_comment'></div>制乡遂以为六师，农隙则教战，而天下之兵强；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181028_comment'></div>自家党以上至于国都，皆立学以训导，而天下之士得其素养；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181028_comment'></div>六卿率属，辅昌王治，中外之务必举，而天下之官无倖位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181028_comment'></div>凡所以用于政教者，皆可循而守之，其贤智才能之人，惟在办事，而不复有加损废置之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181028_comment'></div>迨夫两汉之兴，皆乘丧乱之极，三代之宏规大范，盖无存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181028_comment'></div>其君臣之计议，多出于一时之茍简，而百度未俱，不足为后世之袭用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181028_comment'></div>及其弊生变起，则贤人君子裁量揆叙而为之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181028_comment'></div>是以七国交峙，而外有尾大之衅，反者将起，则晁错献削地之说，以弱诸侯而彊王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181028_comment'></div>百姓背本而趋末者众，淫侈之俗日长，而财用大蹶，则贾谊陈务农之计，欲驱游手而归之南亩，以广储积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181028_comment'></div>兼并之路不塞，而富室拥资巨万，贫弱愈困，则仲舒贡限田之议，以检过制而补不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181028_comment'></div>牧人之吏屡见罢易，而生民不能绥静，则朱浮申苛察之戒，欲久其职，俾人服从上教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181028_comment'></div>选举失实，贤不肖混乱，而无以协宣风教，则左雄抗限年之请，以考练名实，要之得人而任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181028_comment'></div>刑烦禁密，世主以峻政为威，而元元陷于惨暴，则陈宠上蠲法之疏，愿除其溢于甫刑者，以应经中礼而济群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1181028_comment'></div>凡为是者，大概缀缉缺漏，枝柱倾邪，随形栽割，期措斯民于康靖之域而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1181028_comment'></div>抑又闻，圣人之政，皆切致治而不能无弊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1181028_comment'></div>学者之言，务好陈文而未必可以适用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1181028_comment'></div>以不足适用之言，陈不能无弊之政，则华采浮胜，而事非根切，岂所谓有补于世哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1181028_comment'></div>昔汉文以恭俭治天下，号为隆平，朝廷无大过，边鄙无大忧，天道地化无大变异，生民无大失职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1181028_comment'></div>然而献书者以为可痛哭、可流涕、可长太息、背理伤道，难遍以疏举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1181028_comment'></div>岂当时之势诚尔邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1181028_comment'></div>盖亦激于忠愤，力为切直可畏之语，冀以感悟人生之意故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1181028_comment'></div>陶尝读六经，探索要归，舍章句之习，而务以简要明切为之本统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1181028_comment'></div>又尝历览旧史，窃迹近事，考究古今得失盛衰、治乱安危之变，而仅有得者，乃言而笔之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1181028_comment'></div>不溺于侈辞夸说，以求工于文，而庶几焉一有以资治理之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1181028_comment'></div>治平中，知者谓其可塞天子直言之诏，采而闻诸朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1181028_comment'></div>验于今日，则时异事变，而畴昔之论，多无取矣，然犹勉竭区区，欲求合于科举之式度者，盖知其指归也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1181028_comment'></div>恭惟阁下德业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1181028_comment'></div>文章之懿，充积于中，辉光于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1181028_comment'></div>以二帝三王之道献告吾君，讲修国具，以幸万世，博收天下之材而权乎器任，俾尽其用，安以一介为微而不见录于左右哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1181028_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「菁菁者莪，在彼中阿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1181028_comment'></div>言君子长育人材，则天下喜乐而咏歌之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1181028_comment'></div>又曰：「先民有言，询于刍荛」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1181028_comment'></div>言古之贤者谋及匹夫，而取其善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1181028_comment'></div>夫二《雅》之奥训，皆明哲之所履蹈，以完其事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1181028_comment'></div>陶固不足被长育之赐，亦庶乎先民之询者矣，惟阁下一与之进，幸甚幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1181028_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年9月24日</a>　神宗御殿试策，吕陶上对策，多论王安石新法之非。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年9月</a>　司马光等赞吕陶论对，上吕陶等论各六首。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='55b69d44d7ed46969d644d2f2ee36a9a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("55b69d44d7ed46969d644d2f2ee36a9a");'><span id='55b69d44d7ed46969d644d2f2ee36a9a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1086')">1085-1086年</a>，58-59岁</div><div id='55b69d44d7ed46969d644d2f2ee36a9a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年12月</a>　入朝，任司门郎中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年闰2月</a>　由御史中丞黄履等举任殿中侍御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年闰2月</a>　有辞免扎子。作品：《辞免殿中侍御史扎子》<div id='poem_1180911' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180911' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180911?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免殿中侍御史劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年闰2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180911")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180911_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180911'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180911'>臣今月二十一日准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨除殿中侍御史者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180911_comment'></div>闻命震悸，不知所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180911_comment'></div>窃以副端之与丞、杂，虽轻重不伦，而任责略等，非材识兼茂、望临一时，何以称选？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180911_comment'></div>矧时多艰，厥任尤重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180911_comment'></div>如臣朴陋之学，岂能有行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180911_comment'></div>衰迟之踪，无所可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180911_comment'></div>赐还旧列，曾未踰时，无补秋毫，方图丐罢，遽蒙擢序，大惧无以仰副睿明耳目之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180911_comment'></div>欲望圣慈追寝新命。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1180911_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年闰2月</a>　作辞表。作品：《辞免殿中侍御史表》<div id='poem_1180985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180985' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180985?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免殿中侍御史表<span class='inlineComment2'>（元祐元年闰二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年闰2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180985")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180985_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180985'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180985'>官有其责，实系纪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180985_comment'></div>材非所长，徒累名器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180985_comment'></div>方睿明之善继，惟听纳之处先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180985_comment'></div>宜任忠纯，以司献替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180985_comment'></div>如臣者生而孤远，学则迂疏，不通治道之本原，安能论政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180985_comment'></div>未熟朝廷之典故，何以绳愆？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180985_comment'></div>愿回拔擢之恩，慎委端良之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180985_comment'></div>庶使言能适用，官不备员，圣君有得于谋猷，愚者获安于分守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180985_comment'></div>所有告命，未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1180985_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年闰2月</a>　有答贺启。作品：《答庆帅贺右史启》<div id='poem_1181054' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181054' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181054?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答庆帅贺右史启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年闰2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181054")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181054_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181054'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181054'>叨被<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1181054", 1181054, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>诏音</span>，误升柱史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181054_comment'></div>名非实称，幸与愧并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181054_comment'></div>伏念某学尝诵经，仕欲行己，涉道至浅，彊文不高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181054_comment'></div>岁月驰迈于忧患之涂，志气耗凋于尘滓之域，青缃黄卷，虽素业之未忘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181054_comment'></div>文石赤墀，岂寒乡之可到？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181054_comment'></div>胡然冒据，率有夤缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181054_comment'></div>此盖某官恕以爱人，公于引类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181054_comment'></div>谓其有一日之雅，常借品题；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181054_comment'></div>知其无万乘之容，阴为援助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181054_comment'></div>乘光以进，省己甚明，力若舟航。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181054_comment'></div>已拜嘉于德宇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181054_comment'></div>音如金玉，又承教于风邮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181054_comment'></div>徒极置藏，曷穷染叙？</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1181054_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年闰2月</a>　弹劾司农少卿范子渊，黜知兖州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年闰2月</a>　论蜀茶事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年闰2月</a>　论劾蔡京等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年闰2月</a>　论福建、江西、湖南等路盐法之弊。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年3月</a>　论差除之法弊端。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年3月</a>　与刘挚、孙升先后三论安焘知枢密院不当。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年3月</a>　上疏论坊场城郭等事。作品：《奏乞放坊场欠钱状》<div id='poem_1180884' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180884' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180884?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞放坊场欠钱状</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180884")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180884_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180884'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180884'>臣伏见近岁以来，四海之利，多归公上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180884_comment'></div>官司之积，动计钜万；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180884_comment'></div>私室之有，十已九空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180884_comment'></div>恭惟圣政日新，德泽流霈，穷幽极远，蒙被生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180884_comment'></div>其事如大病之后，偶得良药，以活其命，有望更生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180884_comment'></div>而脏腹空虚，支体瘁弱，喘息之气，所存无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180884_comment'></div>切宜调护抚养，俾就安完，天下之肥，然后可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180884_comment'></div>是以堆垛、市易、义仓、抵当、免行之类，凡为聚敛者，一切废罢，此诚德惠及民之深，而与之休息也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180884_comment'></div>独有出卖坊场一事，最为深害，亦愿体恤，以慰其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180884_comment'></div>其立法之初，盖为在官司吏无有纪极，百费浮冗，贪吏从而侵渔，州郡衙前既勒力役，而所得酒榷之利，尽以奉于公家，有至财竭破生而死于冻馁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180884_comment'></div>朝廷知其如此，于是拘收坊场，官自出卖，所得净利，一以募人执役，二以给公家之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180884_comment'></div>行之渐久，弊从而生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180884_comment'></div>盖小人之情，竞利而不虑患，实封投状，务在必得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180884_comment'></div>既妄添所买之直，又虚增抵产之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180884_comment'></div>适值民间钱币阙乏，酒货不售，课利、净利、抽贯税钱供纳不足，才出季限，又有罚钱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180884_comment'></div>或委保百姓管押纲运，其押纲之人，往往盗窃官物，走窜失陷，则须勒保人赔填；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180884_comment'></div>或原买价高，界满无人交割，转更拖欠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180884_comment'></div>缘此数事，坊场多有破败，乃至出卖抵产，以偿官钱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180884_comment'></div>或抵产价高，出卖不行，则强责四邻承买；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1180884_comment'></div>或四邻贪乏，承买不尽，则摊及飞邻、望邻之家，抑令承买；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1180884_comment'></div>或本户抵产罄尽，尚欠官钱，则勒保人代纳，亦须破坏产业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1180884_comment'></div>或虚指债负，妄起<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1180884", 1180884, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>讼端</span>，横赖论索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1180884_comment'></div>郡县急于官课，不问有无逋欠，遂使平人承认。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1180884_comment'></div>械颈受箠，道路相望，囚系坐狱，殊无虚日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1180884_comment'></div>其甚者，至于自经沟渎，鬻及男女，而犹不能免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1180884_comment'></div>大率一县之内，中户以上，因买坊场或充壮、保而破散拖欠久者，十常四五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1180884_comment'></div>官方如此百计督责，极力掊聚，而逐界所得实钱，十分只及五六<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1180884_comment'></div>一则因元买价高，虚张其数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1180884_comment'></div>二则为物轻钱重，酒无厚利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1180884_comment'></div>三则日趋困穷，难于偿纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1180884_comment'></div>以此天下坊场钱积压少欠，其数极多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1180884_comment'></div>神宗皇帝深知其弊，曾于元丰三年明堂大赦并八年正月赦文累行蠲放，及与展送纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1180884_comment'></div>诏令所至，人皆鼓舞歌颂，以为天地大恩莫过于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1180884_comment'></div>除已蠲放外，至今欠钱不下八九百万贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1180884_comment'></div>簿书之内，虽有现欠之名，刑狱之下，必无可足之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1180884_comment'></div>方当陛下布政之初，聚敛刻剥之事大半罢去，天下臣庶，欣戴称颂，以为仁宗复生，尤宜广霈德泽，以慰其望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1180884_comment'></div>臣愚伏愿陛下特降睿旨，所系今日以前因买坊场拖欠课利、净利并抽贯税钱及过月罚钱之类，见勒买人或保人送纳并破卖抵产者，并与除放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1180884_comment'></div>庶几穷困之人，普沾大恩，复遂馀生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1180884_comment'></div>况皇帝陛下、太皇太后陛上下恭俭慈仁，出于天禀，内无土木华靡之费，外无兵戈攻战之赏，四海所入，国用丰盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1180884_comment'></div>虽放免数百万贯逋欠，如去泰山之一尘，何阙于事！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1180884_comment'></div>且天下之务，固有是非轻重，惟聪明睿智，能权而行，遂中于理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1180884_comment'></div>今放释逋负，以安生灵，与督责收敛，以广用度，何者为是，何者为非，何者为轻，何者为重？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1180884_comment'></div>权而行之，正在此日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1180884_comment'></div>又况冬春以来，雨雪愆候，祈祷备至，未闻沾足，则除放欠负，俾民免于冻馁，亦可以感天地之佑，召阴阳之和，使风雨时若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1180884_comment'></div>臣又闻真宗皇帝尝御偏殿，亲阅三司逋欠，放八万三千数，盖真宗以逐次降赦放欠，多为有司废格不行，或根究追逮，益为烦扰，故按籍引对而释之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1180884_comment'></div>臣愿陛下远法真庙之恤民，近仿神宗之布惠，断自圣意，特行蠲放坊场欠钱，天下不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1180884_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1180884'>〔贴黄〕臣今所奏，只是乞朝廷特放坊场欠负，可与不可，禀自圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1180884_comment'></div>即非冲改户部条贯，须至立法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1180884_comment'></div>伏乞留中裁酌，早赐施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1180884_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1180884'>〔又〕臣每见赦令放欠，多为有司百端抑遏，追究根穷，幸其稍戾于法，遂不除放，使圣朝仁泽，不及困穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1180884_comment'></div>大抵人君发号施令，当如震雷时雨，不测而至，则天下知恩出于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1180884_comment'></div>若委自有司，毫釐契勘，立为条约，然后施行，则弊生于下，有损治体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1180884_comment'></div>伏愿圣慈如以臣言万一可行，即乞将臣此奏留中，作朝廷意旨，降诏蠲放，不必付在有司。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1180884_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1180884'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_26_1180884_0'>⑴ 成都管内坊场，第一界卖七十二万馀贯，第二界六十六万馀贯，第三界四十二万馀贯，大率则收得一半入官外，馀无可催理。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1180884_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年4月</a>　先后论劾范子奇、李定等。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='fcb9f2409fdf400abb6f227b02375683_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fcb9f2409fdf400abb6f227b02375683");'><span id='fcb9f2409fdf400abb6f227b02375683_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1087')">1086-1087年</a>，59-60岁</div><div id='fcb9f2409fdf400abb6f227b02375683' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年10月</a>　从蜀还朝，上奏论役法。作品：《上殿扎子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年10月</a>　从蜀还朝，奏十事。作品：《奉使回奏十事状》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年10月</a>　论罢黄隐。作品：《请罢国子司业黄隐职任状》<div id='poem_1180892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请罢国子司业黄隐职任状</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180892")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180892_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180892'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180892'>臣窃以士之大患，在于随时俯仰而好恶不公，近则隳丧廉耻，远则败坏风俗，此礼义之罪人，治世之所不容也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180892_comment'></div>大学者，教化之渊源，所以风劝四方而示之表则，一有不令，何以诲人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180892_comment'></div>臣伏见国子司业黄隐素寡问学，薄于操行，久任言责，殊无献告，惟附会当时执政，茍安其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180892_comment'></div>及迁庠序，则又无以训导诸生，措注语言，皆逐势利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180892_comment'></div>且经义之说，盖无古今新旧，惟贵其当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180892_comment'></div>先儒之传注，既未全是，王氏之解，亦未必尽非，善学者审择而已，何必是古非今、贱彼贵我，务求合于世哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180892_comment'></div>方安石之用事，其书立于学官，布于天下，则肤浅之士，莫不推尊信向，以为介于孔、孟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180892_comment'></div>及其去位而死，则遂从之而诋毁，以为无足可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180892_comment'></div>盖未尝闻道，而烛理不明故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180892_comment'></div>隐亦能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1180892", 1180892, "Clauses/42/Comments/2")'>诵记</span>安石《新义》，推尊而信向之久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180892_comment'></div>一旦闻朝廷欲议科举，以救学者浮薄不根之弊，则讽谕其太学诸生，凡程试文字，不可复从王氏新说，或引用者，类多黜降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180892_comment'></div>何取舍之不一哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180892_comment'></div>诸生有闻安石之死而欲设斋致奠，以伸师资之报者，隐辄形忿怒，将绳以率敛之法，此尤可鄙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180892_comment'></div>夫所谓师弟子者，于礼有心丧，古人或为其师解官行服与负土成坟者，前史书以为美，后世仰以为高，此固不论其学之是非而特贵其风谊尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180892_comment'></div>昔彭越以大恶夷三族，诏捕收视者，栾布一勇士，敢祠而哭之，汉祖犹恕而不杀，班固亦以为能知所处，盖气节之可尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180892_comment'></div>今安石之罪虽暴于天下，推其师弟子之分，则亦不可辄废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180892_comment'></div>而诸生之设斋致奠，又非彭越、栾布之比，隐何必忿怒而遽欲绳之以法乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180892_comment'></div>抑可见其不知义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180892_comment'></div>向者有司欲复声律，朝廷方下其事，集群臣而议之，隐乃不详本末，奉为定令，揭榜学舍，谓朝廷已复诗赋，使学者知委，传播四方，人皆疑惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1180892_comment'></div>此又见其躁妄趋时之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1180892_comment'></div>夫道德所出之地，长育多士，而庶几成材，乃以欺人为之贰，则何以养廉耻、厚风俗哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1180892_comment'></div>伏请早行罢黜，以示劝戒，无使邪憸之士，久累教化之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1180892_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1180892'>〔贴黄〕大率隐好自任，凡考校生员文字，多不与祭酒、博士共议，意欲徇私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1180892_comment'></div>向者违条差补经谕不当，郑穆自举觉申礼部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1180892_comment'></div>近日定王适程试，高下异论，隐辄有申请，上烦朝廷与夺，益见其取与不协公论，不能称职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1180892_comment'></div>隐为御史三年，无所建明，为司业经年，职事乖失如此，已试不效，徒累名器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1180892_comment'></div>伏乞量其所能，与一外官，盖教化之地，非所宜处。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1180892_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年11月</a>　论劾蒲宗闵、曾肇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年11月</a>　上奏宽保甲等第。作品：《奏乞宽保甲等第并灾伤免冬教事状》<div id='poem_1180886' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180886' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180886?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞宽保甲等第并灾伤免冬教事状</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180886")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180886_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180886'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180886'>臣伏见保甲之法虽已更改，犹有二弊未便于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180886_comment'></div>其一为罢去二十亩以下免教，指挥却令五等户有三丁者，皆赴冬教一月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180886_comment'></div>缘民之贫富，不系丁之多少，而教与不教，则有幸不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180886_comment'></div>今田有百亩，家有二丁则免教，是谓之幸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180886_comment'></div>田有十亩，家有三丁则赴教，是谓之不幸，此贫富力役大为不均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180886_comment'></div>况今之教阅，官中不给钱米，一月之食，皆其自办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180886_comment'></div>夫有田二十亩之家，终年所收，不过二十石，赋税伏腊之外，又令供赡一丁，则力亦难给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180886_comment'></div>盖昔日推行之始，不暇讲求利害，惟务其多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180886_comment'></div>今虽将五等下户精专阅习，万一或有调发，虽破竭家财，所得几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180886_comment'></div>裹粮而行，岂不重困？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180886_comment'></div>臣愚欲乞于三等以上，或等第虽低而家业及一百贯有三丁者，方得差充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180886_comment'></div>其二为陕西州郡今秋雨涝，高原之地，虽谓顺成，下湿之田，稼亦不善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180886_comment'></div>人户有诉灾伤去处，而蠲税不及五分，并须赴教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180886_comment'></div>官司奉法，不敢放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180886_comment'></div>臣窃谓保甲之令，行已累年，朝廷知其有弊，多所釐改，欲民休息，若须候灾伤及得五分方与免教，亦恐德泽未广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180886_comment'></div>臣愚欲乞应系灾伤县分，并特免冬教，以惠陕西三路之民，不胜大幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180886_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1180886'>〔贴黄〕又况郡县自来检视灾伤，多有通计一县所放，立为分数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180886_comment'></div>如原管税一千石，放及五百石，则谓之五分，即非以逐户所伤，立为分数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180886_comment'></div>其被灾既有多少之异，而通计一县大数，偶不及五分，遂不免教，此朝廷之所当察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1180886_comment'></div>如蒙圣慈，以灾伤之故，不限分数，特免教阅，则朝廷武备未为废缺，而生民受惠深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1180886_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1180886'>〔又〕臣访闻陕西诸县人户有为田土绝少，虽家有三丁，有以田产微薄，陈状乞免教者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1180886_comment'></div>并有诉述本户灾伤过多，但为一县总数不及五分，亦乞免教者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1180886_comment'></div>逐县拘碍条禁，下敢辄行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1180886_comment'></div>伏乞早赐指挥，庶宽民力。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1180886_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年11月</a>　再论差役之法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年12月</a>　朱光庭、王岩叟等论苏轼策题之罪，陶为苏轼争之，党争起。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年11月</a>　上殿奏事。作品：《又上殿扎子》<div id='poem_1180913' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180913' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180913?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又上殿劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180913")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180913_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180913'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180913'>臣奉使远方，察知民间疾苦及官政未安凡一十事，已尝呈奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180913_comment'></div>其一乞减泸州戍兵，不示贼以形，且省馈运之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180913_comment'></div>其二乞不筑雅州城，以节横费，免于远方生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180913_comment'></div>其三乞立科折条约，使转运司与州县同任其责，以戒重歛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180913_comment'></div>其四乞添和买布价，以宽民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180913_comment'></div>其五乞减成都机院小料绫绮，罢监官，免勾百姓助工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180913_comment'></div>其六乞复成都府犀浦、绵州、西昌、陵井监、贵平等县，使民户力役均平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180913_comment'></div>其七乞兴州济众监铸减轻钱，庶使疲民不为炉冶所困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180913_comment'></div>其八乞详审改蔡濛所减铁价并所夺人铁炉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180913_comment'></div>其九乞开卓筒盐井，以济困穷，赖其课入，可助本路之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180913_comment'></div>其十乞罢兴州青阳镇铜锡场监官，以减冗滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180913_comment'></div>凡此十者，或陈一道之利害，或指一郡之休戚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180913_comment'></div>或议一邑，或言一官，以朝廷视之，乃细琐毫末，不足上裨国论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180913_comment'></div>以远方望之，则皆切近人情，最为急务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180913_comment'></div>仰惟圣治，愿赐采纳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1180913_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年1月</a>　论坊场之害。作品：《奏乞相度逐界坊场免欠钱状》<div id='poem_1180885' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180885' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180885?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞相度逐界坊场放免欠钱状</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180885")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180885_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180885'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180885'>臣伏见朝廷德惠及生民多矣，臣下聚敛之态，亦已悛革，惟坊场一事，根株深固，条约交紊，犹有馀弊，未尽蠲除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180885_comment'></div>盖累界放买，至今凡十五年，其始则有实封投状，竞利争占，虚增估直，诈通抵产之欺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180885_comment'></div>其中则有净利过重，月纳不足，出限罚钱，年满不替之患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180885_comment'></div>其终则有正名已败，壮、保纳官钱，馀欠尚存，邻人买产业之禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180885_comment'></div>期会严迫，节目烦多，不惟酒户缘此困穷，抑亦平民因而朘削，或系狱，或受箠，或转徙道路，或自经沟渎，天下郡邑，无处无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180885_comment'></div>大率一县之内，上中等户因买坊场及充壮、保而失业破产者，十常四五，多者欠至数千贯，少者亦三五百缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180885_comment'></div>以四海总计，凡几千家罹此疾苦矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180885_comment'></div>每家以十口为率，凡几万人失所矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180885_comment'></div>恭惟陛下至仁博爱，亦宜为之动心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180885_comment'></div>昔者神宗皇帝通知此弊，加意救恤，于元丰三年明堂降赦及八年正月赦文累行蠲免外，仍与展限二年送纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180885_comment'></div>去岁大飨肆赦，亦有权住催理指挥，委监司保明闻奏，当议等第蠲放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180885_comment'></div>德泽之流，非不广及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180885_comment'></div>然而此弊终未尽去者，一则为有司违慢诏旨，忘失法意，少有疑似，遂不保明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180885_comment'></div>二则为物轻币重，钱货乏绝，或灾伤所困，或兵役相仍，衣食之费，尚且不完，至于官钱，何从以纳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180885_comment'></div>况第一界至今已十五年，第二界今亦十二年，往往生业荡尽，子孙沦散，虚载簿书，枉费刑挞，岁月愈久，重不聊生，憔悴之馀，必无可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180885_comment'></div>臣愚伏愿陛下推广先志，霈发异恩，以远近之差，为轻重之序，应第一、第二界现欠者，并与除放；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180885_comment'></div>其第三、第四界，亦乞量立分数蠲免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180885_comment'></div>如此则大法简易，不为官吏之沮遏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180885_comment'></div>圣泽宽深，遂除生灵之疲瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1180885_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1180885'>〔贴黄〕承买坊场之家，抵产物业，原价高大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1180885_comment'></div>为近年物轻币重，田宅槩减价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1180885_comment'></div>今虽拘收在官，出卖之际，必不依得原估，官司仍于欠人身上理纳馀钱，极为骚扰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1180885_comment'></div>伏乞特降指挥，应系因坊场没官抵产，并许依原估价直充折，庶宽民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1180885_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1180885'>〔又〕又况第一、第二界价虚而高，第三、第四界价实而低，今第一、第二界虽欠钱一二分，比之第三、第四界已是增剩，况无可得，宜特蠲放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1180885_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1180885'>〔又〕若须候监司保明奏到，方议蠲免，深恐诸路迁延期限，或所见不一，及吏缘为奸，别生事节，致使朝廷实惠未能均遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1180885_comment'></div>莫若只以界限远近各与蠲减，所贵德泽早及细民。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1180885_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1180885'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_1180885_0'>⑴ 谓如抵产一处原估一千贯，今只值七百贯，即更令纳三百贯之类。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1180885_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年1月</a>　再论劾黄隐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年2月</a>　再劾郭茂恂。作品：《奏乞罢郭茂恂工部郎中状》<div id='poem_1180906' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180906' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180906?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞罢郭茂恂工部郎中状</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180906")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180906_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180906'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180906'>臣去年三月中，曾弹奏郭茂恂前任陕西监牧日，枷禁无罪妇人阿党等，令赔钱雇女使，及在秦州、永兴军皆有不检之迹，丑声流播，道路喧闻，不可为省郎并相度监牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180906_comment'></div>蒙朝廷采纳臣言，罢茂恂库部郎中，更不遣经画牧地，仍除军器少监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180906_comment'></div>当时士大夫谓朝廷既知茂恂猥恶如此而尚不许补外者，盖执政以亲旧之爱，曲为庇护，姑且处之京局，俟人言稍息，必复进用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180906_comment'></div>今日果如所料，乃以茂恂任工部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180906_comment'></div>诏命既传，颇骇群听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180906_comment'></div>且进善退恶者，天下之公议；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180906_comment'></div>信赏必罚者，人主之大权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180906_comment'></div>贪廉既禀于天资，安有昔污而今洁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180906_comment'></div>升黜动关于国体，岂可前是而后非？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180906_comment'></div>倘从辅弼之主张，必误朝廷之任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180906_comment'></div>伏愿陛下深明本末，洞察公私，特罢恩除，庶清郎选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180906_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1180906'>〔贴黄〕况茂恂领军器监以来，仍更违法冒请制造神御帐兴工下手节料了毕等钱，贪猥之行，久而不革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180906_comment'></div>臣已尝弹奏，伏请论罪如律，岂可因其有过，又复迁官？</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1180906_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年2月</a>　有奏状。作品：《奏乞降诏举郡守状》<div id='poem_1180883' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180883' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180883?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞降诏举郡守状</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180883")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180883_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180883'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180883'>臣窃以今日任官之弊，其轻且滥者，惟郡守为甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180883_comment'></div>封疆千里，生聚万众，休戚所系，而不问能否，一以资格用之，为半刺两任，有荐者二人，则得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180883_comment'></div>侮法慢令，戕民害物，十郡之中，常有二三；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180883_comment'></div>阘葺不治，又有一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180883_comment'></div>举天下亿兆之众十分而言，失其惠养者将半矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180883_comment'></div>承流宣化，又何望焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180883_comment'></div>方今朝廷清明，百度讲举，忧劳元元，以固邦本，惟恐一夫不获，而牧守之弊纷繁至此，甚可痛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180883_comment'></div>昔两汉盛时，政平讼理，民安其业者，皆循吏之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180883_comment'></div>唐之贞观、开元，号为善治，太宗亦尝自择刺史，志其姓名于屏风而用之，当时名臣如马周、张九龄辈，皆极言刺史不可轻任，载在史册，足为龟鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180883_comment'></div>前日朝廷患监司不得其人，乃诏近臣举用，而监司之选，稍稍清矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180883_comment'></div>至于郡守，尤为亲民，略而未议，是弃民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180883_comment'></div>臣伏请诏内外待制、太中大夫以上，于通判资序人内岁举堪知州者三人，朝廷更加审察，送吏部籍记名氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180883_comment'></div>凡遇有阙，先差有举主者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180883_comment'></div>如资任未及，即差权知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180883_comment'></div>其次方差资序合入人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180883_comment'></div>庶几牧守之职，有以庇民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180883_comment'></div>循良之风，无愧前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180883_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1180883'>〔贴黄〕天下民事之重，大则一路，付之监司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180883_comment'></div>中则一郡，付之太守；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1180883_comment'></div>下则一邑，责之县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1180883_comment'></div>如臂指之相附，如纲目之相维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1180883_comment'></div>国朝之制，既举监司，以清一路，又举县令，以治一邑，则一郡之守，亦宜举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1180883_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1180883'>〔又〕自八路差注以来，此选尤滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1180883_comment'></div>盖于本道就短求长，自知县两任，则得为通判；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1180883_comment'></div>自通判两任，遂为知州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1180883_comment'></div>其猥滥庸谬，不可胜言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1180883_comment'></div>今已收阙归吏部，似此等又皆可指占州郡之寄，虽人材绝无所取，而资任合入，则不可不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1180883_comment'></div>虚授滥除，生民何赖！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1180883_comment'></div>伏请特立荐格，以清其流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1180883_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1180883'>〔又〕臣今略举无状之尤者数人，望朝廷推其所为，即知可与不可为郡，轻滥之极，理当革也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1180883_comment'></div>王子文者，前知华州，每决打笞罪，须经旬或半月方断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1180883_comment'></div>或有百姓过状者，子文先问其人年几、生月日时，为之算命，告云：「尔星辰未佳，必不得理，且休过状」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1180883_comment'></div>又因杂职行杖生疏，子文下厅亲决一杖示之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1180883_comment'></div>其愚谬如此，今差知怀州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1180883_comment'></div>霍唐臣者，知眉州，每公会设食，须留数品，折请估直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1180883_comment'></div>有法司姓孙为吏，其兄在提刑司祗应，每法司有过，唐臣恕之，仍告云：「我为尔兄且放尔罪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1180883_comment'></div>其猥下如此，今差知海州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1180883_comment'></div>赵衮者，通判果州、权荣州事，一岁中为盐井破败，决一千六百馀人，昼监夜禁，常七八十人，略不存恤，以至为子决父，为妇决姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1180883_comment'></div>及就两州繁处，各请供给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1180883_comment'></div>其贪暴如此，今知广安军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1180883_comment'></div>张尧士者，尧佐同宗之弟，好誇族望，辄敢以温成皇后真容示监司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1180883_comment'></div>又尝差簿尉分往村镇，贩买诸物，图市易之息，日夕往还及百馀里，而获一缗之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1180883_comment'></div>又尝有因病杀牛祭鬼而获罪者，尧士云：「尔虽有病，何如且服药，休杀牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1180883_comment'></div>《周易》曰：『东邻杀牛，不如西邻之礿祭』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1180883_comment'></div>其庸暗如此，今知彰州。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1180883_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年3月</a>　奏劾吕和卿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年4月</a>　论劾童政。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年4月</a>　以旱与梁涛、范纯仁等赴刑部决狱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年5月</a>　傅尧俞、梁涛、王岩叟等以张舜民事，劾吕陶。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年5月</a>　劾李元辅侵损民利。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年5月</a>　任左司谏。上表辞免。作品：《辞免左司谏表》<div id='poem_1180986' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180986' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180986?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免左司谏表</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180986")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180986_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180986'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180986'>官以序迁，人非实称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180986_comment'></div>况七臣之所责，岂一介之可胜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180986_comment'></div>敢沥愚衷，愿还宠命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180986_comment'></div>伏念臣学未能造道，材不足适时，向自郎曹，擢用<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1180986", 1180986, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>言路</span>，徒更岁月，何补涓埃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180986_comment'></div>立仗在廷，尚缓黜幽之典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180986_comment'></div>伏蒲献说，愈怀窃位之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180986_comment'></div>匪惟清议之莫容，抑恐孤忠之易陨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180986_comment'></div>仰祈睿鉴，特寝误恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180986_comment'></div>所有告命，未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1180986_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年6月</a>　奏罢开乐宴。作品：《奏乞罢开乐宴状》<div id='poem_1180903' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180903' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180903?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞罢开乐宴状</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180903")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180903_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180903'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180903'>臣伏闻国朝故事，祥禫既除，有开乐一宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180903_comment'></div>近来中外喧传，谓已择日排办，旦夕必行此礼，臣愚尚窃疑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180903_comment'></div>盖自春徂夏，旱暵为灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180903_comment'></div>陛下忧劳恐惧，避殿减膳，精诚祈祷，夙夜不遑，以至过自贬损，权罢受册，务答天心，以冀享嘉之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180903_comment'></div>此乃旷古未有之德，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180903_comment'></div>今群臣屡拜封章，乞从礼听乐，陛下报诏，未蒙允许，乃未有开宴之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180903_comment'></div>而中外相传，皆谓宴在旦夕，似于事体未便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180903_comment'></div>伏祈宣谕有司，一就坤成节赐宴，则于礼文，亦非简疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180903_comment'></div>内可以隆二圣慈孝之德，外可以称上帝眷佑之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180903_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1180903'>〔贴黄〕臣又闻英宗朝八月将宴后苑，刘庠言「去日食近，非畏天之意」，特为罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180903_comment'></div>神宗朝四月将宴，富弼以灾异为言，亦蒙嘉纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180903_comment'></div>今旱暵之沴虽已消弭，而天道尤宜钦畏。<div class='inline'
