id='poem_sentence_11_1180903_comment'></div>愿陛下无灾而惧，为德天下，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1180903_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年6月</a>　论劾谢景温等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年6月</a>　作刘庠墓志铭。作品：《枢密刘公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181125?labeling=true' target='_blank'>枢密刘公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181125")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181125'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181125'>元祐元年三月某日，枢密学士、朝议大夫、充泾原路经略安抚使、马步军都总管兼知渭州军州、管内劝农使、彭城郡开国侯、食邑若干户、食实封若干户刘公以疾薨于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181125_comment'></div>驿奏至，朝廷悼之，遣内侍护丧以归，赐赠加等，凡所以赈恤其家者甚厚，诏赠太中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181125_comment'></div>越明年七月某日，乃葬于颍昌府某县某里，循礼考吉，务其称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181125_comment'></div>公讳庠，字希道，世为彭城人，其先盖汉楚元王交之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181125_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，祖讳某，皆恬于隐晦，爵禄不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181125_comment'></div>考讳某，博学知道，为世大儒，有器业可巨用，不幸仕龃龉，终青州观察推官，门人考其德义，谥明道先生，累赠银青光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181125_comment'></div>妣李氏，生显家，有贤行，治家教子如古烈妇，以公贵累封某郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181125_comment'></div>公少孤，八岁能诗，为石曼卿所器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181125_comment'></div>年十四，以文谒明道先生之友蔡文忠公，公奇而婿之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181125_comment'></div>以文忠遗奏，试将作监主簿，调宋城县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181125_comment'></div>用程文公荐，改陈州司户参军，移莫州莫县令，治塘水，溉民田数千顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181125_comment'></div>嘉祐二年擢进士第，六年，迁著作佐郎、知河南府伊阳县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181125_comment'></div>遇英宗践阼，迁秘书丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181125_comment'></div>修奉昭陵，百货之须，动辄千万，公治之有序，邑人不告病，而官亦足用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181125_comment'></div>转太常博士、充高密、广平两县教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181125_comment'></div>是时诏两制举御史，知制诏蔡抗荐公可任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181125_comment'></div>会英宗以灾求言，公即上书论世务十馀条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181125_comment'></div>英宗嘉叹，以书示宰相韩忠献公，且问所以，韩以不识对，上益重之，遣内侍宣旨，有「甚知才美」之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181125_comment'></div>遂用抗荐除监察御史里行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181125_comment'></div>及对，英宗曰：「欲用卿久矣，有大臣言卿与蔡抗亲，朕答以内举不避，虽亲何害」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181125_comment'></div>搢绅士大夫咸以为用公之当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181125_comment'></div>九月壬子朔，日有食之，未数日，陈张幄具后苑，以待宴幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181125_comment'></div>公言去日食太近，非畏天之威，恐惧修省也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181125_comment'></div>乃为罢宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181125_comment'></div>会圣宫创仁宗神御殿，宏丽过制，费钜万，公谓「天子之孝，不在宫庙之奢靡，在继先志，隆大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181125_comment'></div>今营建甚盛，非所以昭先帝俭德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181125_comment'></div>英宗为损其制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181125_comment'></div>襄阳郡王允良郊祀不陪祠，久罢朝谒，公陈其桀傲慢上帝，无人臣礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181125_comment'></div>奉宸库失盗，公劾巨阉领皇城司职事者，以严宫城之禁，「愿陛下不以近习挠天下法」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181125_comment'></div>英宗曰：「法令之设，内外一体」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181125_comment'></div>翌日，都知以下皆论罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181125_comment'></div>李珣犯销金，开封府以中旨辄释，公累言乞正国典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181125_comment'></div>请对，又陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1181125_comment'></div>英宗曰：「朕岂私一李珣邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1181125_comment'></div>乃仁宗外家，若行之，天下谓朕如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1181125_comment'></div>更不须言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1181125_comment'></div>公知上意如此，方已其论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1181125_comment'></div>又尝言：「命令失，名器滥，则知制诰还词头，门下封駮，愿申饬臣子举职如故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1181125_comment'></div>谏官、御史皆所以补阙失，柅违谬，宜增其员」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1181125_comment'></div>吕诲等既去位，公累疏乞留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1181125_comment'></div>又求对，奏：「诲等忠正敢言，意在爱君，陛下奈何轻斥之，以累盛德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1181125_comment'></div>上曰：「朕本不贬诲，自是诲等不肯留尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1181125_comment'></div>公恳请召还，词不少屈，时论韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1181125_comment'></div>英宗不豫，公力陈「日食星变，宜崇俭纳谏，布惠泽，以解天意，则转灾为祥，圣体当享无疆之休」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1181125_comment'></div>久之，朝政多自中出，皇嗣未立，人心尤不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1181125_comment'></div>公独拜疏，谓：「太子，天下本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1181125_comment'></div>汉文帝、唐太宗皆于即位元年预建太子，为宗社无穷计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1181125_comment'></div>颍王长且贤，愿陛下亟立为皇太子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1181125_comment'></div>上感悟，大位遂定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1181125_comment'></div>又请颍王侍禁中，阅天下奏报，降付如平时，俟康复乃罢，则圣躬便于颐养而机务不壅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1181125_comment'></div>宰臣韩琦、枢密使文彦博宜夜直，以安人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1181125_comment'></div>英宗崩，百官临福宁殿，太官给肉食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1181125_comment'></div>公谓「先帝弃四海，臣子岂知肉味？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1181125_comment'></div>请给素食，庶近礼」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1181125_comment'></div>「州郡遣子弟纳贡，贺即位，恩补过幸，宜罢去」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1181125_comment'></div>事虽不行，识者以为是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1181125_comment'></div>以神宗登极，恩补主客员外郎、殿中侍御史里行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1181125_comment'></div>未几，迁右司谏兼提举国子监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1181125_comment'></div>一日，神宗语及汉武事，公对曰：「王者当上法尧舜之德，下迹成、康、文、景之治，汉武不足为陛下道」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1181125_comment'></div>神宗悦其忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1181125_comment'></div>时边臣有邀功致戎者，本非朝廷意，公疏其奸谋，请寘于法，以谢天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1181125_comment'></div>及下二府大臣措置边事之宜，定以公罪，庶几不茍简误国事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1181125_comment'></div>又陈中国御戎之体，守信为上，武帝深入为下策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1181125_comment'></div>昔宝元时元昊叛，五来五背，天下为之困敝，今莫若宗大信，舍近功，为国家长利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1181125_comment'></div>古者冢宰制国用，量入以出，请诏二府议大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1181125_comment'></div>京师久不雨，蝗害稼，公引王弼、京房说，以为阴不能固阳，故不雨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1181125_comment'></div>臣安禄兹谓贪，厥灾虫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1181125_comment'></div>请黜臣下不胜任、安禄无德、蔽恶为孽者，则雨以时降，蝗不为灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1181125_comment'></div>又乞贳孙琪，留马默，以来直言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1181125_comment'></div>优容王陶，以全恩旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1181125_comment'></div>公之启沃献替，正纪纲，纠奸佞，著闻于人者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1181125_comment'></div>其秘词切论未尝语于私者，则莫得而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1181125_comment'></div>是年秋，奉使大辽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1181125_comment'></div>故事，两朝国忌不相避，公将还，度以正月八日至白沟，宴用乐，然是日英宗小祥也，公具以告，愿于涿州插宴，则八日达雄州，且行香，得遂臣子之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1181125_comment'></div>辽主叹美，从公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1181125_comment'></div>使还，除集贤殿修撰、充河东转运使，盖公论议刚果，权贵忌之，而利其去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1181125_comment'></div>时晋地旱饥，军费日广，公计一道之产，惟铁利为饶，请复旧冶鼓铸，通隰州温泉盐矾，博易以济用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1181125_comment'></div>又请募民入粟塞下，预为足食计，悉听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1181125_comment'></div>俄迁起居舍人、除天章阁待制，改河北都转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1181125_comment'></div>契丹入侵霸州土场为己地，集兵疑我，河东亦奏契丹徙帐西京，朝廷为之动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1181125_comment'></div>诏公验状，公曰：「云朔去岁饥荒，孰便于屯聚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1181125_comment'></div>今往西京者，不过集部族数万人，西胁秉常，南疑中国尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1181125_comment'></div>安肯舍定州平易之涂，趋并、晋险阨之地而入寇乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1181125_comment'></div>又以五说料其必不能有为，宜安静持重以待，可遂无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1181125_comment'></div>后果如公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1181125_comment'></div>二股河之役，兴兵无馀力，边城遂不完，公谓城垒之设，俯瞰敌境，势不在河防后，请辍二股役兵，备霸州等城，以严守御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1181125_comment'></div>黄河起春夫，御河继之，凡十七万九千人，期以期月罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1181125_comment'></div>公谓今年河始东流，其南北岸创堤防千馀里，以夫役争土功，力不足用，虽责以速成，未见实益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1181125_comment'></div>愿减半先治其急，而徐其他，则无枉费劳民之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1181125_comment'></div>诏约二股北流口，以拔水势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1181125_comment'></div>公言：「河方东流，而遽遏其北，则澶、滑以下，将有溃溢之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1181125_comment'></div>傥以岁月分杀其势，渐议闭塞，乃得治河之策」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1181125_comment'></div>宦者程昉乞益兵助御河之役，欲以奏功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1181125_comment'></div>公谓督工于盛夏，则暍死者众，乃奏缓之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1181125_comment'></div>又请销开塘口泄水势，外示设险之方，而内不失蒲苇樵苏之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1181125_comment'></div>朝廷皆信其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1181125_comment'></div>青苗令始下，公谓不可行，奏愿罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1181125_comment'></div>岁馀，差知成都府，以亲年高，不拜，得知真定府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1181125_comment'></div>属并晋用兵之后，民疲不聊生，上以安辑之旨谕公，又除河东都转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1181125_comment'></div>至则宽力役，蠲逋负，赈流散，以称上意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1181125_comment'></div>凡三阅月，乃召还，知开封府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1181125_comment'></div>前此，议者置厢官分治府事，凡轻罪听决遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1181125_comment'></div>公谓：「京师多豪右，厢官体轻人不畏，或缘而宽纵有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1181125_comment'></div>且政出多门，非所以肃清浩穰之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1181125_comment'></div>昔赵广汉尝患二辅乱其治，犹欲兼之，况厢事之末乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1181125_comment'></div>请罢蔡确、沈振，愿殚力公事，以报万一」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1181125_comment'></div>是时，宰相王安石用事，与公异论，确主于安石，见公不庭参。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1181125_comment'></div>公谓：「朝廷之仪，安可以私废」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1181125_comment'></div>上疏辨之，由是上失宰相意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1181125_comment'></div>神宗亦尝谕之曰：「卿柰何不与一二大臣协心济治乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1181125_comment'></div>公对曰：「臣子于君父各伸其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1181125_comment'></div>臣知事陛下，不知附王安石」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1181125_comment'></div>不数月，除龙图阁学士、知太原府，充河东路经略安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1181125_comment'></div>盖朝廷以二鄙为虑，谓公深知西北事，故以阃制付之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1181125_comment'></div>前帅尝建惹凌议，不足示威武，公奏罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1181125_comment'></div>夏国降羌数千人，公虑其为患，请遣诣境上，召其君归之，有不去者，乃留，外以示大体，内以消奸萌，两得其策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1181125_comment'></div>事未报，果有谋归者，中旨亟令徙内郡，公谓：「降羌迁则生变，宜假宴犒，渐移徙至太原，并边既无虞，比次区析于华人之中，久则吾民矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1181125_comment'></div>从之，塞外以宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1181125_comment'></div>累请复宪州以重形势，还置惠宁、肃定、神木三堡，以备应援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1181125_comment'></div>又请募兵民子弟之彊劲者为勇敢，以壮军声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1181125_comment'></div>如汉谪民戍边故事，下流非巨蠹积奸者，择少壮贳罪徙河外，以实边徼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1181125_comment'></div>皆可其奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1181125_comment'></div>契丹议侵疆，谍者谓有称兵意，朝廷问公，以为未必然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1181125_comment'></div>岢岚、雁门求济师，皆不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1181125_comment'></div>契丹主驻云州，遣数骑涉吾境，逻者得之，契丹驰檄，纷辩不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1181125_comment'></div>公奏曰：「契丹意在疆埸，持此为端尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1181125_comment'></div>臣刺知云州无兵，朔应艰食，愿朝廷缓答而峻拒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1181125_comment'></div>方盛夏，兵未必至，惟以有备待非常，乃得计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1181125_comment'></div>愿遣刘忱等至境上，姑以理谕，臣俾将佐饬兵观衅而动，此事机也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1181125_comment'></div>时朝廷以契丹使言顺礼恭，及持敦睦和好之说，乃录契丹主书付公，谕以地界，且通商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1181125_comment'></div>公复奏曰：「臣窃疑契丹此举非本心，盖见朝廷尚未克复河湟，不得不为唇齿之计，故以此尝我尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1181125_comment'></div>今欲争辨积年已定之疆界，曲固不在中国而在彼，则泛使之来，礼宜偃蹇而反恭顺，辞宜高抗而反卑逊，臣窃恐其意别有所在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1181125_comment'></div>敌意无厌，朝得寸，暮求尺，必又有侥倖之请，宜直以拒，或与以不当得之地，既杜其奸，未必不疑中国有谋，用此以饵之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1181125_comment'></div>若妄意于我，背盟伺隙，恐非岁月可解也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1181125_comment'></div>公争之既不能得，会遭太夫人丧去位，后竟以黄嵬山分水岭地与之，公常以为恨，士大夫为国远虑者，至今惜焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1181125_comment'></div>郡邑酒户，月以课入供河外，远或至千里，公请以季易月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1181125_comment'></div>麟、府州汉户之单丁与蕃族之内附而遇歉者，檄有司蠲其役，且著为令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1181125_comment'></div>晋俗尚焚骸，贫不克葬者，遂委不视，为竁四穴以藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1181125_comment'></div>公在晋二年，治兵与民，皆得其心，以静制寇，不劳而服，父老至今犹能称道感叹之不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1181125_comment'></div>丧既除，又差知成都府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1181125_comment'></div>蜀久安无事，朝廷以德惠抚之，官吏或纵情忘分守，公一切齐以法度，上下宜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1181125_comment'></div>细民竞利，以高直占坊场，破产不能偿，相继箠死或自杀，公请蠲所负，以惠远人，乞推之诸路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1181125_comment'></div>天子可其奏，获免者凡数十万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1181125_comment'></div>文州蕃族有复雠者，当以蕃法论，朝廷欲加诛，请赦之，以宁边圉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1181125_comment'></div>缘罪徙内郡者，愿复之，以示恩信；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1181125_comment'></div>西山六州与汉人为婚姻者，请禁之，以防后患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1181125_comment'></div>悉从公奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1181125_comment'></div>至于治石室黉舍，增置学官，广朝廷教育之意，又新乖崖张公祠，为书韩忠献公碑立祠下，慰蜀人之思，皆有助于治体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1181125_comment'></div>迁礼部郎中、知秦州，充秦凤经略安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1181125_comment'></div>以失举，降秩一等，改虢州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1181125_comment'></div>及期，知江宁府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1181125_comment'></div>官制行，易朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1181125_comment'></div>未踰年，又坐失举，降秩知滁州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1181125_comment'></div>甫三月，特起知青州，充京东东路安抚使，又徙知永兴军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1181125_comment'></div>时征西戎无功，调发恟骇，关右骚然，天子震怒，大臣无敢议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1181125_comment'></div>公过阙赐对，言：「虚内事外，恐动摇根本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1181125_comment'></div>边隅之患，特手足之疥，圣德宜涵容，置之度外，天下幸甚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1181125_comment'></div>上嘉纳焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1181125_comment'></div>陕右保甲行团教法，州邑扰动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1181125_comment'></div>公奏曰：「军旅之后，年饥人劳，正当完养其力，宜权罢教，俾之少休」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1181125_comment'></div>乃得罢一年税租。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1181125_comment'></div>苗役之逋，荐饥不能偿，请倚阁以纾其乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1181125_comment'></div>流徙汉南者，请依富弼青州赈济术，俾京西安集之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1181125_comment'></div>移税往他州，民不堪其劳，请宽下户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1181125_comment'></div>诏皆纳可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1181125_comment'></div>南山逃卒仅百人，依聚山谷，时出剽近县，或杀官吏，厚遗山民为耳目，因保甲团教掠兵器，驱村落马骡乘以遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1181125_comment'></div>捕者虽勇锐，终莫能遏，长安大恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1181125_comment'></div>公于是徙山中居民入保，奏罢并山团教，令歛外马悉归州县，乃发兵驱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1181125_comment'></div>未几，贼势自蹙，遂歼凶渠，而支党亦溃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1181125_comment'></div>是年十二月，拜枢密直学士，旋除知渭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1181125_comment'></div>时转运使办军储非其术，按版籍强民以供，公揭榜罢之，增物价而民来愿输者众，廪计大实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1181125_comment'></div>边吏请发防春兵，公谓疆圉无事，遂不遣卒，无他虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1181125_comment'></div>弓箭手屡以戍废耕，公下番休之令，凡旬有五日而罢，边户便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1181125_comment'></div>朝廷方与民休息，有怀柔四夷之意，公亦以绥边弭寇为先务，不幸在镇三月而卒，故宏规远略，未施一二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1181125_comment'></div>初，公感疾，有大星陨于正寝，人咸异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1181125_comment'></div>及其没也，华人戎族皆恸哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1181125_comment'></div>讣至京师，太皇太后嗟悼之深，且谓：「如刘庠辈不过数人，方将召用，而命不少假」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1181125_comment'></div>搢绅士大夫识与不识，莫不伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1181125_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1181125_comment'></div>公刚方直谅，学造本统，通古今治乱安危之孰为，积深而蓄厚，亲逢睿明，被遇隆眷，发为爱君忧国之谋，推为泽民恤物之利，贤者事业，盖无愧负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1181125_comment'></div>惟屡忤权贵，不忍一俯己徇合，悠然四方，遂至终老，此可悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1181125_comment'></div>太皇太后为宗社万世计，保祐嗣皇，裁决大政，图倚旧德，共厎治安，而公不及见焉，此重可悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1181125_comment'></div>公娶蔡氏，封安康郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1181125_comment'></div>男六人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1181125_comment'></div>端夫，凤翔府观察判官，先公五年卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1181125_comment'></div>次三人早亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1181125_comment'></div>次敦夫，承奉郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1181125_comment'></div>次宽夫，承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1181125_comment'></div>女一人，适定州北平县主簿朱师略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1181125_comment'></div>孙男二人：沔，假承务郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1181125_comment'></div>浩，早夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1181125_comment'></div>女一人尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1181125_comment'></div>公享年六十四，有文集二十卷，奏议三十卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1181125_comment'></div>雅不喜治生，禄廪所入，均以赡族人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1181125_comment'></div>使契丹得金币，则以葬宗党之贫者，凡二十馀丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1181125_comment'></div>兄之子，互以恩补，故捐馆之日，宽夫犹未仕，此人所难能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1181125_comment'></div>储宫之议，公尤晦密，终神宗一朝无知者，此又难能也，视古君子何愧耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1181125_comment'></div>蜀茶之初禁，陶知彭州，辄条其害以闻，朝廷委公与部使审议，公以陶言为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1181125_comment'></div>陶既罪废，公又累疏辨之，知我可谓厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1181125_comment'></div>后八年，见公于渭，从容语议，慨然有忧天下之心，至明年而亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1181125_comment'></div>其德业始终大概，陶可得而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1181125_comment'></div>重以诸孤之勤请，敢哭而铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_201_1181125'>彭城之刘，实继楚元，奕世有显，又生公贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1181125_comment'></div>惟公之贤，以刚济忠，献告二后，靡言不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1181125_comment'></div>治平之末，独建大议，天人合符，传以神器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1181125_comment'></div>始终一朝，公晦不言，方之古人，孰为后先？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1181125_comment'></div>公忠自将，义不附会，天子倚信，用公于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1181125_comment'></div>公之在外，十有八年，威扬惠浃，卒老于边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1181125_comment'></div>离明坤载，协德而济，黄发在廷，惟公已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1181125_comment'></div>生有大节，没有重名，敢告无穷，勒之斯铭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_208_1181125_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年7月</a>　论劾沈季长、韩维。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年7月</a>　有任京西转运副使之命。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年8月</a>　改任梓州路转运副使。有谢表。作品：《谢梓州路转运副使表》<div id='poem_1180988' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180988' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180988?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢梓州路转运副使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180988")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180988_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180988'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180988'>臣陶伏奉告命，差权梓州路计度转运副使兼本路劝农使，臣已于今月二十五日到任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180988_comment'></div>京右输将，转引嫌而愿避；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180988_comment'></div>坤维刺举，复申命以遣行，垒被宠灵，徒知感惧<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180988_comment'></div>伏念臣寒乡寡与，素守自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180988_comment'></div>偶待罪于中台，旋充员于左省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180988_comment'></div>爝火不能助太阳之照，勺水无以益沧海之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180988_comment'></div>每竭虑以上闻，多蒙开纳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180988_comment'></div>及叨恩而外补，尽出保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180988_comment'></div>此盖太皇太后陛下垂计宝图，玩心治道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180988_comment'></div>优容言职，以隆听谏之美名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180988_comment'></div>慎重使权，欲广爱民之盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180988_comment'></div>因而孤蹇，预此光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180988_comment'></div>况巴蜀之数州，去朝廷而百舍，土居俭陋，俗尚孱迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180988_comment'></div>虽平时赋入之饶，经常粗给；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180988_comment'></div>自顷岁军兴之后，疮痏未完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180988_comment'></div>网密则人用怨咨，辔柔则事将废弛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180988_comment'></div>臣敢不讲求中术，推导至仁，少图日月之劳，仰报乾坤之赐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1180988_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='aec48aa3fd4342e68f3d5c5116cd93a2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aec48aa3fd4342e68f3d5c5116cd93a2");'><span id='aec48aa3fd4342e68f3d5c5116cd93a2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1093')">1091-1093年</a>，64-66岁</div><div id='aec48aa3fd4342e68f3d5c5116cd93a2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年11月</a>　十一月壬寅，任右司郎中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年11月</a>　十一月辛酉，因范百禄、苏轼荐，任起居舍人。有辞免状。作品：《辞免起居舍人状》<div id='poem_1180905' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180905' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180905?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免起居舍人状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180905")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180905_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180905'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180905'>閤门告，除臣起居舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180905_comment'></div>伏以柱下之官，记人主言动，备一代典章，传信后世，惟博学多闻，习知史法之士，可称其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180905_comment'></div>如臣衰陋，材不足用，安敢冒据，以速罪戾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180905_comment'></div>仰祈睿明，慎惜名器，特寝误恩，庶允公论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180905_comment'></div>所有告命，未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1180905_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年12月</a>　上奏论臣僚奏请事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年12月</a>　郊祀礼成，有上诗表。作品：《进郊祀礼成诗表》<div id='poem_1180987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180987?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进郊祀礼成诗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180987")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180987_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180987'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180987'>臣闻承天莫重于郊，盖求端而报本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180987_comment'></div>惟圣为能享帝，务荐德以交神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180987_comment'></div>共庆昌期，备熙能事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180987_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下道该元化，运席重熙，勤色养于三宫，动遵慈训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180987_comment'></div>格欢心于万国，肇举严禋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180987_comment'></div>参求今古之宜，仿用祖宗之宪，具陈百礼，并报两仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180987_comment'></div>丕承穰简之休，大布生成之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180987_comment'></div>汤仁解网，周俗虚囹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180987_comment'></div>远之侯甸要荒，尽驱跻于寿域；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180987_comment'></div>小则虫鱼草木，亦茂遂于恩波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180987_comment'></div>臣叨侍清光，亲逢盛观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180987_comment'></div>听圜丘降神之乐，均有虔诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180987_comment'></div>续昊天成命之歌，愧无善颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180987_comment'></div>谨吟成《郊祀礼成诗》一首三十韵，奉表投进以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1180987_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　苏轼来家，观文与可画，作赞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　为友人何大临撰墓志。作品：《奉议郎何君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181143' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181143' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181143?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉议郎何君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐八年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181143")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181143_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181143'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181143'>余尝铭光禄寺丞岷山何公之墓，考论世次及其里居详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181143_comment'></div>君乃光禄仲子也，讳大临，字才叔，少读书，知名教，以修洁治身，以恭愿事亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181143_comment'></div>乡党以善称，闺门以孝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181143_comment'></div>通《诗》、《骚》之学，仿约大致，作为篇章，适情寓物，平畅纯澹，有昔人风格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181143_comment'></div>或告以释氏之说，当虔敬崇奉，乃享令报，则曰：「广慈心即佛，不妄语即经，若乃祸福之应，惟修其在我者，而顺以听命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181143_comment'></div>吾知此而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181143_comment'></div>晚从道家之教，信尚清寂，求以养心治气，归之虚静，故能委置世纷，无竞于物，漠然自得，有方外之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181143_comment'></div>尤长于教子，择师取友必以贤，饬励以经术，欲其慎行而寡过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181143_comment'></div>诱掖以辞章，欲其资身而得禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181143_comment'></div>凡朝夕所肄习而谓之课试者，每与之讲解，切劘不倦，若朋友然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181143_comment'></div>由是起家中第，孟仲接武，西南士大夫举义方之训，皆推君为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181143_comment'></div>君娶倪氏，累封安仁县君，卒十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181143_comment'></div>子五人：宗范，朝散郎、眉州教授；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181143_comment'></div>宗奭早亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181143_comment'></div>宗诲以学求举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181143_comment'></div>宗韩，资州磐石县令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181143_comment'></div>宗哲，果州相如县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181143_comment'></div>孙男十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181143_comment'></div>元丰三年，神宗祀明堂，封君承事郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181143_comment'></div>其后五迁，至奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181143_comment'></div>宗范又尝得五品服，请以赐君，不著于令，诏特可之，议者以为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181143_comment'></div>君享年六十三，元祐五年三月十五日卒于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181143_comment'></div>八年正月四日，葬于青城县之怀仁乡赤木里先茔之北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181143_comment'></div>初，倪氏之葬也，君为寿冢其旁，吊以诗曰：「我来同穴知何日，石火光中更十年」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181143_comment'></div>已而其言验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181143_comment'></div>嗟夫，始终生死之变，岂偶然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181143_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1181143'>每读《五代·忠义传》，至明宗命何瓒入蜀制孟知祥事，未尝不废卷而叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181143_comment'></div>夫以明宗区区暌弱之唐，任一何瓒而欲御权彊僭叛之蜀，岂不难哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181143_comment'></div>瓒意不屈，继以死，何其易也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181143_comment'></div>自瓒至君六世，而子孙之盛如此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181143_comment'></div>究观前人之大节，推验后嗣之吉报，则福禄之来，抑有由矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1181143_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　见蒋堂之子蒋熙州，有诗赠之。作品：《送蒋熙州》<div id='poem_502609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_502609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/502609?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送蒋熙州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_502609")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_502609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_502609'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_502609'>昔登蒋公门，忽忽五十载。<div id='poem_sentence_0_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_502609'>于今见犹子，省记似前代。<div id='poem_sentence_1_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_502609'>庆源得馀波，家范禀性诲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_502609'>笔下吐雄文，滔滔涌江海。<div id='poem_sentence_3_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_502609'>胸中抱英气，落落等嵩岱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_502609'>十尝试一二，卓荦已称最。<div id='poem_sentence_5_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_502609'>还朝才几时，何时又补外。<div id='poem_sentence_6_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_502609'>河湟复古地，形势壮且大。<div id='poem_sentence_7_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_502609'>册府图籍存，充国城垒在。<div id='poem_sentence_8_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_502609'>临洮建都府，节制中机会。<div id='poem_sentence_9_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_502609'>守之扼喉吭，动则攻腹背。<div id='poem_sentence_10_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_502609'>西羌辄犯顺，种落异向背。<div id='poem_sentence_11_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_502609'>呼嗟秦雍间，氛祲恐未艾。<div id='poem_sentence_12_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_502609'>连年困飞挽，何日贮仓廥。<div id='poem_sentence_13_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_502609'>一病费调养，已甚其可再。<div id='poem_sentence_14_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_502609'>绥怀与剪荡，黑白灿利害。<div id='poem_sentence_15_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_502609'>吾君鉴勤远，静制六合内。<div id='poem_sentence_16_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_502609'>仁如天地心，万类悉容贷。<div id='poem_sentence_17_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_502609'>不矜灵旗伐，未奏短箫凯。<div id='poem_sentence_18_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_502609'>一旦春风来，生意入穷塞。<div id='poem_sentence_19_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_502609'>载瞻将军钺，犹识使者旆。<div id='poem_sentence_20_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_502609'>治边信有术，岂徒威克爱<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_21_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_502609'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_502609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_502609'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_502609_0'>⑴ 自注：庆历中，蒋公希鲁侍郎守成都，某蒙赖数载，今五十年矣。观熙州之为人，彊裕清敏，盖得其家法云。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_502609_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年3月</a>　范百禄引用吕陶等川人，黄庆基论劾之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年3月</a>　为常安民之母李夫人作墓志。作品：《李夫人墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181153' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181153' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181153?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李夫人墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐八年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181153")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181153_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181153'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181153'>夫人李氏封寿光县君，故尚书屯田郎中常公讳溥之妇、宣义郎致仕构之妻、左朝奉郎安民之母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181153_comment'></div>其先盖唐之宗室，为盐铁判官，从僖宗西幸，遂居邛州之依政者，曾祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181153_comment'></div>好施不吝，赒及冻馁者，祖元熙也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181153_comment'></div>以文学名乡里，为诗尤工者，父奂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181153_comment'></div>郎中公家范严整，太夫人雅好宾客，夫人夙夕事奉，周尽敬礼，诸姑悦其恭，娣姒服其和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181153_comment'></div>宣义君少从学，不治产，不恤有无，夫人能成其志，不累以家事，凡嫁娶伏腊问遗之具，一切处办，莫不中礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181153_comment'></div>享年六十有六，元祐五年十二月十八日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181153_comment'></div>子六人：长安石，卫尉寺丞，早亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181153_comment'></div>次即安民，志尚清壮，学行治最，推高一时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181153_comment'></div>次安序、安节、安稷，皆举进士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181153_comment'></div>季安时，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181153_comment'></div>女二人：长适左承议郎、宿州州学教授梅贡，次适左承奉郎、大理评事滕友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181153_comment'></div>孙男四人，女七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181153_comment'></div>惟常氏世世守廉约，族属众，资费寡，自夫人之来归，勤俭以修妇职，慈恤以敦母道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181153_comment'></div>损口体之奉，以丰滫瀡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181153_comment'></div>完缯缊之敝，以备袟襦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181153_comment'></div>养足于老，爱隆于幼，三十年间，闺阃雍睦，人无间言，可谓贤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181153_comment'></div>既而二子得禄，安舆洁膳，始有可乐之意，则感疾挛痹，凡十馀年不能痊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181153_comment'></div>朝奉君尝由太常丞除江西转运判官，恳请留京师，力谋疗治，朝廷从之，改宗正丞，迁开封府推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181153_comment'></div>国医高手诊视殆遍，竟不起，得非命乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181153_comment'></div>自郎中公而上，皆葬临邛，至夫人之丧，贫不可以归，乃以八年三月甲申葬于陈州某县受节乡三河村之原，盖亦不悖于礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181153_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1181153'>禄以养，何报之凉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181153_comment'></div>礼以葬，孰为之乡？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181153_comment'></div>有宛惟丘，盖得其藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181153_comment'></div>孝乎亲乎，要之不忘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1181153_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年5月</a>　三省进呈黄敦逸四状，中有论苏轼与吕陶之交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年6月</a>　与姚勔并为中书舍人。有辞表。作品：《辞免中书舍人表》<div id='poem_1180992' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180992' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180992?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免中书舍人表</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐八年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180992")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180992_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180992'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180992'>窃以法从徊翔，盛时尤贵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180992_comment'></div>掖垣润色，儒者共荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180992_comment'></div>既代王言，亦闻政事，贵任至重，简拔惟贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180992_comment'></div>如臣疏愚，况复衰晚，文辞不足以发挥典制，议论不足以补助简书，忽忝诏除，何堪器使？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180992_comment'></div>愿寝已行之命，免贻不称之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180992_comment'></div>所有恩命，未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1180992_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年6月</a>　上任有谢表。作品：《谢中书舍人表》<div id='poem_1180993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180993' class='poemTitle class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180993_comment'></div>便蕃异数，震恐懦悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180993_comment'></div>伏念臣世处寒乡，性非中智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180993_comment'></div>少而向学，粗知为己之方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180993_comment'></div>长亦效官，偶适代耕之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180993_comment'></div>熙宁中以贤科射策，元祐初以言路备员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180993_comment'></div>竟难补报于朝廷，已分栖迟于郡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180993_comment'></div>此盖伏遇太皇太后陛下德由坤载，道契离明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180993_comment'></div>夙夜万事之几，思济于治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180993_comment'></div>庶几晚节，少答洪私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180993_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1180993_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180994_comment'></div>拜命优隆，省躬愧幸<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180994_comment'></div>伏念臣生而孤远，学则迂疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180994_comment'></div>知善恶之异途，惟务养心而自贵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180994_comment'></div>信通塞之有命，安能枉己以求容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180994_comment'></div>进退何常，险夷不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180994_comment'></div>岁月耗凋于奔走之后，形迹阻缩于忧患之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180994_comment'></div>何期雨露之私，误及桑榆之景，爰从右蜀，付以都郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180994_comment'></div>既跻柱史之华，遂及掖垣之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180994_comment'></div>茍片善可收而用，虽至寒不使之遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180994_comment'></div>幸眷于兹，叨尘过甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180994_comment'></div>诏见王者之志，其何以发挥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180994_comment'></div>服有君子之容，敢忘于报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180994_comment'></div>誓坚履尚，特达钧陶。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1180994_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_content_1180995'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180995'>岁有一时之暑，安敢告劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180995_comment'></div>恩加三事之臣，遽令退食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180995_comment'></div>敬承温旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180995_comment'></div>窃愧懦衷<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180995_comment'></div>臣等误以短才，与闻庶政，虽穷日力，莫代天工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180995_comment'></div>适逢庚伏之辰，得遂燕居之欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180995_comment'></div>此盖伏遇太皇太后陛下德该洪造，治格太和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180995_comment'></div>愠已解于薰风，景自长于化国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180995_comment'></div>是致弼谐之职，殊忘勤瘁之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180995_comment'></div>动复便安，极知幸会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180995_comment'></div>在公之事，居常早夜以深思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180995_comment'></div>报上之心，不以炎凉而易辄。<div class='inline'
