ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1094')">1093-1094年</a>，66-67岁</div><div id='d269f1b089a2448e8a1fa0b85c77ac0a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年10月</a>　为石洵直撰墓志铭。作品：《中大夫致仕石公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181128' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181128' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181128?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中大夫致仕石公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐八年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181128")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181128_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181128'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181128'>有宋名卿，蜀之纯德君子，中大夫致仕石公，享年九十有三，以元祐六年十月某日终于眉州私第之正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181128_comment'></div>八年十月某日，葬于眉山县怀德乡先茔之次，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181128_comment'></div>维石氏出万石君之后，唐有仲览者，仕至兵部郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181128_comment'></div>又六世，曰藏用，大历中为羽林大将军，善星纬之学，当朱泚未乱时，已告老，尝谓家人曰：「天下将有变，惟蜀稍安」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181128_comment'></div>乃携孥而西，依其亲眉州刺史李滈，遂家焉，至公七世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181128_comment'></div>曾祖瑭，隐居守道，爵禄不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181128_comment'></div>祖昌龄，累赠屯田员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181128_comment'></div>考待举，赠至开府仪同三司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181128_comment'></div>公讳洵直，字居正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181128_comment'></div>幼有志操，彊学力文，为辞章清赡尚理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181128_comment'></div>举进士，声称翕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181128_comment'></div>中景祐元年甲科，释褐知泾州保定县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181128_comment'></div>又知并之祁县，通判遂、并二州，守凤、归、成、陵、彭五郡，分司南京，遂谢事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181128_comment'></div>自秘书省校书郎五转至太常博士，又八迁为光禄卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181128_comment'></div>官制行，易中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181128_comment'></div>累封开国侯，积勋上柱国，以三品服终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181128_comment'></div>此出处之大概也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181128_comment'></div>始，蜀人去五代乱，俗未向儒，屯田君即其居构层台以储书，以经术教子弟，里人化之，弦诵日闻，号「书台石家」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181128_comment'></div>有子待闻，卒其业，咸平中及进士第，又登贤良方正科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181128_comment'></div>志大言高，与世多忤，仕竟不显，终检校水部员外郎，乃公之季父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181128_comment'></div>公以性质之美，家法之良，深滀厚养，完就德器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181128_comment'></div>刚不暴于容貌，柔不混于履趣，平居恂恂然，即之甚温，及其遇事决可否，则贲育莫亢其勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181128_comment'></div>在成州时，宽恤民力之诏下，部使遣官行郡，有杨士元者，持檄而至，作气势，事求索，重为民病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181128_comment'></div>公以状白转运使，即召之还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181128_comment'></div>李元瑜者，天资憸刻人也，知彭州永昌县，为公属吏，忽就领常平事，辄依法逞其私，傲上凌下，无愧耻，锐意戕剥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181128_comment'></div>公以理解譬，使之驯伏，卒无所施，一郡不被其毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181128_comment'></div>陵之医挟其技，犯分抵禁，诈为疾，幸恩霈以免，公一日引而榜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181128_comment'></div>彭之巫诉于郡僚，构淫祠，诓俗以祸福，公收而置之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181128_comment'></div>其敏决举类此，识者畏其勇力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181128_comment'></div>其少时能安贫重义，不求茍得，既贵，益坚如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181128_comment'></div>在我者约，故于物不扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181128_comment'></div>秭归漆林之饶，官吏多为髹器，以广资用，耗地产，夺民利，上下习以成俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181128_comment'></div>公一切罢去，邦人蒙其惠，殿中御史张唐英因撰漆民语，刻石纪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1181128_comment'></div>陵阳圭田之入，素号优腆，不问岁美恶，倚办较吏，务登其赢，公尽革之，后人遵以为常，君子服其廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1181128_comment'></div>夫勇则识者畏，廉则君子服，然皆公之小者、近者，其大且远者，盖未尝发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1181128_comment'></div>窃尝论之，公少而博学，举进士，为天下第六，风度清懿，从政知治体，茍少露馀蕴以示众，或有资地可凭藉，则推志及物，利泽滋广，功名将赫然，岂特数郡而已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1181128_comment'></div>惟其信道甚笃，处己甚重，待外物甚轻，安晦静默，宝其所有以为高，世所谓进取荣利者，未尝萌于心，出于口，是故人无知者，卒不巨用，亦未尝有毫发不满之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1181128_comment'></div>其高标令节，足以立懦夫，敦薄俗，乡党赖以主风教，多士仰以为师式，其顾视悖义丧耻，以侥倖锱铢之进者，如粪土也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1181128_comment'></div>公既退休，终日闭门，泊然无所营，不与俗子交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1181128_comment'></div>即城南旧圃为亭沼，植名花异卉，每乘舆往游其间，以诗酒为娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1181128_comment'></div>其诗尤平畅閒澹，无一语及荣辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1181128_comment'></div>时大中大夫程公浚、史公瑜亦已引年，庞眉鹤发，安车相还往，燕喜赓唱，里人敬之，号「三卿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1181128_comment'></div>凡如此者二十年，此又非世俗之所能享也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1181128_comment'></div>与夫驰骋于名利之场，一絓世网，终身不复出，回首故乡如逆旅，心欲奋飞而迹不能者，楚乐盖异矣，所得孰为轻重哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1181128_comment'></div>进退岂不裕哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1181128_comment'></div>公娶苏氏，累封仁寿郡君，先卒几年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1181128_comment'></div>子二人：长景修，宣义郎、知嘉州洪雅县；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1181128_comment'></div>次咏，嘉州军事推官、监蜀州陶坝镇，皆亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1181128_comment'></div>女一人，适朝奉郎郭子皋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1181128_comment'></div>孙三人：顺之，承务郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1181128_comment'></div>延之，太庙斋郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1181128_comment'></div>元之，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1181128_comment'></div>孙女六人：长适进士程舆，次适蜀州永康县尉苏某，馀未字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1181128_comment'></div>水部有三子，伯与季皆早世，公既贵，各官其一子，田畴室庐均而畀之，尤见其雍睦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1181128_comment'></div>元祐初，陶为谏官，议事及权贵，得请补外，公之从孙朝奉君嗣庆具以本末告公，公曰：「士之所养有素，动而得一善足矣，安俟其馀」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1181128_comment'></div>斯言其知我哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1181128_comment'></div>及公将葬，朝奉君状公平生行业，求志其墓，其敢辞乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1181128_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1181128'>十寻之木，或植于荒，所立不高，视以为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1181128_comment'></div>我固不竞，谁其度量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1181128_comment'></div>不剖而尊彝，不削而栋梁，不弊于刻剜，不罹于斧斨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1181128_comment'></div>根坚干老，惟日之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1181128_comment'></div>彼自曰胜，此庸何伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1181128_comment'></div>所贵在德，久而不忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（《净德集》卷二二。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1181128_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1181128'>永昌：疑为「唐昌」之误，彭州有唐昌县而无永昌县。</div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1181128_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年11月</a>　使契丹还，拜给事中。有辞表。作品：《辞免给事中表》<div id='poem_1180999' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180999' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180999?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免给事中表</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐八年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180999")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180999_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180999'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180999'>伏以命令之行，贵于中理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180999_comment'></div>论駮之任，慎于择人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180999_comment'></div>或误选抡，将贻罪咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180999_comment'></div>臣学不造道，材非适时，平生安流落之常，晚岁有亨通之渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180999_comment'></div>既尘侍从，未报涓埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180999_comment'></div>忽叨制綍之恩，又进琐闱之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180999_comment'></div>厚颜滋甚，腾口谓何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180999_comment'></div>虽行己直前，无所畏避；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180999_comment'></div>而遇事当断，多涉迂疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180999_comment'></div>茍宣纳之过差，乃是非之混乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180999_comment'></div>伏愿追回成命，妙选良臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180999_comment'></div>使还诏批敕之风，不减前辈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180999_comment'></div>则发号施令之体，无累圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180999_comment'></div>臣之愚诚，虔切于是。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1180999_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年11月</a>　使契丹还，拜给事中。有谢表。作品：《谢给事中表》<div id='poem_1181000' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181000' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181000?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢给事中表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1093年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181000")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181000_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181000'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181000'>润辞西掖，不能发挥典制之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181000_comment'></div>迁职东台，何以报塞朝廷之遇？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181000_comment'></div>恩隆选重，感切忧深<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181000_comment'></div>臣植自孤根，进由朴学，佩服圣贤之训，常秉危心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181000_comment'></div>审知义利之途，敢愆素履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181000_comment'></div>服劳虽久，涉险居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181000_comment'></div>偶暮境之亲逢，致亨衢之序涉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181000_comment'></div>屡尘华贯，叠拜宠章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181000_comment'></div>况封駮之置官，亦论思之任责，岂朝衰薄，辄与选抡？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181000_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下乾健有为，离明能照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181000_comment'></div>揽政机而独断，务举纲条；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181000_comment'></div>循治路以安行，动严枢柅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181000_comment'></div>推任人之诚，而不求其备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181000_comment'></div>操厉世之术，而用劝其忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181000_comment'></div>误以疏凡，处于津要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181000_comment'></div>臣敢不勉遵约守，祗慎攸司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181000_comment'></div>体从政之大方，戒近名之小智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181000_comment'></div>庶无瘝旷，特答生成。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1181000_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年2月</a>　有奏状。作品：《奏乞察小人邪妄之言状》<div id='poem_1180909' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180909' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180909?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞察小人邪妄之言状</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐八年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180909")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180909_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180909'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180909'>臣察谓人君深居九重，尊高如天，虽有圣智，亦未能周知天下之事，必以纳谏为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180909_comment'></div>既能纳谏，则臣子可尽下情，以陈治乱之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180909_comment'></div>今陛下听政之初，臣备位侍从，朝廷之事，得以论思，敢竭愚鄙，少报万分之一，愿陛下特加省览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180909_comment'></div>臣伏以太皇太后保佑圣躬，于今九年，垂帘听政，天下安治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180909_comment'></div>一旦弃四海之养，凡在臣庶，痛心泣血，无所逮及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180909_comment'></div>方其得疾之初，陛下忧形玉色，躬侍药食，衣不解带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180909_comment'></div>告于天地社稷，祷于宗庙山川，薄刑赦罪，释逋轻赋，凡可以祈福禳灾之事讲求备至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180909_comment'></div>及其疾势大渐，则召高族子弟入于禁中，丁宁抚慰，有安心免忧之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180909_comment'></div>既以大殓，内侍有需索酒食者，礼部臣僚谓方当哀毁，不可为闾阎鄙俚之事，恐累圣德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180909_comment'></div>陛下即从批奏，遂罢其请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180909_comment'></div>继有手诏，称扬太皇太后临朝累年，抑损外戚，未尝假借，无以报称盛德，议于高族子弟推恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180909_comment'></div>又虑诸处应奉山陵过有劳费，遂令降诏有司，并须遵依遗诏指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180909_comment'></div>远近臣子，闻此等事，无不感叹，皆谓太皇太后于陛下有天地之功，于社稷有万世之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180909_comment'></div>陛下深知本末，尊而报之，一言一事，不敢违戾太皇太后之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180909_comment'></div>上合天心，足以享万寿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180909_comment'></div>下副人望，足以保四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180909_comment'></div>宗社幸甚，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180909_comment'></div>然臣于此时，以无可疑而为疑，以不必言而为言，则其罪不胜诛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180909_comment'></div>所恃者，陛下仁而好谏，明而察物，必能赦臣私忧过计之罪尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1180909_comment'></div>盖自太皇太后垂帘以来，屏黜凶邪，裁抑侥倖，横恩滥赏，一切革去，小人之心，不无怨憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1180909_comment'></div>万一或有奸邪不正之言，上惑圣听，谓太皇太后斥旧臣更改政事，今日陛下既亲万几，则某人宜复用，某事宜复行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1180909_comment'></div>此乃治乱之端，安危之机，君子小人消长之兆，在陛下察与不察也，辨与不辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1180909_comment'></div>陛下察其是非，辨其邪正，使非不敢胜是，邪不能害正，则君子进，小人退，天下治而安矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1180909_comment'></div>昔元祐之初，臣任台官，尝因奏事帘前，恭闻德音宣谕云：「朝廷政事，若果于民有害，即当更改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1180909_comment'></div>其他不系利害者，亦不须改」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1180909_comment'></div>每改一事，必说与太后，恐外人不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1180909_comment'></div>臣深思此语，则太皇太后凡有更改，固非出于私意，盖不得已而后改也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1180909_comment'></div>至如章惇悖慢无礼，吕惠卿奸回害物，蔡确谤毁大不敬，李定不持母丧，张诚一盗父墓中物，宋用臣掊歛过当，李宪、王中正邀功生边事，皆是积恶已盈，罪不容诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1180909_comment'></div>若败露于先帝之朝，必须不免窜逐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1180909_comment'></div>若暴扬于陛下之手，亦合正以典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1180909_comment'></div>以此而言，则太皇太后所改之事，皆欲生民之便；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1180909_comment'></div>所逐之臣，尽是天下之恶，岂可以为非乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1180909_comment'></div>恭惟陛下聪明圣智，出于天纵，是非邪正，进退可否，必已了然于心，岂待人言而后辨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1180909_comment'></div>臣乃不避斧钺之谴，喋喋以告陛下者，亦婺妇不恤纬而忧宗周之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1180909_comment'></div>夫婺妇以组织为事，惟经纬是恤，今乃不恤其纬，而以周亡为忧，固可怪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1180909_comment'></div>愚者千虑，亦有一得，狂夫言之，明主择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1180909_comment'></div>臣又闻昔者明肃太后称制之日，多以私恩遍及亲党，听断庶物，或涉过差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1180909_comment'></div>及至仁宗皇帝亲政之初，臣下遂有希合上意，言其阙失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1180909_comment'></div>仁宗察见情伪，降诏止绝，其略曰：「明肃太后夙承先顾，保佑冲人，勤约之风，化流四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1180909_comment'></div>或号令之所出，或听断之从宜，盖机务之实繁，虽旰昃而无暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1180909_comment'></div>赏善罚恶，惟命令之已行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1180909_comment'></div>革故鼎新，非孝思之所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1180909_comment'></div>易月方临于庶政，虚怀觊纳于谠言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1180909_comment'></div>其有罔识远图，靡循理体，达于闻听，姑务矜容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1180909_comment'></div>多形琐碎之言，复有迎合之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1180909_comment'></div>宜申诫励，以警奸回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1180909_comment'></div>应明肃太后垂帘日所行诏命，已经施行过诸般公事，更不得更辄上言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1180909_comment'></div>于是天下之人，皆谓仁宗深念社稷之功，能全子母之爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1180909_comment'></div>圣听广大，超越今古，载在史册，垂范后世，陛下所宜法而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1180909_comment'></div>臣愚窃谓明肃太后之政，时有过阙，仁宗念其保护，尚降诏书，不容小人辄有议论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1180909_comment'></div>而况太皇太后垂帘九年，所行之政，皆已便民，所逐之臣，各已当罪，无可拟议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1180909_comment'></div>万一小人狂妄献言，岂可容哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1180909_comment'></div>岂可信哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1180909_comment'></div>愿陛下明示黜罚，杜塞其端，以副天下之望，以隆宗社之福。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1180909_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年3月2日</a>　除集贤院学士知陈州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
广元（绵谷）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='825c2b3ff53645d19eadc3db1d850581_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("825c2b3ff53645d19eadc3db1d850581");'><span id='825c2b3ff53645d19eadc3db1d850581_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1057')">1052-1057年</a>，25-30岁</div><div id='825c2b3ff53645d19eadc3db1d850581' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1054')">1052-1054年</a>　为绵谷县主簿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年4月</a>　为绵谷主簿。利州新城成，作记。作品：《利州修城记》<div id='poem_1181111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181111' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181111?labeling=true' target='_blank'>利州修城记</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181111")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181111_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181111'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181111'>皇祐四年冬，蛮寇岭表，犯诸郡，惟广州城坚可守，攻之五旬不陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181111_comment'></div>自是搢绅大夫言于朝，谓蜀久治安，武备稍废，城当城，不当遂废不议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181111_comment'></div>诏俾治之，此缮修之大槩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181111_comment'></div>利据蜀之四达，古号控扼地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181111_comment'></div>既喉而藩，其势孰御？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181111_comment'></div>将臣之出守者，绾有兵制，统治边疆，朝廷建置之意远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181111_comment'></div>城圮弗顾，焉能率职？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181111_comment'></div>况天子明诏存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181111_comment'></div>郡守太原王侯，勤劳民务，率有矩矱，奉诏祗饬，乃谋于城，寻其广凡千有五百，会其入总十有三万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181111_comment'></div>欲赋于民则地瘠财窘，虽丰年犹有艰食，重困以劳，饥将不膏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181111_comment'></div>欲籍于兵则给役无几，但缓岁月，未克以究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181111_comment'></div>乃请于漕刑二府，仰其资给而成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181111_comment'></div>咸以为天下之事一也，协议而济，孰谓损权？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181111_comment'></div>顾己而处，孰谓知变？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181111_comment'></div>矧为之城，非私一郡，岂宜坐视州郡之阙而恬愉其心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181111_comment'></div>于是集他州羡卒千人，致廪粟数千斛，以周其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181111_comment'></div>郡守王侯日至城所，以劳以食，众罔不勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181111_comment'></div>起甲午仲冬，至乙未夏四月而新城成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181111_comment'></div>观夫墉垒屹立，山河凭辅，以控则壮，以居则完，乃襟带之利也，城之为效可述矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181111_comment'></div>然天下久安，虽三王之政必有敝，不救不革，元元畴依，则利固有大于城，害固有大于不城，必曰警而后虑，非虑之原也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181111_comment'></div>推此及彼，功业乌可涯哉？</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1181111_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　为绵谷县主簿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年12月</a>　为绵谷主簿。利州重建永安庙成，作记。作品：《利州重建永安庙记》<div id='poem_1181112' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181112' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181112?labeling=true' target='_blank'>利州重建永安庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181112")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181112_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181112'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181112'>利城东北隅有隙地，广袤数十步，庙貌栋宇，圮不复见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181112_comment'></div>岁之春秋，郡遣官祭其神，至则设俎豆榛棘间，行献礼，讫事，弃而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181112_comment'></div>考诸图志，庙以永安目之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181112_comment'></div>索其创建之本末，不得而悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181112_comment'></div>然详观称谓，摭《礼经》命祀之说，揆前世所以神，夫岂非法足以济时，功足以保国，捍灾御患，贻斯民之利者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181112_comment'></div>又岂非丘陵川谷出云为风雨，见怪物，资万物之生者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181112_comment'></div>抑良吏嘉政，有以入人之心，没而不能忘者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181112_comment'></div>不然，孰能传庙祀历千百年，虽血食几废，而美名尚存邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181112_comment'></div>嘉祐二年冬十月，郡守张侯遵按祀典，追怀神烈，严其像而屋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181112_comment'></div>于是明灵以安，荐献以位，岁时致报，不黩而肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181112_comment'></div>客有过而叹曰：民荷神之休以生，神于民有功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181112_comment'></div>太守司民甘苦，务宁其生，故推本于神而奉以礼具，以永民之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181112_comment'></div>太守于民无愧也，神享太守之报何愧矣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181112_comment'></div>十二月五日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1181112_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
铜梁
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4e118fa50aae4c20bac6a6c1bf8545f9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4e118fa50aae4c20bac6a6c1bf8545f9");'><span id='4e118fa50aae4c20bac6a6c1bf8545f9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1063')">1058-1063年</a>，31-36岁</div><div id='4e118fa50aae4c20bac6a6c1bf8545f9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　调铜梁令，有政绩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年12月</a>　代吕公弼作成都西楼记。作品：《重修成都西楼记》<div id='poem_1181113' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181113' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181113?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重修成都西楼记<span class='inlineComment2'>（代吕公弼嘉祐七年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181113")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181113_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181113'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181113'>嘉祐六年夏四月，予自延安就领成都节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181113_comment'></div>至则考求风俗之敝，及其所便安，乃知蜀人循柔思义，易以诚感，治得其道，皆能乐生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181113_comment'></div>于是平心而思，律己而动，事罔钜细，务中适宜，庶几宣布皇泽，使之泳游，则亦无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181113_comment'></div>既而普淖大熟，新陈相仍，物遂平价，昔之饥者有腴其肤，向之寒者或温其躯，野农昼嬉，廛叟夜娱，皞皞然不知其从来，若处于唐虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181113_comment'></div>岂非尧仁舜明，覆被幽远，庶黎蒙福之效欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181113_comment'></div>夫然，奉诏令，导德惠，因其安生而与之共乐者，亦牧守之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181113_comment'></div>府署西楼，创建远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181113_comment'></div>据藩翰之峻势，宅林园之胜地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181113_comment'></div>登临阔视，可以极山川之秀景；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181113_comment'></div>燕閒高会，可以快风月之清意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181113_comment'></div>岁之方春，物状尤异，红葩鲜妍，台榭交辉，绿树茂密，亭宇争荫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181113_comment'></div>吾民来游，醉于楼下，实一方之伟观，四时之绝赏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181113_comment'></div>惜乎基级倾圮，梁栱腐桡，遽一风雨，虑至剥覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181113_comment'></div>此而不葺，殆非修旧起废，悦民便俗之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181113_comment'></div>然议者重于兴作，欲改竖厅舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181113_comment'></div>予以为斯楼之建，亦西州故事，一日乘毁辄易，民其谓何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181113_comment'></div>乃办材鸠功，因而新之，不赋于民，不耗于公，未踰月而事具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181113_comment'></div>观夫巍构山立，重楹翚飞，上虚下广，内显外壮，穹隆奂丽，疑若天设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181113_comment'></div>既落成之，酌而谓同僚曰：「昔齐宣、梁惠有园囿台沼之胜，不与民共，孟子议之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181113_comment'></div>会今承平，远方无他忧，斯人熙熙，知乐生之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181113_comment'></div>予幸守土，不咈其欲，则是役也，庶不为孟子所讥耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181113_comment'></div>因笔为记云<span class='inlineComment2'>（《净德集》卷一三。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1181113'>原无此注，据文渊阁本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1181113_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1063')">1059-1063年</a>　任铜梁县令。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
寿阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5f2bfb01145244af91c4d210601b0c4e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5f2bfb01145244af91c4d210601b0c4e");'><span id='5f2bfb01145244af91c4d210601b0c4e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1065')">1064-1065年</a>，37-38岁</div><div id='5f2bfb01145244af91c4d210601b0c4e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　是年，知太原府寿阳县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年5月</a>　知寿阳县。知太原陈升之任枢密副使，还阙，作序送之。作品：《送并帅陈公还阙序》<div id='poem_1181068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181068' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181068?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送并帅陈公还阙序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181068")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181068_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181068'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181068'>兵者，天下之难事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181068_comment'></div>用之难，不若养之难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181068_comment'></div>养之难，不若御之尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181068_comment'></div>用兵而失道，则威沮于外，不可以胜敌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181068_comment'></div>养兵而无制，则生民之害日益增长于内，久而不革，祸败随之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181068_comment'></div>御兵而非其道，则内外之衅乘间以发，速若反掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181068_comment'></div>故用之难不若养与御之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181068_comment'></div>今之兵，习常于治安而不用，将用之固难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181068_comment'></div>惟其养而有制，御而有道，则无几可适于用而不甚患其难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181068_comment'></div>屯田置府之法，不能少仿前世，而聚豪悍不逞之徒，无虑百万，温衣饱食，仰给县官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181068_comment'></div>赋敛过乎什一，公利不遗毫末，而廪帑无数岁之积，耗于兵者十常四五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181068_comment'></div>夫耕而殍沟壑，妇织而寒无以自覆，家苦于转输，户劳于馈饷，斯民之力，有时而竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181068_comment'></div>养兵之制宜尔邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181068_comment'></div>无名不功之赐数下，不能厌满其意，而能开诱其贪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181068_comment'></div>平居摇摇焉，惟恩赉是望，不幸有非常之事，则聚而议赏，嘉祐之末见之，而可为太息也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181068_comment'></div>有偷生之色，无敢死之气，知可爱之政，不知可畏之令，上下恬然，曾莫是恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181068_comment'></div>或匹夫之勇，或数级之多，不诘其忠义智谋何若，遽假以美官重职而措之要地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181068_comment'></div>其甚者以捍边，又其甚者以副一道之经制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181068_comment'></div>夫小人之情，好推其类而归心焉，有唐方镇之变，鲜不由此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181068_comment'></div>御兵之道宜尔邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181068_comment'></div>恭惟图任元臣，总握枢柄，赖其深谋奥略，以御遏四海险暴之萌，而立成富彊不拔之势，伟乎盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181068_comment'></div>惟公忠纯贞亮，卓然当世，出处中外，率本大节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181068_comment'></div>无好名惧谤之意，不为茍简自安之策，早夜孜孜，为朝廷画宏远无穷之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181068_comment'></div>岂非信道笃而自任以天下之重者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181068_comment'></div>上嗣位之二年，念公之贤，不当久于外，乃诏以归，将付之钜任，所以塞天下之望，而仰成重德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181068_comment'></div>夫如是，则毕天下之事不足为了也，功名不足为有无也，惟大君子尽所以致身行己之道，无负而后已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181068_comment'></div>向之所谓难者，俄而易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181068_comment'></div>四夷可怀也，生民可福也，万世之利可享也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181068_comment'></div>昔汉宣帝厉精求治，鍊群臣，核名实，而魏相总领众职，颇称其意，上下相安，莫敢茍且。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181068_comment'></div>又尝陈五兵之要，谏击匈奴右地，言行计从，有三世称藩之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181068_comment'></div>唐宪宗愤国势之陵荡，奋英武，削乱阶，而裴度抗志决策，以靖盘结之祲，奸臣凶将，蓄锐丧气，惮其威棱，二十年间，王室系之轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181068_comment'></div>以古揆今，而观圣贤之会，则公之勋谊德业，岂特偕汉唐名臣而已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181068_comment'></div>国有良史，必能书其详。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1181068_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　唐介以龙图阁学士知太原，有贺启。作品：《贺太原帅启》<div id='poem_1181055' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181055' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181055?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺太原帅启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181055")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181055_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181055'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181055'>四国于蕃，邦家所以示彊干弱枝之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181055_comment'></div>一麾出守，州部所以致承流宣化之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181055_comment'></div>其振举如裘领之从，其委使若臂指之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181055_comment'></div>况论道经邦之旧德，居秉旄杖钺之达尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181055_comment'></div>克壮其猷，增重两山之气象；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181055_comment'></div>所服者众，特高二鄙之威名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181055_comment'></div>岱宗之泽，不出于一朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181055_comment'></div>洪河之润，自及于千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181055_comment'></div>顾惟陋邑，爰属提封，常引领于门庭，敢荐名于竿牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181055_comment'></div>恭惟某官道光群辟，德被斯民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181055_comment'></div>藉裴令之论兵，辍于枢轴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181055_comment'></div>仰郑公之开幕，遄返朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181055_comment'></div>介圭闻入觐之期，绣衮有来归之咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181055_comment'></div>复资远业，永翊昌图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181055_comment'></div>某叨假郡章，获依帅节，弘纲具举，愿遵条目之常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181055_comment'></div>柔辔以驱，庶尽疲驽之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181055_comment'></div>前瞻台席，增抃予心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1181055_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
太原（阳曲）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='233fe038232046619f465170360b57e7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("233fe038232046619f465170360b57e7");'><span id='233fe038232046619f465170360b57e7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1068')">1065-1068年</a>，38-41岁</div><div id='233fe038232046619f465170360b57e7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　唐介辟吕陶为签书判官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　唐介等采吕陶之言以应直言之诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年</a>　与唐介子唐淑问相识。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年9月</a>　唐介被召还朝，作序送之。作品：《送唐子方序》<div id='poem_1181067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181067?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送唐子方序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1067年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181067")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181067'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181067'>治乱之源，出于任人，而贤不肖进退，系天下之幸不幸，世主安得不慎取舍哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181067_comment'></div>盖天下之事，有本末，有重轻，贤者志于远，而不肖者茍于近，此所以任人之得失，为斯民之治乱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181067_comment'></div>汉孝武承文景恭俭之馀，中外丰实，奋然欲鞭笞四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181067_comment'></div>竭数十年滋衍之财，继以盐铁舟车之入，调用于边，犹不能赡，乃至桑弘羊领大农，而尽秋毫之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181067_comment'></div>然户口减耗，邦本摇矣，虽悔且哀，痛无及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181067_comment'></div>唐宪宗力平寇孽，以兵费为先务，而异镈聚敛媚上，乃执大政，虽裴度、崔群谏，辄不听用，上下群情，为之震骇，而元和治体亦寖衰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181067_comment'></div>吾朝举海域之广，利源货法，一制于上，富厚之积，跨拟前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181067_comment'></div>然而兵过百万，日有常养；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181067_comment'></div>二陲向顺，岁有常赐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181067_comment'></div>三载禋赉，万官冗禄，尚方之用，时或不会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181067_comment'></div>平居量入而出，仅无馀焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181067_comment'></div>自康定用师，以四海备一方，而天下之力不复全盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181067_comment'></div>比者数年大变继起，优锡之具，多贷于民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181067_comment'></div>歉饥相仍，十室九空，而朝廷经费不可一日少损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181067_comment'></div>呜呼，用度如此其急也，生民如此其劳也，则天下利柄谁可属任耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181067_comment'></div>上嗣位之九月，亲劢听断，远猷庶政，究索讲举，元臣旧德，简擢信任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181067_comment'></div>念公之贤，不当久于外，乃诏以归，而付之大计，天下于是知上之愿治，而任人得其道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181067_comment'></div>惟公忠纯贞亮，以仁义礼乐贲饰诸外，历辅三圣，无后先游说之助，惟直道自致，惟大节自处，湛然有阜安元元之志，承命而往，岂非天下之幸欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181067_comment'></div>荀卿书虽杂言王霸，至于论足国之道，则曰「节用以礼，裕民以政」，又曰「儒术诚行，则天下泰而富」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181067_comment'></div>夫上所以任公者，本节用裕民之道矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181067_comment'></div>公所以报上者，施儒术而跻富寿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181067_comment'></div>推而措之揆席，以翊成大化，则良史必书其详，此姑述公之行尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1181067_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　在太原府签书判官任上。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
崇州（晋源）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6e7a014ca9d04c3f93f2376cf6b6b3c6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6e7a014ca9d04c3f93f2376cf6b6b3c6");'><span id='6e7a014ca9d04c3f93f2376cf6b6b3c6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1072')">1070-1072年</a>，43-45岁</div><div id='6e7a014ca9d04c3f93f2376cf6b6b3c6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年9月</a>　入贤良方正等科四等，通判蜀州。有谢启。作品：《谢登制科启》<div id='poem_1181038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181038?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢登制科启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181038")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181038_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181038'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181038'>圣问该明，深究一时之弊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181038_comment'></div>刍言猥略，愧非三道之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181038_comment'></div>服宠过优，寄颜良厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181038_comment'></div>夫取人之术，惟名实之辨不欺，则可要以终；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181038_comment'></div>行己之方，惟义利之分不惑，则能伸其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181038_comment'></div>尝观制举之开设，莫盛本朝之选抡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181038_comment'></div>公卿间出，而广有济时之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181038_comment'></div>豪俊继起，而屡闻康国之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181038_comment'></div>高风邈矣，故事存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181038_comment'></div>以科试论之，谓之名而实乃询于阙失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181038_comment'></div>以进取待之，谓之利而义难茍于谀从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181038_comment'></div>虽隆薄之在人，亦轻重之由己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181038_comment'></div>如陶者寒乡寡与，朴学粗坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181038_comment'></div>强为文辞而气格不高，好穷事变而术略无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181038_comment'></div>徒谓前良之可慕，又思圣主之难逢，辄不自量，庶几少立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181038_comment'></div>幸被德音之召，俾从国士之游，咸造广廷，仰承清问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181038_comment'></div>方朝家大有为之日，惟万物更新而询于刍荛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181038_comment'></div>非天下不敢言之时，故一夫进说而宽其罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181038_comment'></div>况夫自汉而下，有唐以来，贤良为举者凡几人，得失最明者惟二子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181038_comment'></div>以谷永之附托，而转攻世主之过咎，则今之愚者所不能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181038_comment'></div>以刘蕡之量切，而卒为有司之弃遗，则古之贤者或不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181038_comment'></div>殊惭谫陋，亦预甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181038_comment'></div>此盖某官讲求治体而务在得人，崇倡化风而乐于进善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181038_comment'></div>权衡之平也，不私高下于彼物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181038_comment'></div>钧轴之运也，不系刚柔于我心，是致孤生，偶尘高选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181038_comment'></div>昔之谋道，素闻取舍之大方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181038_comment'></div>今也丁辰，益励始终之常节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181038_comment'></div>倘力行而寡过，亦论报之一端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181038_comment'></div>过此以还，非敢语及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1181038_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年5月</a>　通判蜀州，有谢公画像记。作品：《巡抚谢公画像记》<div id='poem_1181115' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181115' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181115?labeling=true' target='_blank'>巡抚谢公画像记<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181115")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181115_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181115'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181115'>真宗景德三年夏四月，西南方有大星，占者谓应在蜀分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181115_comment'></div>上恻然动心，以为蜀去朝廷远，民之疾苦尤难知，天有异象，可畏不可忽，其择廷臣之贤而通世务者，往绥元元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181115_comment'></div>于是公以屯田员外郎巡抚利、益，又诏同九河张公咏议鼓铸利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181115_comment'></div>乃考铁价，制钱币，重轻适均，物估用平，众甚便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181115_comment'></div>时方寇乱之馀，百弊滋起，土俗凋困，惟九河公洎公相与谋议，作为宪令，安全舒息，极尽统要，俾其世世子孙，恃之以生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181115_comment'></div>故张公之治蜀，为天下最，实公有以助之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181115_comment'></div>既而举部吏数十，执政以多为疑，公请连坐，冀其必用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181115_comment'></div>自尔奉使，举吏皆连坐，而公之举者，大半有立于时矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181115_comment'></div>蜀土旧风，凡奉使来者，绘像天庆之仙游阁，公之后六十有四年，其孙司封郎中景初师厚以按刑之命至，故亦绘公之像于壁，所以推崇先烈，而永蜀人之瞻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181115_comment'></div>恭惟真宗皇帝承天下熙盛之极，恩隆泽厚，及民骨髓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181115_comment'></div>跂行喙息，罔不欣戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181115_comment'></div>然而星变一出，则恐惧警戒，以蜀为忧，分命良臣，审究时病，岂非奉天爱民之心乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181115_comment'></div>惟公纯诚大略，深体上意，施设有原，期底静安，岂非推己济物之义乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181115_comment'></div>夫奉天爱民，圣君之令德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181115_comment'></div>推己济物，贤臣之能事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181115_comment'></div>王道之起，莫先于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181115_comment'></div>而君臣两得，惠加远方，固可以著示后世，率为大范也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181115_comment'></div>公讳涛，字济之，为太子宾客、陈留伯，薨，以子绛知制诰，赠礼部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181115_comment'></div>若乃出处之本末，勋烈之始终，则范文正公之碑、欧阳公之志、尹师鲁之行状，悉得而载，此特治蜀之一端尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181115_comment'></div>师厚儒者，知治体风槩，落落有援世之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181115_comment'></div>时方改作，以福斯民，而或忘义利之辨，师厚累疏列其不可，无愧于祖构云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181115_comment'></div>熙宁四年五月二十日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1181115_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年12月</a>　通判蜀州，有文。作品：《府学经史阁落成记》<div id='poem_1181116' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181116' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181116?labeling=true' target='_blank'>府学经史阁落成记<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181116")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181116_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181116'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181116'>蜀学之盛冠天下而垂无穷者，其具有三：一曰文翁之石室，二曰周公之礼殿，三曰石壁之九经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181116_comment'></div>盖自周道衰微，乡校毁废，历秦之暴，至汉景、武间，典章风化，稍稍复讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181116_comment'></div>时文翁为蜀郡守，起学于市，减少府用度，以遗博士，遣诸生受业京师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181116_comment'></div>招子弟，为除更繇，且以补吏，或与之行县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181116_comment'></div>民用向劝，几比齐、鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181116_comment'></div>自尔郡国皆立学，实文翁倡之，所谓石室者存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181116_comment'></div>至东汉之季，四海板荡，兵火相仍，灾及校舍，弦诵寂绝，儒俗不振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181116_comment'></div>兴平中，郡将陈留高眹修旧补废，作为庙堂，模制闳伟，名号一新，所谓「礼殿」者见焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181116_comment'></div>及五代之乱，疆宇割裂，孟氏茍有剑南，百度草创，犹能取《易》、《诗》、《书》《、春秋》、《周礼》、《礼记》刻于石，以资学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181116_comment'></div>吾朝皇祐中，枢密直学士京兆田公加意文治，附以《仪礼》、《公羊》、《谷梁》传，所谓《九经》者备焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181116_comment'></div>始汉景末，距今凡十六代、千二百四十馀年，崩离变革，理势不常，而三事之盛，莫易其故，然则冠天下而垂无穷，非夸说也，考实以议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181116_comment'></div>惟经史阁之成，基势崇大，栋宇雄奥，下视众屋，匪隘即陋，聚书万卷，宝藏其间，斯亦近类三事，传千百年而不可辄废者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181116_comment'></div>龙图阁直学士濮阳吴公因其成也，会僚佐与蜀之士大夫及其讲师弟子凡若干人，饮酒以落之，德风洋洋，颂声愉愉，布宣于一方，有若阙里弟子集雩坛之下，咏歌先王道德而归诸圣门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181116_comment'></div>又若鲁侯至泮水之上，国人望其车旗和鸾而乐见之，视其颜色笑语而有感恩向化之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181116_comment'></div>呜呼，其盛矣夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181116_comment'></div>公纯诚好善，治有本末，所至以劝学为先，见一士可以语道，诱进之常若不及，乃诗人所谓能长育人材则天下喜乐者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181116_comment'></div>某于是推明公义而言焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181116_comment'></div>夫治性修身，以及国家天下，大略本之仁义，其文莫赅于经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181116_comment'></div>鉴见古之人注措发施，正邪粹驳，与其生民幸不幸，其迹莫著于史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181116_comment'></div>世之学者，不矜诵数而率履其言，不竞多闻而慎择其是，则为有得，亦庶几善学欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181116_comment'></div>初，阁之营建，皆幕府太常博士王君霁为之谋，君修洁有文，尝典吴兴郡学，挈其规范，来遗诸生，匪独施诸阁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181116_comment'></div>时熙宁四年十二月一日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1181116_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　论永康军不可废。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年3月</a>　为成都备武堂作记。作品：《成都新建备武堂记》<div id='poem_1181117' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181117' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181117?labeling=true' target='_blank'>成都新建备武堂记<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁五年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181117")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181117_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181117'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181117'>安危治乱之变，岂不难言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181117_comment'></div>人之情狃常习故，舍先几，取后患，盖亦多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181117_comment'></div>今朝廷所谓外忧者，无如西北，故秦、晋、赵、魏皆宿劲兵为之用，治军抗武，于政最先，而天下之势亦以为最重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181117_comment'></div>夫重轻者，天下之异势，安危治乱所从出，易而无备，则变逆之资也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181117_comment'></div>汉之衰，冀州之兵起，唐之季，桂林之戍叛，祸结不解，乃底灭亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181117_comment'></div>前辙往鉴，足以惩警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181117_comment'></div>议者知三路之为重，而不知蜀之不可为轻，岂善计乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181117_comment'></div>夫蜀之四隅，绵亘数千里，土腴物衍，赀货以蕃，财利贡赋，率四海三之一，县官指谓外府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181117_comment'></div>北倚剑阁，险绝天下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181117_comment'></div>东连獞獠，蟠聚深固；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181117_comment'></div>西南皆蛮诏，自古犷彊，唐天宝后，尝与吐蕃并力，以二十万众，三道入寇，又尝止成都西郛，大掠华人数万而南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181117_comment'></div>方其王政衰圮，则奸豪凭险自安，或七八十载不以赋税归中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181117_comment'></div>吾朝混平寰宇，恩柔威御，咸有深意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181117_comment'></div>淳化之际，吏暴于上，泽壅不流，经制烬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181117_comment'></div>民心怀危，盗乘而作，起甲午，距庚子，七年三乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181117_comment'></div>狂夫一呼，群应如响，今日取某州，明日陷某县，向风辄靡，何啻卷席之易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181117_comment'></div>戴白父老，往往犹言其状，闻者为之寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181117_comment'></div>然则戎防军政，敢一日废邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181117_comment'></div>龙图濮阳吴公之开府也，驭兵如民，条教详明，凡居处饮食之具，与其役任之劳逸，先治以宜，用壹厥心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181117_comment'></div>乃度府门之右，作备武堂，所以讲师律而训戎伍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181117_comment'></div>日练月习，率有定令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181117_comment'></div>数视屡阅，飨劳继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181117_comment'></div>金鸣鼓奏，士倍其勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181117_comment'></div>万众旁睨，震动耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181117_comment'></div>实镇守之重务，氓俗之深利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181117_comment'></div>昔晋武既平吴，欲去州郡兵，以衒治安，虽山涛、卢钦力陈大本，以为非是，亦莫能用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181117_comment'></div>及永宁之后，寇难交起，则郡国无备，不能制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181117_comment'></div>唐穆宗初，两河既定，萧俛、段文昌谓武不可黩，乃议销兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181117_comment'></div>及燕赵之乱，始募市人以战，复丧河朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181117_comment'></div>斯皆固不知变，拨去根本，茍近效，忘远图，安能成天下之务哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181117_comment'></div>蜀无事七十有三年，议者恬然不怪，民尚嬉乐，恶闻干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181117_comment'></div>公一旦远思长虑，而及于此，不独为蜀之计，乃为朝廷计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181117_comment'></div>始民恶兵，异公之为，懦夫曲士，从而腾说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1181117_comment'></div>逮其久也，则曰「吾将赖之以安」，而说者亦愧悔不敢议《易》之《萃》：「君子以除戎器，戒不虞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1181117_comment'></div>兵法：「无恃敌之不至，恃吾有以待」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1181117_comment'></div>其公之意欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1181117_comment'></div>且鲁有治戎之备，足为世法，孔子序录，附于王言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1181117_comment'></div>《春秋》书治兵大阅，虽以义制文，中存奥训，盖亦国之大事，谨兴作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1181117_comment'></div>堂之成，敢不第叙本末及其岁月云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1181117_comment'></div>熙宁五年三月一日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1181117_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年11月5日</a>　为华阳薛文恭公真像作记。作品：《薛文恭公尚书真像记》<div id='poem_1181118' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181118' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181118?labeling=true' target='_blank'>薛文恭公尚书真像记<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁五年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年11月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181118")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181118_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181118'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181118'>尝观西汉之兴，高祖勤于创业，谋臣猛将，乘时而起，相与经营，乃底靖康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181118_comment'></div>功成事济，咸享封爵，其君臣恩义之笃，则著位于朝，藏籍于庙，示以带砺，申以盟信，期之千百年而无有绝灭，厥初岂不盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181118_comment'></div>及二三世，或寖衰落，以至除国失姓，甚者乃陷庸保，何物理隆替不常如是耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181118_comment'></div>抑其后裔不克嗣守，而先烈因隳没也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181118_comment'></div>永言堂构菑穫之论，宜为寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181118_comment'></div>宋有重德君子尚书薛文恭公，讳某字某，世为华阳人，太平兴国中擢进士第，遂居某郡，至景祐某年薨于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181118_comment'></div>历事三圣，率有大节，出入中外，风迹蔼然，书在国史，实显以光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181118_comment'></div>诸孙之得录者凡若干人，西京左藏库使某，其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181118_comment'></div>按刑总兵，留蜀五稔，欲求远祖之丘陇而展省之，则陵谷异变，终不能识；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181118_comment'></div>欲询族属党巷之旧而亲接之，则契阔流散，亦莫得知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181118_comment'></div>盖仕宦四方，岁月绵久，而情好不相通故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181118_comment'></div>平居感慨，每有故乡之念，于是绘公真像于玉局观之西室，庶以荣里闬之观，而慰士林之思，其尊先贵本之心亦勤矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181118_comment'></div>惟蜀去朝廷最远，而贤士大夫最多，或以忠义立，或以文章称，或以操行著，盖自汉而下，世常有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181118_comment'></div>惟公生于盛时，能以道德致位八座，而子孙又能蒙其遗泽馀美，保有爵位，既蕃且昌，匪惟不坠乃祖之烈，而亦足以夸耀吾蜀之事，远视前古，皆无愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181118_comment'></div>夫于国为名臣，于乡为先生，存有远业，没有重名，此晚辈所以仰望而矜式者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181118_comment'></div>某闻公之风，用自饬励，继以左藏君之请，故从而记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181118_comment'></div>熙宁五年十一月五日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1181118_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　作李平墓志铭。作品：《陇西李君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181147' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181147' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181147?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陇西李君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁五年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181147")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181147_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181147'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181147'>皇祐甲午正月二十六日，陇西李君以疾终于家，享年七十，贫不克葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181147_comment'></div>熙宁壬子十二月二十二日，其子著作佐郎逢始以君及夫人毕氏之丧葬于大邑县依仁乡临江里，循宜考吉，务中礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181147_comment'></div>君讳平，字仲和，世居唐安郡，有高行三，皆众人所难能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181147_comment'></div>淳化中，蜀寇起，大扰州邑，虽父子或不相携持以遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181147_comment'></div>母刘氏方娠，君才十岁，侍而往，俱匿野泽中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181147_comment'></div>既生子，病且不粒，君昼夜望天号泣，若以危难诉之，求完其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181147_comment'></div>已而采蔬如药者，煮以饲，疾乃愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181147_comment'></div>会有盗过，又得所弃米，以具饘粥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181147_comment'></div>盗稍息，扶以还舍，父老惊异叹服，谓其笃孝，为神灵阴助，虽汉江次翁、唐支叔才殆不能过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181147_comment'></div>既长，庄谨自律，鄙绝玩好，善治家，不为米盐斗筲之计，而田至数顷，赀数万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181147_comment'></div>诸弟欲析而享，君一毫不忍私，罄所有与之，里人称其友爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181147_comment'></div>自是不复营产，惟聚书延贤师友以教子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181147_comment'></div>或告之宜少蓄藏，庸畀后裔，君曰：「吾子而力学，他日能大吾门，其得失岂润屋比耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181147_comment'></div>毕氏性懿淑，能尽妇道于内外，仁而好施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181147_comment'></div>常阅书，善诲诸子，往往执经问其大旨，闻弦诵吟讽之声则喜见容色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181147_comment'></div>子与朋友归，必亲馈馔，虽贫不敢废礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181147_comment'></div>享年五十有一，至和庚寅六月二十七日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181147_comment'></div>故李氏家范最号雍睦，盖夫人有助于君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181147_comment'></div>君之先世多隐晦乡闾，曾祖充，祖勤，父圜，皆不仕进，至君以高行饬齐其家，而逢遂以显，得非庆善之报欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181147_comment'></div>子四人，其长乃著佐君也，字承之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181147_comment'></div>曰适，曰迁，曰遘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181147_comment'></div>适，从承之官秭归，死年三十四，今祔葬于亲之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181147_comment'></div>迁，继夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181147_comment'></div>遘，举进士，未第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181147_comment'></div>三女，早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181147_comment'></div>予早从度支阎公颙学，公材高识明，于人物少许可，常器奖承之，予因与之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181147_comment'></div>承之有文而敏于政，君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181147_comment'></div>将葬其亲，来求铭，予其敢辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181147_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1181147'>孝其亲，友其弟，训其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181147_comment'></div>三德备，宜炽而昌，验于后世。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1181147_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　与胡右丞唱和，有诗。作品：《奉和胡右丞视学所赋》《再和胡右丞视学》<div id='poem_502618' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_502618' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/502618?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和胡右丞视学所赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_502618")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_502618_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_502618'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_502618'>成都学最古，肇自西汉时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_502618'>寥寥千馀载，间有或盛衰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_502618'>庆历始下诏，四方如响随。<div id='poem_sentence_2_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_502618'>良哉乐安伯<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，治体由本基。<div id='poem_sentence_3_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_502618'>远模类文翁，故事循鲁僖。<div id='poem_sentence_4_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_502618'>课试月为度，讲解日有规。<div id='poem_sentence_5_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_502618'>教育犹父兄，片言不迩遗。<div id='poem_sentence_6_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_502618'>学子五百人，弦诵何仪仪。<div id='poem_sentence_7_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_502618'>陶成礼义俗，大变西南维。<div id='poem_sentence_8_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_502618'>距此已一世，继者贤其谁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_502618'>胡公庙堂老，天子深倚毗。<div id='poem_sentence_10_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_502618'>下车急先务，劝学为之师。<div id='poem_sentence_11_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_502618'>时异心则同，两哲吹埙篪。<div id='poem_sentence_12_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_502618'>作诗遗诸生，字字皆典彝。<div id='poem_sentence_13_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_502618'>近欲美材成，远使纯风熙。<div id='poem_sentence_14_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_502618'>砻石建巨堂，竖柱不复攲。<div id='poem_sentence_15_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_502618'>九经满四壁，高下相支持。<div id='poem_sentence_16_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_502618'>首尾传注完，粲然日星垂。<div id='poem_sentence_17_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_502618'>斯经与斯堂，天下难等夷<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_18_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_502618'>度地得胜势，西隅敞高扉。<div id='poem_sentence_19_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_502618'>气象自宏显，出门见通逵。<div id='poem_sentence_20_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_502618'>嘉木种千本，敷阴接春晖。<div id='poem_sentence_21_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_502618'>人将不剪伐，异日甘棠枝。<div id='poem_sentence_22_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_502618'>贱子昔在泮，执经趋绛帷。<div id='poem_sentence_23_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_502618'>尝闻先生训，敢告多士知。<div id='poem_sentence_24_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_502618'>读书有本统，宜先穷是非。<div id='poem_sentence_25_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_502618'>微言率简易，众说殊支离。<div id='poem_sentence_26_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_502618'>详观圣贤迹，于我犹蓍龟。<div id='poem_sentence_27_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_502618'>不独事辞章，华葩竞葳蕤。<div id='poem_sentence_28_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_502618'>岂徒换爵禄，称谓生光辉。<div id='poem_sentence_29_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_502618'>立已如远游，纵横亦多岐。<div id='poem_sentence_30_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_502618'>取舍各异辙，义利难两驰。<div id='poem_sentence_31_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_502618'>一足少蹭蹬，终身陷污卑。<div id='poem_sentence_32_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_502618'>君子与小人，古今不同归。<div id='poem_sentence_33_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_502618'>勉哉笃志操，行副公所期。<div id='poem_sentence_34_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_502618'></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_502618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_502618'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_502618_0'>⑴ 自注：蒋公自谓，盖从郡望与封爵也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_18_502618_0'>⑵ 自注：洛雍虽有石经，未若蜀本注释之完。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_502618_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_502619' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_502619' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/502619?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再和胡右丞视学</a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_502619")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_502619_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_502619'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_502619'>士有幸不幸，所逢皆一时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_502619'>道隆学自正，文敝俗亦衰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_502619'>匪惟古今异，况复好恶随。<div id='poem_sentence_2_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_502619'>观诗不观政，争议毓与基<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：诗有孙毓、王基之学。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_502619'>穷经不穷法，区区论桓僖。<div id='poem_sentence_4_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_502619'>必得大匠诲，然后圆中规。<div id='poem_sentence_5_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_502619'>譬欲考躔度，亦先由浑仪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_502619'>所以君子教，众材无弃遗。<div id='poem_sentence_7_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_502619'>公来镇西州，为民张四维。<div id='poem_sentence_8_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_502619'>且曰化未孚，执咎归之谁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_502619'>醇醲造礼义，偷薄生夸毗。<div id='poem_sentence_10_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_502619'>予其本庠序，动以经为师。<div id='poem_sentence_11_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_502619'>善道易牖进，应和如埙篪。<div id='poem_sentence_12_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_502619'>自此石室生，处躬无匪彝。<div id='poem_sentence_13_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_502619'>勤诚戒挑达，美颂赞缉熙。<div id='poem_sentence_14_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_502619'>屡闻讲鼓集，不见儒冠攲。<div id='poem_sentence_15_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_502619'>远或千里至，箧笥相携持。<div id='poem_sentence_16_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_502619'>公堂坐无地，布满东西垂。<div id='poem_sentence_17_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_502619'>学殖务栽培，心茅悉芟夷。<div id='poem_sentence_18_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_502619'>前瞻数仞墙，竞欲趋公扉。<div id='poem_sentence_19_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_502619'>谓公富经术，执卷将问逵。<div id='poem_sentence_20_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_502619'>诵公勤学篇，华柔鄙玄晖。<div id='poem_sentence_21_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_502619'>杏坛乘春风，一日千万枝。<div id='poem_sentence_22_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_502619'>昔公长乌台，奏囊成殿帷。<div id='poem_sentence_23_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_502619'>药石尽晦密，世人罕闻知。<div id='poem_sentence_24_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_502619'>今公倡儒教，群情革其非。<div id='poem_sentence_25_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_502619'>道胜逢大壮，文明契重离。<div id='poem_sentence_26_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_502619'>继有巨篇作，拜贶如受龟。<div id='poem_sentence_27_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_502619'>咸韶奏清庙，音中爽与蕤。<div id='poem_sentence_28_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_502619'>琳琅聚宝肆，亘夜腾晶辉。<div id='poem_sentence_29_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_502619'>蛙鼓畏不鸣，鼠璞羞路岐。<div id='poem_sentence_30_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_502619'>信矣蜀政美，声闻已四驰。<div id='poem_sentence_31_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_502619'>海宇翘首望，天高终听卑。<div id='poem_sentence_32_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_502619'>行闻十行诏，匪朝促公归。<div id='poem_sentence_33_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_502619'>虽欲在泮饮，盛事安可期。<div id='poem_sentence_34_502619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_502619'></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_502619_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
彭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ca0496a51c2247059e5f176f44537d35_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ca0496a51c2247059e5f176f44537d35");'><span id='ca0496a51c2247059e5f176f44537d35_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1077')">1073-1077年</a>，46-50岁</div><div id='ca0496a51c2247059e5f176f44537d35' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　是年，迁知彭州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　在知彭州任上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　在知彭州任上。有记文。作品：《蜀州新堰记》《文与可画墨竹枯木记》《鹿鸣燕诗序》<div id='poem_1181119' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181119' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181119?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蜀州新堰记<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁八年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181119")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181119_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181119'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181119'>熙宁七年冬十二月朔，唐安新堰成，广民利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181119_comment'></div>岷山之旁，三水合而北注，至郡之东隅与大江会，湍悍湓激，又溃而五，霖潦间作，横山散漫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181119_comment'></div>高则没丘垄，下则漂田庐，止者患溺，行者苦泞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181119_comment'></div>江之故道，日漏且涸，弃失馀润，不能浸远，末壖之稼，屡植尽槁，盖八九年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181119_comment'></div>渠江黎希声既守郡，深恤隐弊，加意于此，思有所以捍防之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181119_comment'></div>欲责于兵以致力，则无羡卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181119_comment'></div>欲出于廪以充食，则无馀粮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181119_comment'></div>欲重困元元以起大役，则素所不忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181119_comment'></div>时旱甚谷贵，流徙满道，皆仰给于公养，而壮者仅三千人，晨夕饱饫，可任以事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181119_comment'></div>会新津老人陈汝玉亦状本末以献，乃按度冲会，布为巨楗，制导异派，归之旧踪，循源而下，大患自弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181119_comment'></div>始秋八月，至是有成，凡溉田三万九千亩，濒侧之民，安而粒者无虑五千家，其为利亦博矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181119_comment'></div>诚能讲葺以时，久且完固，虽或亢沴，岁望庶几不失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181119_comment'></div>予尝究利害废兴之说，盖生民幸不幸系焉，君子必审而后动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181119_comment'></div>大率因物之自然，徇人之所欲，不矜妄智，不计近功，则事之有作简以济，民之受惠远以深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181119_comment'></div>若乃自用而凿，智巧饰伪，背天理，反物性，茍期成效，以要利取宠于一时，而不虑吾民之困戚者，彼安足与论利害耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181119_comment'></div>西南虽号沃壤，然赋敛百出于农，耕夫日夜劬劳，而三时有馁色，百亩之家，占名上籍，而歉岁或不免饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181119_comment'></div>惟是沟畎渠防之务，于政最切，上之人茍置不议，非所以抚惠赤子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181119_comment'></div>希声儒者，通经术，以忠厚治，常先民急，故所施如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181119_comment'></div>昔汉循吏皆以乐易德爱为之本，济时及物，凛然足称，若召翁卿之于南阳、王仲通之于芍陂，前史嘉其风迹，著范来世，则唐安新堰者可略而不述哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181119_comment'></div>八年四月五日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1181119_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1181120' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181120' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181120?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文与可画墨竹枯木记<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁八年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年6月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181120")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181120_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181120'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181120'>君子之智思能过于人，则事无巨细，皆足以取高，此众人所以尊仰钦爱之不已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181120_comment'></div>画者，中有拟象，而发于笔墨之间，茍臻其极，则近见群物之情状，远参造化之功力，自古贤俊，往往能之，盖取其如此欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181120_comment'></div>与可之于墨竹枯木，世之好事者皆知而贵，子瞻尝谓尽得其理，固不妄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181120_comment'></div>顷年来成都，画此两物于嘉祐长老纪师之方丈，纪师宝之，以誇识者，乃西州僧舍胜事之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181120_comment'></div>与可在文馆二十年，其材可巨用，将老矣，尚恂恂小州，胸中之蕴，曾不少露，通塞荣悴，无一毫罥诸心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181120_comment'></div>名教至乐之馀，时作墨竹枯木一二，以寓其幽怀远趣，真所谓粹静君子也，岂特笔墨之间有以过人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181120_comment'></div>知则语其大，不知则语其小，知不知于与可何损益耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181120_comment'></div>此可与高爽明达者言，不可与鄙闇道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181120_comment'></div>熙宁八年六月十日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1181120_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年10月</a>　为同年进士何大章之父何敏作墓志铭。作品：《光禄寺丞致仕何君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181142' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181142' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181142?labeling=true' target='_blank'>光禄寺丞致仕何君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁八年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181142")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181142_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181142'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181142'>何氏之先，盖晋之卿佐封于韩者，子孙因以为氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181142_comment'></div>秦灭韩，其后流散四方，或谓韩为何，故汉魏以来始著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181142_comment'></div>何氏有居于闽者，至瓒乃显，即君六世祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181142_comment'></div>仕后唐，历太原留守，除西川副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181142_comment'></div>会孟氏僭窃，耻屈其下，饮恨以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181142_comment'></div>子柔不能东，乃家青城，遂为青城人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181142_comment'></div>柔生令昕，令昕生缮，不幸逢乱离，无复振起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181142_comment'></div>缮生中，即君皇考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181142_comment'></div>任道晦处，无意官禄，以聚书为能，以赋诗为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181142_comment'></div>蜀之耆儒李畋渭卿、戈渊仲颜皆与之友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181142_comment'></div>子四人，君其季也，讳敏，字希颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181142_comment'></div>简悫庄重，克承厥家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181142_comment'></div>贫而能力生，以养亲奉祀，至于抚养百口，靡有不给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181142_comment'></div>富而能好善，以训其子孙，至于起家从仕，翘然有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181142_comment'></div>旁支外属之无归，则倍仰而济，乡闾识者，以吉人君子称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181142_comment'></div>熙宁初，今天子祀南郊，以君之子大章登朝，封大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181142_comment'></div>四年，明堂大飨，迁光禄寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181142_comment'></div>六年十一月某日终于家，享年七十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181142_comment'></div>八年十月某日葬于县之某乡某里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181142_comment'></div>君娶李氏，今封仁寿县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181142_comment'></div>生三子：大章，皇祐四年中进士第五，迁太常博士，通判汉州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181142_comment'></div>大临、某，皆勉饬乡行，不坠先训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181142_comment'></div>孙四人：宗元，荣州荣德县令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181142_comment'></div>宗范，合州巴川县令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181142_comment'></div>某、某，悉志于学，期以自立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181142_comment'></div>惟何氏来蜀，中叶不耀，至博士君始以学文得禄，而荣德、巴川二君又能同时取科第，士议荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181142_comment'></div>君可谓有后矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181142_comment'></div>某与博士君同进士籍，且为姻家，君之葬也，敢志而铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181142_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1181142'>何迁于岷，五世至君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181142_comment'></div>既永以年，再光以恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181142_comment'></div>山之阿，江之濆，祗厥祀，传后昆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1181142_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　为同年进士张复之父张惟德作墓表。作品：《赠大理评事张府君墓表》<div id='poem_1181157' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181157' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181157?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠大理评事张府君墓表<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181157")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181157_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181157'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181157'>南荣有道之士清河张君，既以皇祐初元三月己亥疾卒于家，春秋四十有九，三年十一月庚午葬于荣德县荣川乡归政里先陇之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181157_comment'></div>后二十五年，君之子复为丞秘书，天子大享霈赦，赠君大理寺丞，均庆赉，贲潜德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181157_comment'></div>太博君擢进士第，与予同时，每惧先烈之不耀，思得推叙大略，著示后世，乃求予文表诸墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181157_comment'></div>按君谱系由来最远，盖晋司空华、唐曲江公九龄后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181157_comment'></div>天宝中，有从明皇西幸者，占南荣，为钜姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181157_comment'></div>曾祖讳俨，建隆时王师伐蜀，率土兵导所向，补先锋将，力战有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181157_comment'></div>祖讳让，亦以智能补和义县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181157_comment'></div>考讳文焕，摄州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181157_comment'></div>君讳惟德，字辅之，幼以孝谨闻，执亲丧不忘礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181157_comment'></div>读书先经术，务穷大旨，尤好《春秋》、《孟子》，凡杂家駮说未尝顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181157_comment'></div>一试于乡，不荐，遂无仕进意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181157_comment'></div>训子孙以雍睦清慎为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181157_comment'></div>平居择交游，恶茍合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181157_comment'></div>间或赋诗见志以诲人，语纯格整。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181157_comment'></div>与朋友言，多援前史得失否臧，以相警励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181157_comment'></div>乡人善者好焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181157_comment'></div>君袁氏婿，其僚婿凡七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181157_comment'></div>袁，富族也，为之婿者，或私其赀币以豪，君独不尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181157_comment'></div>袁父母尝厌他婿之求，欲以馀积委君，则再拜避谢，卒不以一金自污。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181157_comment'></div>此其众人所难，而君子所贵者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181157_comment'></div>子男七人：曰纶，曰衍，曰复，曰衡，曰纪，曰绎，曰侃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181157_comment'></div>复即太博君，今知陵井监，履尚敦懿，居官有能名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181157_comment'></div>衡犹未仕，馀则亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181157_comment'></div>女四人：长适勾侨，次适袁绶，次未嫁而卒，季适袁璐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181157_comment'></div>孙男六人：希逸、希道已夭，希圣、希孟、希简、希古皆建侯宾王，舋舋向学，克承厥家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181157_comment'></div>孙女五人，归孙诰、贾麟、袁晦、句龟年、句师皋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181157_comment'></div>曾孙男十人，女六人，并幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181157_comment'></div>予尝阅史载，见昔人出处大致，若司空在晋、曲江公在唐，其德操义烈，皆社稷臣，虽百千年，犹使人仰畏不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181157_comment'></div>今考君谱系，原究本始，则二公之苗裔，固可书也，况嘉行有足纪乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181157_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1181157'>人之生无穷达显晦，傥有一节异于众，可以宪子孙、风流俗，则谓之不朽，非必高爵重位，乃取贵后世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181157_comment'></div>女有归矣，父母爱之，而私以金币，虽受之未为大过，君独无取，岂临财不茍其得欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181157_comment'></div>彼求而惟日不足者，闻君行谊可愧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181157_comment'></div>呜呼，廉哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1181157_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年10月</a>　为彭山人冯损之作墓志铭。作品：《长乐冯先生墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181146' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181146' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181146?labeling=true' target='_blank'>长乐冯先生墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁八年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181146")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181146_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181146'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181146'>蜀之有道君子冯先生讳某字损之，其先盖长乐郡著姓，自五代祖俦仕孟氏，任眉州司户参军，卒官，因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181146_comment'></div>曾祖少连，祖承谅，父知礼，皆为彭山人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181146_comment'></div>先生生而聪颖，与他儿异，才五岁，闻邻人诵书辄喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181146_comment'></div>稍长，遂好学，读《五经》，尤专《诗》、《书》，探深抉奥，志其本统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181146_comment'></div>泛阅古史百氏，该综得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181146_comment'></div>举进士不第，退而讲学诲人，每正席横经，演明大旨，凡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1181146", 1181146, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>训传</span>之殊骋及其肤说，则判别是否，归于至当，学者多信向之，往往化而博强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181146_comment'></div>先生常曰：「学所以治性修身，而充吾之所有，非特誇论辨，要利禄为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181146_comment'></div>能积乎中，发而粹乎外，则无愧为君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181146_comment'></div>若夫贵贱荣辱，通塞险易，当以义命委之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181146_comment'></div>世俗所谓厄穷憔悴者，安足累吾灵台」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181146_comment'></div>是以抗志砺行，愈困愈笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181146_comment'></div>口不出柔言，目不顾令色，不枉己以徇物，不违义以求人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181146_comment'></div>箪瓢藜藿，裕然白首，乃贫无谄怨，饭疏馀水，曲肱而乐之徒欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181146_comment'></div>娶唐氏，亡九年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181146_comment'></div>二子：长曰敢，静默有文，登进士科，累迁彭州军事判官，得禄就养，里人荣之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181146_comment'></div>次曰敏，力学慎检操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181146_comment'></div>盖隐德不位，而庆流于后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181146_comment'></div>三女，皆嫁良族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181146_comment'></div>孙男三人，女五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181146_comment'></div>先生享年九十一，熙宁八年五月某日，卒于天彭之官舍，十月某日，葬于彭山安镇乡祖茔之次，举唐氏之丧以祔焉，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181146_comment'></div>其平生所著歌诗若干卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181146_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1181146'>寿考、康宁、好德、终命，此四者，先生兼享之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181146_comment'></div>不富以利，而富以道，《洪范》之五福亦具矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181146_comment'></div>昔太史公以颜、蹠之分，求天道之是非，盖疑焉而未之得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181146_comment'></div>今先生积学慎行，而所享如此，其嗣子又能承家显荣，则报施善人，诚当其理，于先生何疑哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1181146_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年4月</a>　论交趾寇广西事。又奏乞朝廷为成都选差官兵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年4月23日</a>　知成都府蔡延庆改知渭州，作诗送别。作品：《送蔡帅赴平凉》<div id='poem_502694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_502694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/502694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送蔡帅赴平凉</a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年4月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_502694")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_502694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_502694'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_502694'>剑外开三蜀，回中宿万兵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
