id='poem_sentence_1_502694'>召还宜北觐，赐钺又西征。<div id='poem_sentence_1_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_502694'>体貌均先后，权纲一重轻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_502694'>渊衷尤慎简，舆意尚难平。<div id='poem_sentence_3_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_502694'>伊昔藩条振，于今治体成。<div id='poem_sentence_4_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_502694'>有为终简易，无迹但恢闳。<div id='poem_sentence_5_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_502694'>笔下销顽弊，樽前得隐情。<div id='poem_sentence_6_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_502694'>快如长剑立，通若巨河倾。<div id='poem_sentence_7_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_502694'>阔刃从虚落，醇源及物情。<div id='poem_sentence_8_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_502694'>山川增气象，草木遂勾萌。<div id='poem_sentence_9_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_502694'>暖褐三冬足，丰畴百室盈。<div id='poem_sentence_10_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_502694'>咏歌今父母，畏服古神明。<div id='poem_sentence_11_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_502694'>方幸华轮柅，俄闻瑞节迎。<div id='poem_sentence_12_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_502694'>渴心犹借寇，翘望欲还琼。<div id='poem_sentence_13_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_502694'>况复盘关路，常瞻部使旌。<div id='poem_sentence_14_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_502694'>十连依玉帐，一道固金城。<div id='poem_sentence_15_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_502694'>后诏光前出，新棠似旧荣。<div id='poem_sentence_16_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_502694'>于宣推德业，所至尽功名。<div id='poem_sentence_17_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_502694'>塞马宁非福，溟鹏岂问程。<div id='poem_sentence_18_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_502694'>惟期未温席，归去纂家声。<div id='poem_sentence_19_502694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_502694'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_502694_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年10月22日</a>　论劾王中正。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年11月</a>　十月，知成都府冯京召知枢密院，十一月离蜀，作诗送之。作品：《送冯枢密》<div id='poem_502691' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_502691' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/502691?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送冯枢密</a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_502691")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_502691_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_502691'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_502691'>帅领来全蜀，抡魁祗一人<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_502691'>崧高雪山势，清彻锦江津。<div id='poem_sentence_1_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_502691'>旒冕思长策，机衡属老臣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_502691'>部中方拜赐，天下又回春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_502691'>出处无非道，安危系此身。<div id='poem_sentence_4_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_502691'>岩赡殊庆快，涂说敢开陈。<div id='poem_sentence_5_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_502691'>圣运重熙久，皇威万里振。<div id='poem_sentence_6_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_502691'>勒兵充宇宙，按剑待烟尘。<div id='poem_sentence_7_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_502691'>权术轻三表，韬铃贵五申。<div id='poem_sentence_8_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_502691'>招怀及蛮徼，指顾下洮岷。<div id='poem_sentence_9_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_502691'>文诰传荒服，天声压外邻。<div id='poem_sentence_10_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_502691'>捷书连岁上，故壤一朝新。<div id='poem_sentence_11_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_502691'>计费千金易，论功百胜频。<div id='poem_sentence_12_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_502691'>征衣空杼轴，战骨委荆榛。<div id='poem_sentence_13_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_502691'>水旱乾坤惨，锥刀畎亩贫。<div id='poem_sentence_14_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_502691'>人情危欲镇，帝泽壅难均。<div id='poem_sentence_15_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_502691'>幸会公归国，相欢物在钧。<div id='poem_sentence_16_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_502691'>华心生草野，和气满枫宸。<div id='poem_sentence_17_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_502691'>士论归依切，风谣祷颂真。<div id='poem_sentence_18_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_502691'>嘉谟凭献纳，大事费经纶。<div id='poem_sentence_19_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_502691'>治术关休戚，规模有革因。<div id='poem_sentence_20_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_502691'>号寒思挟纩，引哺愿尝珍。<div id='poem_sentence_21_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_502691'>图治虽更化，封侯漫富民。<div id='poem_sentence_22_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_502691'>高明深鉴照，密勿定咨询。<div id='poem_sentence_23_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_502691'>悟主言称舜，论兵谕借秦。<div id='poem_sentence_24_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_502691'>无为群动悦，不陈四夷宾。<div id='poem_sentence_25_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_502691'>宝鼎千钧重，薰琴九奏纯。<div id='poem_sentence_26_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_502691'>放怀留化日，反掌叙彝伦。<div id='poem_sentence_27_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_502691'>邦体还清静，王纲务率循。<div id='poem_sentence_28_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_502691'>太平勋业就，寰海被尧仁。<div id='poem_sentence_29_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_502691'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_502691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_502691'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_502691_0'>⑴ 自注：由进士状元镇蜀者，惟公一人。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_502691_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年2月</a>　上奏放免宽剩役钱，不报。作品：《奏乞放免宽剩役钱状》<div id='poem_1180877' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180877' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180877?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞放免宽剩役钱状<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁十年三月十日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180877")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180877_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180877'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180877'>今具本州九陇等四县，自熙宁六年至九年原科役钱共计二十二万六千七百八十七贯六百二文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180877_comment'></div>已支、见在如后：已支一十七万八千八十贯九百三十七文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180877_comment'></div>见在宽剩钱四万八千七百六贯六百六十五文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180877_comment'></div>右，谨具如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180877_comment'></div>臣伏以朝廷欲宽为役，立法召募，使民均出佣钱，雇人应役，初无过敛民财之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180877_comment'></div>有司奉法，惟恐不能足用，遂于一年合支役钱数外，增添科出，谓之宽剩，盖欲准备修葺桥道廨舍，并买置什物之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180877_comment'></div>官中逐年支用虽少，民间两科所出甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180877_comment'></div>自熙宁六年施行役法以来，至今四年，臣本州四县已有宽剩钱四万八千七百馀贯，今岁又须科纳一万馀贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180877_comment'></div>以成都一路计之，无虑五六十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180877_comment'></div>推之天下，现今约有六七百万贯文宽剩在官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180877_comment'></div>岁岁如此，科出不已，民间何以送纳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180877_comment'></div>况今泉币绝乏，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1180877", 1180877, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>货法</span>不通，商旅农夫，最受其弊，盖是现钱大半入官，市井少有转用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180877_comment'></div>臣愚深恐朝廷不知免役钱外有此宽剩数目，伏乞圣慈指挥诸路提举仓司，契勘现在宽剩钱数，约度支得几岁不至阙乏，霈发德音，特与免数年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180877_comment'></div>或乞逐年限定数目，不得过役钱十分之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180877_comment'></div>所贵民力不至重困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180877_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1180877'>〔贴黄〕朝廷如以臣言可采，只乞下司农寺取索今日以前天下支役钱外宽剩钱数，便见利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180877_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1180877'>〔又〕臣伏见二年以来，川中见钱绝少，物价减半，银每两、绢每匹各只直一贯四五百文，米每石一贯二三百文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180877_comment'></div>其如免役并宽剩钱并依旧数送纳，比之熙宁六年所出，即似加一倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180877_comment'></div>若不契勘除减，深恐民间不易。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1180877_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年3月</a>　为常溥作墓志铭。作品：《尚书屯田郎中致仕常公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181137' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181137' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181137?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书屯田郎中致仕常公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁十年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181137")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181137_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181137'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181137'>尚书屯田郎中致仕常公，享年七十有八，熙宁丁巳岁正月朔日卒于成都孙男安民之官舍，即以三月壬申葬于大邑县多融乡安宁里先茔之次，从大夫礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181137_comment'></div>公讳溥，字周用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181137_comment'></div>其先居长安，自唐季有为唐安掾著，子孙因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181137_comment'></div>至高祖某，则又徙临邛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181137_comment'></div>曾祖某，祖某，遂为邛大姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181137_comment'></div>父某，以信义著乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181137_comment'></div>淳化盗起，能与众捍之，盗不敢犯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181137_comment'></div>又能率土军迎王师以从讨，活污染者千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181137_comment'></div>蜀平议赏，不愿仕，君子知其有后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181137_comment'></div>洎公之贵，累赠工部侍郎，追封母杜氏长安县太君，继母费氏永康县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181137_comment'></div>公天资纯愿，少力学，既冠，从乡举，辄先诸进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181137_comment'></div>景祐五年始登第，调陕府陕县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181137_comment'></div>母丧，父继殁，服除，授成州南溪县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181137_comment'></div>旁邑有地讼，指七木堰、暮露滩为说，凡十七年不决，部使者委公听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181137_comment'></div>公考验图卷，详辨讹误所谓「漆木、墓路」者，以折分争，人伏其明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181137_comment'></div>官满，调鄂州节度掌书记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181137_comment'></div>炭场吏私贷官缗，将陷重辟，公悯其非大恶，偶不知法，遂至是，谕以偿之，免九人死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181137_comment'></div>改著作佐郎、知濠州定远县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181137_comment'></div>县素多讼，吏积习为奸，号难治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181137_comment'></div>公以简处剧，以严济恕，纲开条举，乃至无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181137_comment'></div>于是修孔子祠，会诸生，躬为课试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181137_comment'></div>时旱蝗相仍，公祷之必应，独一县沾洽，蝗亦及境而毙，诚忱感格，如古循吏之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181137_comment'></div>转秘书丞、太常博士，通判彭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181137_comment'></div>属县鹤鸣堰，岁岁冲溃，大破民产，公度视岸势，因水之性，凿高就下，得以不决，民蒙其利，乃用「常公」为堰之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181137_comment'></div>迁屯田员外郎、通判宁州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181137_comment'></div>遇英皇践祚恩，迁都官员外郎，亦以雩祀获报，郡人爱之，有号「都官雨」者，犹前世以御史称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181137_comment'></div>改职方员外郎，审官考其课在异等，荐为御史，不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181137_comment'></div>今天子即位，授屯田郎中，通判海州、提举楚海涟水盐纲，时年六十八矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181137_comment'></div>彊明无恙，满岁赏劳，当自宰府除便郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181137_comment'></div>一日，登景疏楼，感物赋诗，浩然有归意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181137_comment'></div>或劝之俟从心而去，公曰：「吾起白屋，位郎曹，于素志何负？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181137_comment'></div>士之进退，惟以义，必曰七十而谢，则非出于诚，出于法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181137_comment'></div>吾老矣，其西归乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1181137_comment'></div>岁时奉丘陇，旦暮会朋戚，啸歌觞咏，以佚吾生，其乐与宦游孰胜耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1181137_comment'></div>既得请，乃还临邛，号鹤峰归老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1181137_comment'></div>安车野服，惟所欲往，燕吟谐笑，终日欢然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1181137_comment'></div>凡如此者十年而没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1181137_comment'></div>公谦懿和裕，不忤于物，接人无少长贵贱，一以礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1181137_comment'></div>处事无艰易巨细，一以诚，真乐易君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1181137_comment'></div>凡平生所著杂文歌诗若干篇，为一集，传于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1181137_comment'></div>今枢密冯公之未仕，公尝以台辅期之，既而贵显，则亦报公之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1181137_comment'></div>议者谓公有知人之明，而冯公厚于义，莫不韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1181137_comment'></div>公娶何氏，有妇德，封仁和县君，春秋七十七，后公二十六日而终，举祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1181137_comment'></div>子二人：楫，黎州军事推官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1181137_comment'></div>构，尝举进士，已而退处，乐于名教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1181137_comment'></div>女六人：长适廖世卿，次适杜修辅，次适徐钧，次适宿松尉李寅，次适汉阳尉张伯遵，次适崔君平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1181137_comment'></div>孙男十人：长安道，预太学荐，早卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1181137_comment'></div>次安义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1181137_comment'></div>次安石，遂州节度推官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1181137_comment'></div>次安民，成都府府学教授；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1181137_comment'></div>次安雅、安中、安政、安节、安世、安术，皆务家学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1181137_comment'></div>孙女五人，重孙亦如之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1181137_comment'></div>公之葬也，教授君状其行来求铭，陶窃谓世之士大夫，或役于禄利，往往癃老未谢去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1181137_comment'></div>或谢而归，失素所嗜，则沮郁有闷容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1181137_comment'></div>或后裔慢于送往，以至暴棺累岁，不得即藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1181137_comment'></div>如公之勇退，退而能自得，及其亡也，子孙又能时而葬之，亦可以警昏薄、劝笃厚矣，敢不为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1181137_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1181137'>仕而知止，请老以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1181137_comment'></div>老而有终，葬不踰时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1181137_comment'></div>惟义保躬，公能履之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1181137_comment'></div>惟礼笃亲，子孙从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1181137_comment'></div>吁嗟公乎，无憾于斯。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1181137_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年3月8日</a>　上奏榷茶利害事。作品：《奏具置场买茶旋行出卖远方不便事状》<div id='poem_1180879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180879?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏具置场买茶旋行出卖远方不便事状<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁十年三月八日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年3月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180879")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180879'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180879'>今具本路置场买茶往熙河博卖，并尽榷诸州茶货入官，便收三分利息，旋行出卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180879_comment'></div>致令细民失业，枉陷刑宪，大于远方不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180879_comment'></div>谨具画一条列如后：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1180879'>一、臣伏以国家富有四海，山泽之利，多与民共。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180879_comment'></div>自仁祖临御以来，深知东南数路茶法之害，制诏有司，一切弛放，任令通商，货法流行，德泽深厚，圣时盛事，高出前世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180879_comment'></div>今天下茶法既通，而两川独行禁榷，此盖言利之臣不知本末，茍贪劳赏而妄为之，非所以绥静远方之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180879_comment'></div>况乎两川所出茶货，比方东南诸处，十不及一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180879_comment'></div>日月所照，文轨混同，法无二门，仁不异远，岂可诸路既许通商，两川却为禁地？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180879_comment'></div>亏损治体，莫甚于斯，乃为害之大者，故臣敢先言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180879_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特宽茶禁，所贵法令平一，以幸远方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1180879'>一、本路既为置场买茶，将往熙河等处，并逐旋取利出卖之后，更不许民间衷私买卖，遂令诸色人告捕，依《编敕禁榷茶法》断罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180879_comment'></div>州县承此指挥，后来累有成都府邛州百姓马吉等为衷私卖茶，被人告捕，有至徒罪，各追赏钱，一路之民，遂生怨诽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180879_comment'></div>盖缘立法太重，有害于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180879_comment'></div>大凡官中原有之物，民间私侵其利，方是犯禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180879_comment'></div>只如解州有盐池，民间煎者乃是私盐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180879_comment'></div>晋州有矾山，民间炼者乃是私矾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180879_comment'></div>今川蜀茶园，本是百姓两税田地，不出五谷，只是种茶，赋税一例折科<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，役钱一例均出，自来采茶货卖，以充衣食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180879_comment'></div>伏缘此茶本非官地所产，乃是百姓己物，显与解盐、晋矾事体不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180879_comment'></div>一旦立法，须令尽卖与官，或敢私相交易，便成犯禁，斤数稍重，乃至徒刑，仍没纳随行物色，别理赏钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180879_comment'></div>恭惟陛下仁圣恤物之心，必不如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1180879_comment'></div>伏乞别立条约，以救苛刻之弊，免使刑辟滋彰，有伤和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1180879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1180879'>一、本州导江县蒲村、堋口、小唐兴、木头等镇，各准茶场司指挥，尽数收买茶货入官，并已施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1180879_comment'></div>民之受弊，大率均一，惟导江县一处，尤为切害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1180879_comment'></div>盖缘本处是西山八州军隘口，自来通放部落入城博易买卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1180879_comment'></div>其蕃部别无现钱交易，只将到椒、蜡、草药之类，于铺户处换易茶货，归去吃用，谓之茶米。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1180879_comment'></div>或有疾病，用此疗治，旦暮不可暂阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1180879_comment'></div>今来官中须要现钱出卖，则蕃部难更将椒、蜡等物入场博买，若于铺户处博易，则铺户价例自然增长<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，蕃部买卖，便致阻节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1180879_comment'></div>况茂州事宜之后，人情方始安帖，岂宜更使茶货不通，别生边事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1180879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1180879'>一、茶园人户，多者岁出三五万斤，少者只及一二百斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1180879_comment'></div>自来隔年留下客放定钱，或指当茶苗，举取债负，准备粮米，雇召夫工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1180879_comment'></div>自上春以后，接续采取，乘时高下，相度货卖，中等每斤之利可得二十文，次者只有十文以来，累世相承，恃以为业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1180879_comment'></div>其铺户收贮变易，却以白土拌和，每斤之息，不及十文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1180879_comment'></div>所以川中茶价，不甚涌贵，民间日用充足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1180879_comment'></div>今来既被官中尽数收买，价直一定，若将银色准折，每两须高抬四五百文<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，或多支交子，少用现钱<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1180879_comment'></div>交子所支既多，钱陌又须亏折，则园户所收茶货，只得避罪纳官，安敢更求馀利？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1180879_comment'></div>一旦失业，何以为生？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1180879_comment'></div>臣恐户口逃移，赋役失陷，渐由此起<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1180879_comment'></div>又缘旋买旋卖，先抽三分之息，只此一事，极未为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1180879_comment'></div>日来州县逐旬各申时估，或增或减，官司据以为定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1180879_comment'></div>岂可朝买一贯之茶，暮收三百之利？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1180879_comment'></div>一日之内，贵贱两般，则州县所供实直遂成空文，有司出纳之际乃同聚敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1180879_comment'></div>且铺户既与官中出利，则民间岂有贱茶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1180879_comment'></div>日用之物，渐见不足，锥刀敝法，徒可敛怨，必非朝廷理财之本意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1180879_comment'></div>伏乞圣断，特赐改更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1180879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1180879'>一、本州所准茶场司今年二月二十四日指挥，限半月令园户、铺户尽数出卖旧茶，不得夹杂入官，如限满更不施行，如有违犯，并依法施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1180879_comment'></div>臣虽即时行下逐处，然计其日，限令至三月十日已满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1180879_comment'></div>缘民间累年积贮茶货，准备高价相度变卖，一旦偶因官中为买新茶，亦不预先晓示，忽然责立近限，令将旧茶疾出速卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1180879_comment'></div>若出限未卖，被人告捉，斤数稍重，即至杖脊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1180879_comment'></div>安有数日之内，尽底变易得行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1180879_comment'></div>旧茶因此大段减价，无赖小人辄有告捕之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1180879_comment'></div>臣寻具状称：若只限半月，令尽数出卖，则必是减落价例，变转不行，消失钱本，便见失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1180879_comment'></div>兼虑才出限日之后，被牙子或别人告捕送官，枉陷深刑，显属不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1180879_comment'></div>又缘新茶与旧茶色目不同，若将旧茶投税出卖，则与官中收买新茶事不相妨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1180879_comment'></div>本州须至申明，欲令逐场一面收买新茶，民间出卖所有旧茶，乞限至今年八月终，晓示园户并停塌之家，尽将赴场投税出卖，令税务公明声说，给引前去破卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1180879_comment'></div>仍乞指挥逐处官司，如有诸色人把捉到衷私买卖货，却须辨认新旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1180879_comment'></div>如是新茶，即乞依法施行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1180879_comment'></div>若是旧茶，只乞罪在捉事之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1180879_comment'></div>所贵积贮旧茶之家，破卖得行，不枉受罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1180879_comment'></div>两次申茶场司，未蒙指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1180879_comment'></div>若不许展限，则贮积旧茶之家，便见破荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1180879_comment'></div>如此措置，岂不害民？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1180879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_1180879'>一、官中买茶，明收三分利息，方行出卖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1180879_comment'></div>沿路税钱，尽已批过，更无分毫侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1180879_comment'></div>商旅兴贩，必是细算不行，难以尽数贩卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1180879_comment'></div>窃闻蜀州永康一处，现今积压茶五十六万馀斤在务，臣料将来出卖不尽之后，则必积压损坏，亏折官钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1180879_comment'></div>若般往熙河，亦误边计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1180879_comment'></div>或仍旧停贮，则岁课不登，难沾赏典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1180879_comment'></div>建议之臣，必须均匀配卖与贩茶之家，如此则他日铺户不胜其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1180879_comment'></div>伏乞指挥茶场司，具去年终已买及已卖数目申奏，仍令分析现馀茶货，若经隔年岁，合如何变转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1180879_comment'></div>即自然见得此法可与不可经久施用，免令言利之臣有误朝廷大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1180879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_1180879'>右，谨具如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1180879_comment'></div>所有茶禁不通，细民失业，刑辟太重，最于远方不便事理，并已条析如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1180879_comment'></div>臣窃见熙宁七年，朝廷遣李杞、蒲宗闵入川，相度买茶往熙河博马等事，当时使者急于进用，不察事体，遂认定逐年息钱四十万贯应付熙河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1180879_comment'></div>后来运茶积滞，岁课不足，即便擘画，却于彭、汉二州，逐年收买狭布各十万匹，名为折当脚钱，其实将布上所得之息充入茶利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1180879_comment'></div>自后又恐买布亦难敷及原数，则乞雇回脚船车般解盐入川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1180879_comment'></div>洎至盐法难行，则又乞将川中有茶去处并行收买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1180879_comment'></div>前后乖错，非止一事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1180879_comment'></div>只是切欲功赏，不恤民间病弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1180879_comment'></div>臣愚伏望圣慈特赐采察，所贵远方之俗，被惠安身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1180879_comment'></div>至如官史费耗，道涂阻节，税额亏损，得不补失，则臣不敢喋喋开陈，以渎天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1180879_comment'></div>乞以臣此奏下本路安抚，转运、提刑司，相度利害，特赐施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1180879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_1180879'>〔贴黄〕若蒙朝廷垂察，即乞下本路取索熙宁八年九月分永康县银价，比对茶场折银<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_80_1180879", 1180879, "Clauses/311/Comments/0")'>贯陌</span>，自见有无侵损园户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1180879_comment'></div>免令将来高价折银，亏损本州卖茶之家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1180879_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_1180879'>〔又〕臣所谓得不补失者，窃闻永康县熙宁九年发茶三百驮往熙河，除诸般费用及沿路批税外，计算每斤已是一百九十四文足，其兵士请米犹在数外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1180879_comment'></div>不知到熙河货卖所得几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1180879_comment'></div>如此事理，亦乞朝廷体察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_84_1180879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1180879'><span class='label'>按：</span>《净德集》卷一。又见《续资治通鉴长编》卷二八二，《国朝诸臣奏议》卷一○八，《容斋三笔》卷一四，《宋史》卷一八四《食货志》下六、卷三四六《吕陶传》，《文献通考》卷一八，《历代名臣奏议》卷二六九，嘉庆《四川通志》卷六九。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_1180879_0'>⑴ 茶园税每三百文折纳绢一疋，三百二十文折纳䌷一疋，十文折纳绵一两，二文折纳禾草一束。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_25_1180879_0'>⑵ 官茶每斤先收三分息钱，官中每斤若用一百文买，即作一百三十文卖；若用五十文买，即作六十五文卖。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_32_1180879_0'>⑶ 臣窃闻蜀州熙宁八年，银每两官折二贯三百文足，市价一贯六百文；九年，银每两官折二贯二百文足，市价一贯四百文。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_32_1180879_0'>⑷ 茶场司指挥成贯并支交子，馀○方支现钱。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_35_1180879_0'>⑸ 臣窃知永康军熙宁九年买获并税过客人茶货，共一百三十二万馀斤，比八年计亏九万馀斤；比七年亏二十六万馀斤。盖是园户畏罪失业，造茶减少，是致税数有亏。以此推之，则失陷税赋诚有其渐。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1180879_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年3月18日</a>　再上奏榷茶利害事。作品：《奏为茶园户暗折三分价钱令客旅纳官充息乞检会前奏早赐改更事状》<div id='poem_1180880' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180880' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180880?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏为茶园户暗折三分价钱令客旅纳官充息乞检会前奏早赐改更事状<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁十年三月十八日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年3月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180880")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180880_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180880'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180880'>右，臣先为本路置买茶，般往熙河，并明收三分利息，旋行出卖，大于远方不便，寻具画一条列，申奏去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180880_comment'></div>愚瞽之言，必已上浼天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180880_comment'></div>臣伏见国家置市易司，笼制百货，岁出息钱，不过二分，须以一年为率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180880_comment'></div>盖为今年支出官本一百万贯，至年终要见息钱二十万贯，即不是早买一百贯物，晚卖一百二十贯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180880_comment'></div>今来茶场司却不以一年为率，务将重刑立法，尽榷民间茶货入官，旋买旋卖，取利三分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180880_comment'></div>或今日买十贯之茶，明日便作十三贯卖于客旅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180880_comment'></div>或朝卖一贯，暮作一贯三百出卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180880_comment'></div>日逐将官本变转，殊不休已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180880_comment'></div>其公牒行下州县，乃云务令买卖通快，无致妨滞钱本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180880_comment'></div>则所出利息，比至岁终，不可胜算，岂止三分而已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180880_comment'></div>比于市易原条，自相违越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180880_comment'></div>窃缘茶是民间日用之物，有如水火，一旦忽被官司尽数收榷，独专其利，仍以严刑过绳其罪，远方细民，生长休息，在朝廷恩德之内，岂识此事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180880_comment'></div>兼据本州堋口镇茶场申，自今月十日至十五日终，逐旋买到茶八百八十六斤，计本钱一百六贯三百二十文，随日出卖，收到息钱三十一贯八百九十六文，别无存贮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180880_comment'></div>臣看详上件申报，窃疑本处首尾六日之中，买获茶货八百八十六斤，随日便卖了当，并无现在存贮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180880_comment'></div>虑恐买卖之际，别有侵损官私，寻行体访，乃是客旅并牙子等，为见榷茶不许衷私买卖，一向邀难园户，或称官中高抬斤两，或言多方退难，遂使于外面预先商量减价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180880_comment'></div>其园户各为畏法惧罪，且欲变货营生，穷迫之间，势不获已，情愿与客旅商议，每斤只收七分实钱，中卖于官，所馀三分，留在客人体上，用充买茶之息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180880_comment'></div>才投场中卖了当，即时却是客人明立姓名，正行请买，所以随日卖尽<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180880_comment'></div>如此则是园户只得七分价钱，暗折三分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180880_comment'></div>官中虽得三分之息，自是园户本钱，客人未曾出息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1180880_comment'></div>窃缘山乡人户自来以采茶为业，输纳两税，折科最重，并出役钱，养生之计，并在其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1180880_comment'></div>一旦既遭禁榷，遂被商旅并牙子等恐动邀难，顿减三分价直，行之日久，必见穷困，诚可嗟悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1180880_comment'></div>其如逐处买茶官司，多是畏惧茶场司威势，务欲买卖通快，出得息钱，庶可免罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1180880_comment'></div>以此互相欺诞，不敢申陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1180880_comment'></div>臣伏谓园户是国家两税土著之民，今来被好利之臣设此弊法，要出息钱，却令商旅生奸，侵损两税人户，最于远方不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1180880_comment'></div>又况随日计利，殊无分限，显是违越市易原条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1180880_comment'></div>伏乞圣慈检会臣前奏，特降指挥下本路安抚、转运、提刑司，体量诣实，早赐改更，庶使王泽不壅，可救大弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1180880_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1180880'>〔贴黄〕若官中实于客人体上收得息钱三分，则尚恐货法不通，民受其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1180880_comment'></div>而况自是园户暗有赔折，其买茶之人，原不出息，岂得稳便？</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1180880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1180880'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_1180880_0'>⑴ 假如茶一百斤，每斤合卖一百三十文，计价钱十三贯。其园户既被邀难恐动，情愿只作十贯卖与官场，即时却是客人纳钱一十三贯请买，文历虽正，情弊则深。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1180880_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年4月24日</a>　三上奏榷茶利害事。作品：《奏为官场买茶亏损园户致有词诉喧闹事状》<div id='poem_1180881' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1180881' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1180881?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏为官场买茶亏损园户致有词诉喧闹事状<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁十年四月二十四日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年4月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1180881")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1180881_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1180881'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180881'>今再具官场买茶取息太重，亏损园户，致有词诉及生喧闹，画一奏列如后：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1180881'>一、据九陇县税户党元吉等状称：「自来相承山坝茶园等业，每年春冬，雇召人工薅刬，至立夏并小满时节，又雇召人工趁时采造茶货，逐日收来堋口投场货卖，得钱收买粮食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1180881_comment'></div>每一称和袋一十八斤，内除出上件破用并输税、免役等钱折除算计外，每称只有利息一百五十至二百文以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1180881_comment'></div>往年早茶每斤货卖得九十至一百文，今来官中置场收买，每贯上出息钱三百文，招诱客人货卖其茶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1180881_comment'></div>牙子并兴贩客人为见官中息钱，却只于茶园人户茶货上估定，价例低小，每斤卖得一百文以来者，现今只卖得六十至七十文，却将馀上价钱令客人用作官中息钱，收买前去，以此园户盘费不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1180881_comment'></div>念元吉等家各只有些小茶园，并不种植得诸般苗色，又为路途遥远，往复相去本场约一百五十里以来，若此价例低小，难以造作茶货，必见破败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1180881_comment'></div>伏乞指挥，贵获存济」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1180881_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1180881'>一、据九陇县税户牟元吉等状称：「自来只以佃食茶园为业，其茶园偏峻，不任种植诸般苗色，逐年举取人上债利粮食，雇召人工，两季薅刬，指望四月小满前后造作讫茶，投场破卖得钱，填还债利，并送纳诸般税赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1180881_comment'></div>若遇丰熟之年，米价平和，每袋上除折上件盘缠、输税外，上头只馀得利息一二百文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1180881_comment'></div>或遇年辰较恶，米粮价贵，天时亢旱，茶生短浅，以此数目减少，虚折薅刬盘缠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1180881_comment'></div>今蒙官中置场收买园户茶货，每贯上出息三百文，其茶每称和袋十八斤，牙子只称作十四五斤，若是薄弱妇女卖时，只称作十三四斤以来，每称约陷著一二斤，别无上头利息，心极忧惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1180881_comment'></div>昨蒙提举推官躬亲在茶场内看觑收买茶货，不与园户分擘逐处茶场、时候、早嫩、粗细、等第色额，只作一样收买，去年时节每斤卖得七八十文，今来只卖得五十文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1180881_comment'></div>除牙子钱了，收得四十七文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1180881_comment'></div>所有馀上钱数，令客人用作官中息钱收买，不管园户裹缠不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1180881_comment'></div>若不具状申讫，切恐将来转见沦亡失所」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1180881_comment'></div>本州所据党元吉并牟元吉等二状，寻行遣帖堋口茶场，钤束茶牙子并专拦等，不得准前大称园户茶货，及剩除园户牙钱，仍仰常切点检茶货粗细、等第色额，一依自来价例收买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1180881_comment'></div>并申茶场司，更乞措置，免致亏损园户去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1180881_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1180881'>一、据堋口茶场申：据至德山人户将到炭焙新茶赴场中卖后，却出纳三分息钱收买，请引出外货卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1180881_comment'></div>又申：自三月二十一日至月终，买到第二等新茶，并是园户马吉等情愿出纳息钱，请引前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1180881_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1180881'>一、据蒲村茶场申：本场逐日据园户将到新旧茶货赴场，随日收买出卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1180881_comment'></div>内有园户自出纳三分息钱，请引前去破卖，亦有客人在外，与园户商量价例了，却于园户处除下息钱，投场收买，请引前去，不虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1180881_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1180881'>一、据九陇县园户石光义等状称：「今月五日将到茶货投场破卖，每袋计一十八斤，和袋不委茶牙子除折，只称得一十四斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1180881_comment'></div>其茶系第二等，每斤合准直价钱九十文，当日减下价例，每斤只收得大钱四十七文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1180881_comment'></div>至到十三日，其茶每斤系第三等，合准直价钱七十文，每斤又再减价例，又只作大钱三十七文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1180881_comment'></div>今来茶牙收光义等茶货，比前山下路人户粗茶一样减下价钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1180881_comment'></div>念光义等住处系在后山，为地土寒冷，以此至小满前后，只造作得似前山第一等、第二等茶货，现在委的不依每年逐时等第价例，一样取意团断，即光义等各为雇召人工，每日雇钱六十文，并口食在外，其茶破人四工，只作得茶一袋，计一十八斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1180881_comment'></div>切虑光义等家，向后必有失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1180881_comment'></div>乞指挥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1180881_comment'></div>本州所据园户石光义等陈诉亏价事理，已帖堋口茶场，仰检详承受前后所降敕条指挥，候茶园户将到茶货赴场中卖，请监官当面看验前山、后山、色额、等第、粗细，依自来市色实直、粗细、逐时市价，添减两平，称来收买，画时当官支给价钱，即不得容令牙子、专拦等依前低作价例，只作一等茶货收买，及非理大称斤两，致有亏损园户，无故拥并阻节，仍仰出榜晓示园户知委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1180881_comment'></div>如受此指挥后，却将好为恶，将贵作贱，只作一等价例收买，致令园户再有词说；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1180881_comment'></div>或因本州察探得知，其牙子、专拦等必当勾遣赴州报勘施行，官员亦当勘劾闻奏，仍取责监官并牙子、专拦等知委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1180881_comment'></div>仍仰本场分析今月十三日因何将石光义等第三等茶每斤只作三十七文收买因依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1180881_comment'></div>并两次申茶场司，更乞措置，免致亏损园户去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1180881_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1180881'>一、据管勾堋口茶场秘书丞尹固并濛阳主簿同共买茶薛翼等二状申：「今月十七日收买茶六万斤，计钱三千六百贯文，支用茶本、净利钱并尽，遂于十八日申州，乞相度支移交子六千贯文，应副十九日并二十一日市收买茶货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1180881_comment'></div>至十九日，天色才晓，据园户将到茶货赴场中卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1180881_comment'></div>当日巳时后，固等为现请交子未归，兼更值雨，遂向园户道：『请交子相次回归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1180881_comment'></div>及等候天晴，与你称茶』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1180881_comment'></div>其园户便自将茶直上来厅堆垛，团围固等，须要称茶，及向牙人道：『尔等当时通出抵产在官，今来官中无钱买茶，你牙人须著与我出钱买茶一市』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1180881_comment'></div>固等各回廨宇及安下处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1180881_comment'></div>主簿薛翼行至净众院门，其园户却致打本官手下公人，兼扯破薛翼袍袖，更寻牙人，意要相争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1180881_comment'></div>其牙人为见如此，各自回避，现不住差人四散寻觅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1180881_comment'></div>固等切恐二十一日市别牙子买卖茶货，又虑园户准前争闹，别致不虞，系属人众，难为止约，乞差九陇县官一员，赴茶场告谕园户，三五日所贵晓会」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1180881_comment'></div>本州所据尹固、薛翼申报，寻体访得今月十九日有园户五千人以来投入茶场，直上监官厅上，指约不得，致打公人，并毁骂官员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1180881_comment'></div>盖为刘佐等起请，须要旋买旋卖，出息三分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1180881_comment'></div>其逐场若尽价收买到，恐客人兴贩无利，将来出卖不行，以此须至低估价例收买，每斤委只及一半价钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1180881_comment'></div>又缘逐日买及数万斤，监官实难照管得尽，其园户既被亏损，无可申诉，遂便聚众喧闹，人数颇众，难为约束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1180881_comment'></div>今来后山正当茶货出众时节，切恐少钱收买，准前争闹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1180881_comment'></div>当州勘会前后六度支与堋口茶场交子、现钱一万一千二百馀贯，银一千两，其银为园户不肯折请，已分与九陇等县出卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1180881_comment'></div>又为市并绝无现钱，因是货卖未得外，馀茶场司兑拨交子一万贯文，至今未到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1180881_comment'></div>若得上件交子，尽数支用，亦只买得三两市<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1180881_comment'></div>本州虽已出榜，严行约束，指挥本处，候园户将到茶货赴场，即便依次称来收买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1180881_comment'></div>如是园户准前要致打公人等，或毁骂官员，仰擒捉送州，待凭取勘，依法施行，兼差九陇主簿勾龙骧前往晓谕，同共买卖茶货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1180881_comment'></div>切虑园户准前喧闹，别致不虞，又差本县令薛高三五日一次，在前照管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1180881_comment'></div>寻申茶场司催促交子，并乞大段支钱赴州，应副使用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1180881_comment'></div>及乞检会本州今月十七日申石光义等告说亏价事理，许令添展价钱去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1180881_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_1180881'>右，谨具如前，所据茶园户党元吉等状并蒲村、堋口两镇申述，并已条列在前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1180881_comment'></div>臣伏见刘佐、李杞、蒲宗闵等妄陈愚见，茍希进用，尽将川茶禁榷，旋买旋卖，立法太重，取利太多，致令茶户被此深害，遂于今年三月八日后来，两次具状论奏，乞赐更此弊法，以幸远方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1180881_comment'></div>狂瞽之言，未蒙采纳，方且日俟朝旨，俯就诛殛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1180881_comment'></div>而臣部内百姓，累有申诉，皆言被官场减下价例，大有侵损，以至嗟怨，聚众喧闹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1180881_comment'></div>臣虽严行约束，及差官同其管勾，须得相度茶色，添长价钱去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1180881_comment'></div>今若隐而不言，虑恐因此生事，上误朝廷，须至再具论列，烦浼圣断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1180881_comment'></div>盖缘刘佐等起请要出息三分，若逐场尽价收买之后，将来商旅计算不成，不愿兴贩，则积坏茶货，例被责罚，及干连人必著赔填。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1180881_comment'></div>以此须至顺承茶场司风旨，减价收买，所贵客人愿来兴贩，变转得行<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1180881_comment'></div>或是园户自纳三分息钱，请引出外<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1180881_comment'></div>情弊如此，上下通知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1180881_comment'></div>茶场司臣僚恐出息不多，难沾赏典，空行文牒，督迫州县，其实则任令减价收买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1180881_comment'></div>逐场监官畏惧茶场司威势，恐遭责罚，干系人众，深虑将来积压陪填，一向刻剥园户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1180881_comment'></div>州县之吏，熟视疾苦，无力以救之，日久为害转深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1180881_comment'></div>恭惟陛下仁民爱物，与天地等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1180881_comment'></div>夙夜孜孜，讲求治要，惟恐一夫未得其所，必不容此刻薄小人茍希劳效，作为敝法，以困西南生聚，有累圣政，众所不平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1180881_comment'></div>臣愚伏望圣慈检会臣今年三月八日并十八日及今来所奏，早赐睿断，特降指挥下本路监司或帅臣，采访利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1180881_comment'></div>如臣所言有一事一件稍涉虚诞，甘俟诛戮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1180881_comment'></div>若万分有一可以采用，即乞更张茶禁，以便远民，或限数收买，或量减息钱，则山乡茶户，不胜至幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1180881_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_1180881'>〔贴黄〕臣体问得六月以后，犹有晚茶一色，贵者每斤三十文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1180881_comment'></div>若尽收买，所出之息，亦不甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1180881_comment'></div>缘逐处自开场至今，买获茶货，旋行出卖，稍有厚利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1180881_comment'></div>如或朝廷谓此成法难便改更，即乞自六月一日以后，权住收买，放令准私交易，所贵园户留得晚茶一二分，尽价卖与客旅，稍助生计，亦遗秉滞穗与民之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1180881_comment'></div>伏乞圣明，特赐采察<span class='inlineComment2'>（《净德集》卷一。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1180881_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_1180881'>九百六十：文渊阁本作「九百四十」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1180881_comment'></div>九百八十：文渊阁本作「九百六十」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_78_1180881_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1180881'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_48_1180881_0'>⑴ 在州现今实直，第二十七界交子卖九百六十，茶场司指挥作一贯文支用；第二十六界交子卖九百六十，茶场司指挥作九百八十文用。此亦亏损园户之一端也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_61_1180881_0'>⑵ 假如茶一百斤，每斤一百文，若便作一十贯买，则恐客人不肯用一十三贯请买，以此减下园户价钱，只作七贯文收买，便于客人作十贯文请买。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_62_1180881_0'>⑶ 园户茶货须得中卖于官，若欲别处变卖，便成犯禁，无引不行，被此抑逼，须至自纳息钱三分，请引出外。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1180881_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年5月</a>　为榷茶事上帅府并二司奏状。作品：《申帅府并二司状》<div id='poem_1181027' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181027' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181027?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申府帅并二司状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181027")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181027_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181027'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181027'>右，陶自今年四月三日后来，累据九陇县茶户等各陈文状，申说彼官场减价买茶，却将馀上价钱，令客人充息请买；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181027_comment'></div>及不分早嫩粗细色额，只作一般取买，委有侵损，乞指挥，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1181027", 1181027, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>贵获</span>存济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181027_comment'></div>陶寻帖堋口茶场，令依市价收买，两平称来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181027_comment'></div>如敢准前以好为恶、将贵作贱，及不分等第、高称斤两，牙子专拦，必定根勘断决，监官云按劾申奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181027_comment'></div>如此行下，非不丁宁，缘议者立法，要出息三分，旋买旋卖，逐场若尽价收买之后，将来客旅计算不成，不愿兴贩，必至积压损坏，监官例遭责罚，干连人尽著赔填。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181027_comment'></div>以此须至顺承茶场司风旨，减价收买，所贵客人愿来兴贩，变转得行<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181027_comment'></div>或自园户纳三分息钱，请引出外<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，情弊如此，上下通知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181027_comment'></div>茶场司臣僚恐出息不多，难沾赏典，空行文牒，督迫州县，其实则任令减价收买；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181027_comment'></div>逐场监官畏惧茶场司威势，恐遭责罚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181027_comment'></div>干系人则深忧将来损坏赔填，一向刻剥园户，低估价直收买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181027_comment'></div>每斤除牙税、头子钱及交子陌外，只及半价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181027_comment'></div>州郡之吏，熟视疾苦，无力以救，行之日久，为害转深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181027_comment'></div>茶户嗟怨，屡有词说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181027_comment'></div>及至今月十九日，为本场支钱并尽，有园户三百家以来，约及三千人，指约不住，各自将茶直上监官厅堆垛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181027_comment'></div>团围秘丞尹固、主簿薛翼，语言不逊，须要称茶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181027_comment'></div>逐官各回廨宇，众人遂便扯破薛翼袍袖，并致打随行手力等，其牙子一十二人并各回避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181027_comment'></div>陶寻出榜，且令园户任便四散，暂将茶货往蒲村、木头、导江等处官场中卖，并行诸县，晓谕保正等不得妄有在路阻节，及差九陇主簿勾龙骧前往晓谕园户，同共买卖，兼差本县令薛高三日或五日一次前去照管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181027_comment'></div>陶当时即不敢张皇申覆，亦不敢繄行根究致打手力之人，盖缘愚民聚众，忿怒争闹，情虽难恕，而亏损茶价，其曲在己，从而卖法，愈更厚颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181027_comment'></div>以此一面出榜，严行约束及根究次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181027_comment'></div>陶再详山户茶货，若外面私卖一两，便成犯法，将至官场，例被减价，费用不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181027_comment'></div>大抵小人之情至于穷塞，则何所不为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181027_comment'></div>深恐此事非西南之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181027_comment'></div>伏望某官更赐体访减价事理、喧闹因依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181027_comment'></div>如陶所言不妄，即乞特为敷奏，乞改茶法，以便远方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181027_comment'></div>陶兼体问得六月以后，犹有晚茶一色，贵者每斤不过三十文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181027_comment'></div>若尽收买，所出之息，亦不甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181027_comment'></div>缘逐处自开场至今，买获茶货，旋行出卖，颇有厚利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181027_comment'></div>如或朝廷谓此成法难便改更，即乞自六月一日以后权住收买，放令衷私交易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181027_comment'></div>所贵园户留得晚茶一二分，尽价卖与客旅，稍助生计，亦遗秉滞穗与民之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181027_comment'></div>谨具状申知府龙图、运使学士、运判太博、提刑郎中。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1181027_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1181027'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_1181027_0'>⑴ 假如茶一百斤，每斤一百文，若便作一十贯买，则恐客人不肯用一十三贯文请买；以此减下园户价钱，只作七贯收买，所贵有客人作十贯请买。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_1181027_0'>⑵ 园户茶货须得中卖与官，若将往别处变卖，便成犯禁，无引不行。被此抑逼，须至自纳息钱三分，请引出外。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1181027_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年5月</a>　朝廷以吕陶等奏，罢榷茶取息三分。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
简阳（金水）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d40481641bd34fb2abc79e64671dd7aa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d40481641bd34fb2abc79e64671dd7aa");'><span id='d40481641bd34fb2abc79e64671dd7aa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1082')">1077-1082年</a>，50-55岁</div><div id='d40481641bd34fb2abc79e64671dd7aa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年7月</a>　以论榷茶事冲替，责监怀安商税。刘庠疏辩其无罪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年9月1日</a>　监怀安商税。九月，为僧文爽寿塔作记。作品：《圣兴寺僧文爽寿塔记》<div id='poem_1181121' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181121' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181121?labeling=true' target='_blank'>圣兴寺僧文爽寿塔记<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰元年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年9月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181121")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181121_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181121'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181121'>僧文爽诣予而言曰：「文爽之先居济南，姓朱氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181121_comment'></div>方少时，去父母，来成都，学浮图道，得圣兴寺，蕴中而礼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181121_comment'></div>会真宗皇帝吴国长公主为报慈正觉大师，以普恩落发，今六十九载矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181121_comment'></div>自为童读佛书，以至隶僧籍、登讲座、主赞忏、长戒坛、居副职、衣紫方袍，无一不足者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181121_comment'></div>行年八十，复何为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181121_comment'></div>惟晦默澄静，日俟终化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181121_comment'></div>有为我穴西郊之地，他日以烬骨藏其间而谓之寿塔者，敢请文以志焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181121_comment'></div>陶伏闻家君言：师字鉴之，相从最旧，知其为人有律行，该通教典，终日演讲，仅五十年，就坛禀戒者无虑千数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181121_comment'></div>尝委橐金新护净寺门阑，求所利益，天章待制李公为记其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181121_comment'></div>年虽耄，意气不少衰，陶向遭先妣丧，数为水陆大供，觊享冥福，师夜诵真谛，亹亹达旦，声韵远畅，愈于壮夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181121_comment'></div>盖诸经所载佛语者尝总而记之，故多且不遗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181121_comment'></div>悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181121_comment'></div>世之妄人牵联驰突于利欲之坠裒恶贮过，以自封殖，伐灭天和，投坠罪境，不知其神魄之丧夺固已久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181121_comment'></div>而犹蚤夜惕惕，恒恐浮躯之忽坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181121_comment'></div>凡如此者，又安能知释氏之于死生甚近而易，乃有往来彼此之论，虽然，以师之轻清悦豫，不夸能，不役智，则未可以岁月期也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181121_comment'></div>曰仲倪、仲昂、惟贤、士昙、士独五人者，实继其后云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181121_comment'></div>元丰钺午岁季秋朔日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1181121_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年10月1日</a>　十月，为眉州醴泉寺善庆堂作记。作品：《眉州醴泉寺善庆堂记》<div id='poem_1181122' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181122' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181122?labeling=true' target='_blank'>眉州醴泉寺善庆堂记<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰元年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年10月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181122")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181122_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181122'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181122'>士君子少而从政，老而谢事，去仕途之劳，就林泉之佚，康宁寿考，泰然自得，其始终往返之际，固已高于人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181122_comment'></div>至于子孙，皆能有立，从而光大之，则尤可高也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181122_comment'></div>吾乡秘书监程公，践历寄任凡四十年，风迹凛凛，德惠在民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181122_comment'></div>及其老也，得请而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181122_comment'></div>高堂广厦，足以奉起居之安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181122_comment'></div>芳亭茂榭，足以遂吟赏之乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181122_comment'></div>安车轻盖，足以便游从之趣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181122_comment'></div>道衣野服，足以资萧散之味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181122_comment'></div>凡尘埃网罗、深可厌恶之事，无一毫辄累其怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181122_comment'></div>宾客到门，则置酒高会，剧谈大笑如少壮时，往往日暮夜阑，不欲其去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181122_comment'></div>有子五人，而官者四，其一人则又以才能见用，而仕亦显矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181122_comment'></div>此退休之美，绍续之隆，皆可高也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181122_comment'></div>非独此而已，抑有可纪者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181122_comment'></div>公尝念仲弟泳之之亡而禄秩未及，乃以一子恩及其犹子，所以公之幼子尚未仕，而泳之之子已为丞于大理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181122_comment'></div>则昆弟义好之笃，于古无愧，宜其见爱于乡党而推尊之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181122_comment'></div>郡城之西曰醴泉寺者，公之先世实葬其侧，岁时上冢，必止息焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181122_comment'></div>榛芜满前，栋宇败陋，公出力而完之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181122_comment'></div>僧绍良德公之深，乃建新堂，以绘公之像及诸子之仕者凡六人，而尊奉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181122_comment'></div>且推本公之祖考以来，积累深厚之所致，而谓之「善庆」，尚虚西壁，以俟俊哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181122_comment'></div>程氏之族，信盛矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181122_comment'></div>昔人盖有父子皆至公卿，兄弟同时为二千石，则前史录以为嘉事，后世藉以为美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181122_comment'></div>考古揆今，良可尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181122_comment'></div>公官三品，年八十，古之乡老也，斯堂之成，必饮酒以落之，子孙列侍于旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181122_comment'></div>乡人爱公而来贺者，或以爵，或以齿，序位于前，起而执觞，罗拜而为寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181122_comment'></div>宾主相与，尊斝相交，乐作于庭，酒行而无次，老者得尽其乐，少者不敢忘其恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181122_comment'></div>一席之间，有悦豫而无惰慢，于此观焉，亦乡饮之遗风欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181122_comment'></div>陶同郡人也，喜公之落成，而不得偕众宾之末，酌以献公，已而，从杖者以出，安能无慊于心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181122_comment'></div>得书其事，不敢辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181122_comment'></div>元丰元年十月朔日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1181122_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年3月</a>　三月，为李彤撰墓志铭。作品：《李太博墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181141' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181141' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181141?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李太博墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰元年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181141")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181141_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181141'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181141'>君讳彤，字周伯，姓李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181141_comment'></div>其先京兆人，八世祖远从唐僖宗幸蜀，调晋原令，因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181141_comment'></div>高祖臻，仕孟氏朝，为永平军节度推官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181141_comment'></div>曾祖某，亦任太子司议郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181141_comment'></div>祖某，不愿仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181141_comment'></div>父某，以君登朝，赠大理寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181141_comment'></div>母黎氏，赠成都县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181141_comment'></div>君少笃学，颇颖秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181141_comment'></div>时乡先生职方员外郎张公中行守岳阳，君往就正，得《易》与《春秋》大旨，朋友畏其博闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181141_comment'></div>又尝摭前世忠邪事，以类相从，为《史断》十二篇，以监治乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181141_comment'></div>庆历六年中进士第，调眉州青神尉，言者谓蜀人官近乡非所宜，于是近皆徙远，移万州司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181141_comment'></div>岁满，用陟状迁江陵府松滋令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181141_comment'></div>丁寺丞君忧，终丧，授陇州判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181141_comment'></div>吏部上其课，转著作佐郎、知太原府平晋县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181141_comment'></div>今天子践阼，改秘书丞，寻迁太常博士、知华州郑县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181141_comment'></div>以疾分司西京，卒于盩厔之寓，止享年五十四，实熙宁五年春二月某日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181141_comment'></div>既没七年，贫不克葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181141_comment'></div>至元丰元年三月某日，乃葬于某乡某里先陇之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181141_comment'></div>君彊明，喜节廉，自处素高，待交游如少所与，然不废于义，休戚可以同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181141_comment'></div>于政事知大略，而未尝以忿恚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181141_comment'></div>任刑听断，适其理，大率刚而不挠，耻为流俗态度也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181141_comment'></div>在万州有箠人之脉者，提点刑狱视之，疑且怒，欲以骨折论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181141_comment'></div>太守畏不敢辩，君提伤者以告曰：「折则上下不相属，今举其上而下不少曲，非折明矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181141_comment'></div>使者无以胜，卒轻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181141_comment'></div>又有三人谋杀一人者，君方摄督邮，当议法，即白守曰：「一人死，安可戮三人，坐谋首可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181141_comment'></div>守不听，有诟责言，君持之益坚，请于提点刑狱，且曰：「某宁解印绶去，安忍妄杀人，求顺太守意邪」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181141_comment'></div>得闻之朝，止报一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181141_comment'></div>万州帑失缗钱数千万，俾君验之，君以为贯朽铁坏，不知几十载，一旦指为盗，疑或刻深，请饬吏共偿，无烦构狱，守从之，免数辈刑窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181141_comment'></div>松滋产茗，岁输府千斤，春未社，牧遣校至，督所有，君曰：「今未知茗之芽否，可偕往视」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181141_comment'></div>即斸根株，俾校持以归，愿牧植之后园，俟其芽可责输矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181141_comment'></div>牧始不怿，既而从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181141_comment'></div>植者既芽，则谓同僚曰：「李松滋以芽为期，今可取乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181141_comment'></div>校复至，具言，君乃戒茗户以五日集，如其令，无一毫私挠，民深德之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1181141_comment'></div>有宿寇数十，结山民聚境上，往往害捕吏，累岁莫获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1181141_comment'></div>君开以威信，许其归首，乃至无盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1181141_comment'></div>功当赏，君不言，赏亦不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1181141_comment'></div>陇之汧源号难治，凡阅岁定籍，则吏民相因为奸，历十数年，官不敢辄易其旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1181141_comment'></div>君权涖未几，遂定籍，高下适当，人伏其平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1181141_comment'></div>平晋民冒居公地，而县隶为输租，缘此以敛剥，习久，纵不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1181141_comment'></div>君使冒者自陈，尽得其实，免代输之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1181141_comment'></div>又尝为增堤，以捍汾流，以军事未报，君已解去，既而大水，一城荡然，识者称其先见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1181141_comment'></div>郑县之西，旧以石堤水过守居洎他官池圃，以及富彊沼榭，君始来，方谕民得取以溉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1181141_comment'></div>水既不至，为总管者谩其词，移檄于县，觊水以御火，符下凡四五，君悉不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1181141_comment'></div>时都官员外郎郭君源明以方静为州，君具白所以然，信之，民甚赖其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1181141_comment'></div>洎引疾而去，有恤君之贫者，告曰：「愿一日留，则终月禄入可享」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1181141_comment'></div>乃笑而谢之，即日不视事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1181141_comment'></div>君先娶包氏，在万州时遇君之疾，以忧卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1181141_comment'></div>再娶郭氏，封寿安县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1181141_comment'></div>包氏生子觐，孝友力学，自二曲护丧归葬灵泉，不违治命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1181141_comment'></div>长女适泸州司户文朝光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1181141_comment'></div>郭氏生子规，治经力学，从举，尝荐于乡，必能世其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1181141_comment'></div>次女适乡贡进士李葆光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1181141_comment'></div>二孙曰皓、曰晏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1181141_comment'></div>呜呼，君平生施为如此，刚矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1181141_comment'></div>苟遭时得志，尽发胸中蕴，则轩腾驰骤，立事致功，卓然有奇节，可必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1181141_comment'></div>惜乎仁不显，而见于用者止此耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1181141_comment'></div>予少从君游，洎官晋阳，又与之同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1181141_comment'></div>窃思仲尼「未见刚者」之说，信刚者之难见，爱君气节旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1181141_comment'></div>觐来请铭，敢为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1181141'>刚近于仁，亦鲜克举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1181141_comment'></div>刚生于气，充则孰御？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1181141_comment'></div>申枨徇欲，义所不取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1181141_comment'></div>孟子养浩，以是为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1181141_comment'></div>家山之东，乔松之坞，呜呼刚者，李君之墓。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1181141_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　作诗送友人什邡县令杜某。作品：《送杜翁东行》<div id='poem_502612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_502612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/502612?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送杜翁东行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_502612")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_502612_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_502612'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_502612'>我为怀安官，君作什邡令。<div id='poem_sentence_0_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_502612'>封疆苦不远，音驿稍频并。<div id='poem_sentence_1_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_502612'>乘閒强吟诗，寄去同赋咏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_502612'>其言类谐谑，间或有讥病。<div id='poem_sentence_3_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_502612'>蒙君屡酬答，往问复来聘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_502612'>长谣颇壮赡，短语亦清劲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_502612'>大率如为人，圭璋有馀莹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_502612'>得之每急读，醉魄时暂醒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_502612'>方从文字乐，忽尔报成政。<div id='poem_sentence_8_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_502612'>秋风飘行色，万里去意迥。<div id='poem_sentence_9_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_502612'>知君最留滞，文价早驰骋。<div id='poem_sentence_10_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_502612'>策名二十载，位未立朝廷。<div id='poem_sentence_11_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_502612'>一官奚足论，百态委前定。<div id='poem_sentence_12_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_502612'>自古有通塞，谁与造物争。<div id='poem_sentence_13_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_502612'>任此不系舟，所至遂游泳。<div id='poem_sentence_14_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_502612'>西山白云起，回首念温凊。<div id='poem_sentence_15_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_502612'>恭闻陛前语，归拜堂上庆。<div id='poem_sentence_16_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_502612'>仆驭倦游否，尘中多捷径。<div id='poem_sentence_17_502612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_502612'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_502612_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年1月</a>　监怀安商税。撰宋慎交墓志铭。作品：《著作佐郎致仕宋府君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181145' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181145' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181145?labeling=true' target='_blank'>著作佐郎致仕宋府君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰二年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181145")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181145_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181145'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181145'>宋氏之先居京兆，唐僖宗时为屯田郎中，随乘舆入蜀，任彭、眉二州刺史，讳挺者，乃君七世祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181145_comment'></div>卒官，葬武阳，因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181145_comment'></div>其后有五宗，次曰殷，始迁邛之蒲阳，遂为邛大姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181145_comment'></div>殷生贤，贤生珂，珂生皓，皓生平，即君皇考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181145_comment'></div>君讳慎交，字葆初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181145_comment'></div>七岁失所恃，执丧如成人，族属异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181145_comment'></div>既长，刚方厚重，若少缘饰，然有识度，不以贱贫荣富动怀，无一语及非义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181145_comment'></div>谈说慷慨，历历可听，多与名教合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181145_comment'></div>其治家有范，约而中礼，耻徇浮侈之俗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181145_comment'></div>其教子有术，严不伤爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181145_comment'></div>从学者谕以修身砺行，效官者勉以急吏缓民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181145_comment'></div>其待物甚恕，盖虽有怨不复，里人伏其量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181145_comment'></div>熙宁元年，上亲祀昊天，以子炤登朝，封大理评事，累迁光禄寺丞、著作佐郎，享年七十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181145_comment'></div>十年九月某日卒于成都之别第，卜以元丰二年正月戊子葬于依政县某乡某里四公山先垄之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181145_comment'></div>君娶李氏，封仁寿县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181145_comment'></div>生四子：炜，早亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181145_comment'></div>焕，举进士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181145_comment'></div>炤，为屯田员郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181145_comment'></div>爟，尝贡于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181145_comment'></div>孙男十二人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181145_comment'></div>自君之丧，屯田君哀毁骨立，早夜惟窀穸是谋，日月先其吉，宅兆贵其安，衣衾棺椁，悉以度数，吊者不冗，挽者不哗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181145_comment'></div>既祖于庭，虽亲朋犹有未知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181145_comment'></div>君子谓宋氏之葬，得其所以葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181145_comment'></div>初，刺史君葬武阳，后葬四公，至殷迁蒲阳，则葬升平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181145_comment'></div>君常爱四公有佳山水，已而葬焉，亦遵平昔之志，且不远其祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181145_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1181145'>质直好义，犯而不校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181145_comment'></div>二者圣贤，著以为教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181145_comment'></div>君有是德，匪习而乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181145_comment'></div>听言则厉，人可法效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181145_comment'></div>爱子则严，纳于忠孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181145_comment'></div>族别而五，疏矣情好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181145_comment'></div>墓析而三，异矣祠报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181145_comment'></div>四公之冈，祖始之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1181145_comment'></div>君归于斯，夙昔所诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1181145_comment'></div>期百千年，铭此以告。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1181145_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年3月</a>　刘庠知秦州，充秦凤经略安抚使，作诗送之。作品：《送刘希道龙图赴秦亭》<div id='poem_502594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_502594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/502594?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送刘希道龙图赴秦亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_502594")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_502594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_502594'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_502594'>君子异众人，所系惟大节。<div id='poem_sentence_0_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_502594'>著见在功业，何尝一毫缺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_502594'>幽能动金石，明可贯日月。<div id='poem_sentence_2_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_502594'>其间有用舍，舒卷不同辙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_502594'>言之尺与寻，轻重自区别。<div id='poem_sentence_4_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_502594'>公以道德进，义操非孑孑。<div id='poem_sentence_5_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_502594'>早岁在言路，屡补衮衣阙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_502594'>一语定大计，永祚庆绵瓞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_502594'>西来委重镇，远业粗施施。<div id='poem_sentence_8_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_502594'>岷峨固不动，江汉亦澄澈。<div id='poem_sentence_9_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_502594'>譬如公输木，巨细归檃括。<div id='poem_sentence_10_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_502594'>又如后夔音，合止付椌楬。<div id='poem_sentence_11_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_502594'>尔其遂生成，吾岂任呴沬。<div id='poem_sentence_12_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_502594'>愚者多竞利，破产营酒蘖。<div id='poem_sentence_13_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_502594'>官缗逋数万，私计鲜毫发。<div id='poem_sentence_14_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_502594'>虽云鬻儿女，未免就缧绁。<div id='poem_sentence_15_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_502594'>巨械压羸颈，重箠困流血。<div id='poem_sentence_16_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_502594'>亦有冻馁毙，枯骸不藏穴。<div id='poem_sentence_17_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_502594'>兹事关进退，闻之宜结舌。<div id='poem_sentence_18_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_502594'>壮哉仁者勇，拜疏为论列。<div id='poem_sentence_19_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_502594'>诏书即日下，蠲除允公说。<div id='poem_sentence_20_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_502594'>皇慈极霶沾，治体非眇末。<div id='poem_sentence_21_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_502594'>推此不忍心，疲瘵庶全活。<div id='poem_sentence_22_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_502594'>方将秦川命，又仗元师钺。<div id='poem_sentence_23_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_502594'>何时归廊庙，民望甚饥渴。<div id='poem_sentence_24_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_502594'>天网举无外，海势包有截。<div id='poem_sentence_25_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_502594'>威德广所被，神武专不杀。<div id='poem_sentence_26_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_502594'>两阶虞舜舞，六月宣王伐。<div id='poem_sentence_27_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_502594'>梯航走琛赆，早夜畏鞭挞。<div id='poem_sentence_28_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_502594'>相因太仓粟，红腐以时发。<div id='poem_sentence_29_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_502594'>已朽外府贯，浩荡流不竭。<div id='poem_sentence_30_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_502594'>乘此全盛力，万事易裁割。<div id='poem_sentence_31_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_502594'>泰山可转徙，巨浸可壅遏。<div id='poem_sentence_32_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_502594'>深惟汉唐治，丞辅次皋卨。<div id='poem_sentence_33_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_502594'>弱翁知故事，论议颇谆切。<div id='poem_sentence_34_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_502594'>开府善守文，规模亦宏阔。<div id='poem_sentence_35_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_502594'>敢告天子圣，邦基系明哲。<div id='poem_sentence_36_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_502594'>斯言得之公，非以为容悦。<div id='poem_sentence_37_502594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_502594'></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_502594_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　作赵荐墓志铭。作品：《都官员外郎赵君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181135' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181135' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181135?labeling=true' target='_blank'>都官员外郎赵君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181135")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181135_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181135'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181135'>熙宁十年三月，都官员外郎赵君既守荣州，乃建悦老堂，日奉二亲，尽所以乐亲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181135_comment'></div>君为州已大治，亲方寿考，而能极恭致养，适其欢心，虽天下之至乐，无若此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181135_comment'></div>于是搢绅士大夫多为歌诗褒誉，德美乡闾，族属指以为荣，且爱慕之不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181135_comment'></div>越明年闰正月某日，丧其父太子中允祐，二月某日，又丧其母万年县君张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181135_comment'></div>君哀毁屡绝，仅能扶丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181135_comment'></div>归，昼夜哭如礼，又时强饮食，凡四十九日而病，又五十一日而卒，实元丰改元四月辛亥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181135_comment'></div>哀哉，君子孝爱其亲，终继以死，可谓不幸矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181135_comment'></div>君讳荐，字宾兴，邛州依政县人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181135_comment'></div>曾祖翱，祖文，皆隐民籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181135_comment'></div>至中允君，以君立朝，有封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181135_comment'></div>始君少向学，善词章，既冠，举进士，一试登乙科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181135_comment'></div>调绵州司法，以陟状迁凤翔府虢县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181135_comment'></div>县介岐、雍间，民以豪悍相胜，抵禁自若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181135_comment'></div>君设为规范，谕以可不可，民信之，刑省五六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181135_comment'></div>巨盗伏境中，捕吏畏罪，执非辜以告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181135_comment'></div>旧令傅致之，狱具如实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181135_comment'></div>君审辨诈伪，纵去不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181135_comment'></div>乃任谋下令搜擿党与，未踰月，果获真盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181135_comment'></div>有司以功上，迁安化军节度推官、知河中府河西县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181135_comment'></div>君曰：「为县不能使无盗，诚可愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181135_comment'></div>捕之，职也，安可藉以茍赏」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181135_comment'></div>辞不拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181135_comment'></div>识者高其廉，当涂交荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181135_comment'></div>后三年，改著作佐郎、知汾州西河县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181135_comment'></div>县剧于虢，处治益办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181135_comment'></div>今天子践阼，授秘书丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181135_comment'></div>未几，转太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181135_comment'></div>岁满，监成都府军资库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181135_comment'></div>是时天章阁待制赵公帅延安，乃以宾佐请君，即签书彰武军节度判官，改屯田员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181135_comment'></div>洎公被命南伐交趾，又辟君以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181135_comment'></div>君怀亲思归，不敢往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181135_comment'></div>公入见上，言君父母留远方，皆老矣，不当久在边，当使之归养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181135_comment'></div>且言君才可用，愿用焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1181135_comment'></div>上乃许君不俟秩满而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1181135_comment'></div>踰年，除知荣州，转都官员外郎，方将大用之，命未下而君卒，春秋四十有八，故交亲知者，莫不悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1181135_comment'></div>君襟度夷畅，无少凝塞，接人无贤不肖，皆得其驩，至于判析是否，则中甚皎然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1181135_comment'></div>尤好为诗，触物感意，有得辄书，凡一十八卷，四千三百首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1181135_comment'></div>或多至数百言，虽赡不冗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1181135_comment'></div>或止于二韵，虽浅不俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1181135_comment'></div>远探近拾，率有理致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1181135_comment'></div>君先娶黄氏，封蓬莱县君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1181135_comment'></div>再娶杨氏，封仁和县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1181135_comment'></div>男六人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1181135_comment'></div>曰彀，曰韬，曰彊，曰彍，曰某，曰某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1181135_comment'></div>一女，未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1181135_comment'></div>始，君从宦游，未尝治产，世赀家帑，委其兄庄，廪俸之入，往往归诸书画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1181135_comment'></div>既不幸，诸孤甚贫，乃丐田于庄，为谋葬养生之具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1181135_comment'></div>遂以二年十月某甲子葬君于蒲阴乡山泉里皈岩山之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1181135_comment'></div>陶与君进士同时，既铭其墓，乃请于太常吴公为之书，又请于紫微李公为之题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1181135_comment'></div>盖二公西南望人，皆恻然见从，则君之为人，又可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1181135_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_1181135'>人皆伤君之亡，又忧孤弱之重不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1181135_comment'></div>及予见君之长子，而问其家之有无，则曰乞田于伯父，可以葬以养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1181135_comment'></div>问其诸弟之长稚，则曰与之谋婚姻，而训以学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1181135_comment'></div>予于是有感焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1181135_comment'></div>嗟夫，寄死托孤之风坏，而愚夫肆行不义，此君子之深悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1181135_comment'></div>以君有行有文与政，而独不克寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1181135_comment'></div>要之报施，则子孙当有以立者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1181135_comment'></div>理势宜尔，君其无憾欤！</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1181135_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　与杨宗惠相识。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　作诗答任师中。作品：《答任师中》<div id='poem_502623' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_502623' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/502623?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答任师中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_502623")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_502623_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_502623'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_502623'>石城山下居，草草已经岁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_502623'>终日对山吟，何尝问阴霁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_502623'>自知有义命，百事安拙计。<div id='poem_sentence_2_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_502623'>每蒙亲朋念，尺书来者继。<div id='poem_sentence_3_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_502623'>岂徒问寒温，亦惑慰穷滞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_502623'>惟公见爱心，不逐时情替。<div id='poem_sentence_5_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_502623'>亲迂老匠笔，特枉长吟惠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_502623'>良金岂雕刻，文锦自灿丽。<div id='poem_sentence_7_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_502623'>太羹充馁肠，灵药去昏翳。<div id='poem_sentence_8_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_502623'>所得适所怀，拜赐敢不励。<div id='poem_sentence_9_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_502623'>诗骚久寂寞，俗士鲜缉缀。<div id='poem_sentence_10_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_502623'>公常得之深，豪赡有规制。<div id='poem_sentence_11_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_502623'>顷闻湖州祸，文字倦且废。<div id='poem_sentence_12_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_502623'>朝廷极仁恕，风俗当训厉。<div id='poem_sentence_13_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_502623'>终令服宽典，不忍投四裔。<div id='poem_sentence_14_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_502623'>吾侪今唱酬，正可颂治世。<div id='poem_sentence_15_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_502623'>况当导情性，无自取罪戾。<div id='poem_sentence_16_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_502623'>敢于韶濩前，率尔献郑卫<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_502623'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_502623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_502623'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_17_502623_0'>⑴ 自注：时苏子瞻以诗得罪，贬黄州。盖词云：黜置方州，以励风俗，往服宽典，勿忘自新。故及之。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_502623_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1082')">1080-1082年</a>　不详。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
广安（渠江）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='21083b92e91d4e9aa95516164297b169_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("21083b92e91d4e9aa95516164297b169");'><span id='21083b92e91d4e9aa95516164297b169_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1085')">1083-1085年</a>，56-58岁</div><div id='21083b92e91d4e9aa95516164297b169' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　起知广安军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年11月</a>　十一月撰程浚墓志铭。作品：《太中大夫武昌程公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181126' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181126' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181126?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太中大夫武昌程公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰六年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181126")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181126_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181126'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181126'>通义郡西，醴泉山之阳，有巨冢焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181126_comment'></div>山隆而磐，水悠而澄，松槚丛郁以深，门阙崇广以严，乃有宋太中大夫武昌程公葬于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181126_comment'></div>维程氏为眉大姓，世有令德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181126_comment'></div>曾祖讳沼，祖讳仁霸，值时季乱，爵禄不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181126_comment'></div>考讳文应，以公故累封大理寺丞，赠官光禄大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181126_comment'></div>妣宋氏，封长安县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181126_comment'></div>公讳浚，字治之，天禀方厚，少有大志，力学举进士，时辈推其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181126_comment'></div>天圣五年，赐同学究出身，选河中府猗氏县尉、戎州司户参军、凤翔府节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181126_comment'></div>用荐者言，授大理寺丞。<div class='inline'
