class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1100')">1096-1100年</a>，69-73岁</div><div id='76d932300091405c8c5cf3a19b4d3ee5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年7月28日</a>　落职差监潭州南岳庙。有谢表。作品：《谢责降南岳表》<div id='poem_1181007' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181007' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181007?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢责降南岳庙表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年7月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181007")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181007_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181007'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181007'>坏法容私，义当显戮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181007_comment'></div>谪官领局，恩许自新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181007_comment'></div>伏省过尤，良增战灼<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181007_comment'></div>伏念臣禀生寒陋，涉世艰危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181007_comment'></div>早窃虚名，晚尘膴仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181007_comment'></div>持从臣之橐，无补猷为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181007_comment'></div>佩郡守之符，多隳职业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181007_comment'></div>纵细民之盗铸，致私镪之公行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181007_comment'></div>罪状甚明，刑书未议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181007_comment'></div>洎忝乡邦之寄任，数为风眩之侵陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181007_comment'></div>拜疏自陈，方觊退休之幸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181007_comment'></div>原情必罚，俄闻责黜之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181007_comment'></div>仰畏雷霆，俯惊冰谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181007_comment'></div>欲继上归田之请，虑难逃慢令之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181007_comment'></div>即扶病以之官，已具舟而去里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181007_comment'></div>穷途易塞，衰气复伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181007_comment'></div>适当起缆之初，几有盖棺之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181007_comment'></div>遽飘流于三峡，遂放荡于重湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181007_comment'></div>以七十之羸躯，尽八千之去路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181007_comment'></div>备尝险阨，屡及倾虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181007_comment'></div>偶全犬马之馀生，深荷堪舆之厚赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181007_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下乾行适治，丰照通幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181007_comment'></div>督群吏之循公，光昭先宪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181007_comment'></div>宽一夫之垂尽，滋广至仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181007_comment'></div>未即诛锄，止从废逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181007_comment'></div>正其罪以警偷惰，锡之禄以养衰残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181007_comment'></div>臣敢不追讼愆违，恪遵检押。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181007_comment'></div>虽有负薪之疾，岂敢乞骸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181007_comment'></div>空怀结草之心，终期报德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181007_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1181007_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　在衡阳见陈绶，为其父文集作序。作品：《陈传正退居类稿序》<div id='poem_1181073' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181073' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181073?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈传正退居类稿序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181073")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181073_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181073'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181073'>予尝志中表陈公传正之墓而铭焉，其行其学其政事既可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181073_comment'></div>后十二年，谪居衡阳，遇公之子绶，始得公《汉南退居类藁》二十卷读之，信乎志铭之不妄与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181073_comment'></div>夫君子之学，始于治性修身，而终于事业，岂特规规于辞采章句而谓之文乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181073_comment'></div>积于中，乃发于外；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181073_comment'></div>蕴其实，乃形于言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181073_comment'></div>表里之相符，本末之相济，而后能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181073_comment'></div>譬夫辉山之玉，不责功于琢刻，抚之则温润，击之则清越；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181073_comment'></div>跃冶之金，不资巧于鍜鍊，举之则坚重，扣之则铿鍧，皆本其所有而见焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181073_comment'></div>公忠于君，孝于亲，信于朋友，仁于物，故其文之典厚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1181073", 1181073, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>详正</span>，出于天质之自然，乃仲尼所谓「有德者必有言」也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181073_comment'></div>庆历二年，仁宗皇帝试进士，置在乙等，上览卷嘉美，谓曰辞理优赡，遂擢甲科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181073_comment'></div>抑亦士林之宗仰，清议之敬服，其可欺乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181073_comment'></div>公初名东琪，后改曰习，字传正云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1181073_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年10月</a>　为董丕之母祝氏撰墓志。作品：《长安县君祝氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1181155' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181155' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181155?labeling=true' target='_blank'>长安县君祝氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣三年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181155")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181155_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181155'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181155'>秘书监济阴祝君正辞，在嘉祐、治平间守密、深、卫、襄四州，皆有治效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181155_comment'></div>朝廷嘉其才，尝降诏赐金以褒显之，盖当时良二千石也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181155_comment'></div>其女嫁同郡人奉议郎致仕董君綎，生四子：曰丕，朝请郎、知阆州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181155_comment'></div>曰萃，未仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181155_comment'></div>曰平，兖州瑕丘令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181155_comment'></div>曰中，渭州平凉尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181155_comment'></div>孙十一人：曰耕，隰州隰川尉，早卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181155_comment'></div>馀皆从学举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181155_comment'></div>夫人以丕登朝，封长安县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181155_comment'></div>元祐三年十一月十七日终于家，春秋六十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181155_comment'></div>绍圣三年十月庚午，葬济阴县安平乡南十里，存荣没哀，其中礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181155_comment'></div>董氏与祝皆为良族，以纯约治家，以雍睦闻乡党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181155_comment'></div>自夫人之归，奉其姑以孝，从其夫以礼，友其夫之妹以和，教其子以立己之大方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181155_comment'></div>紃纫组缀之事，虽劳必亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181155_comment'></div>蘋蘩簠簋之荐，虽老必勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181155_comment'></div>女功妇道，兼修两得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181155_comment'></div>由是闺阃之内，益治而明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181155_comment'></div>至于不诵佛书，不讲淫祀，惟儒者礼法是从，皆妇人之所难能者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181155_comment'></div>诸子既仕，则告之曰：「凡不欺于心，不害于物，谓之君子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181155_comment'></div>反是，谓之小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181155_comment'></div>穷达异分，贵贱殊辙，惟不悖于义，则无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181155_comment'></div>为君子，不为小人，虽五斗之奉，吾不憾也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181155_comment'></div>为小人，不为君子，虽万钟之养，吾不悦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181155_comment'></div>尔等勉之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181155_comment'></div>慈训所及，率有令懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181155_comment'></div>予尝与朝请君为同僚，爱其趣操方静，多文而敏于政，则夫人之贤，从可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181155_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1181155'>祝氏之庆，克昌子孙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181155_comment'></div>夫人钟之，德慈行温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181155_comment'></div>董氏之法，有严闺门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181155_comment'></div>夫人守之，礼隆教存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181155_comment'></div>致养以禄，惟义乃尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181155_comment'></div>享封以邑，惟善乃闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181155_comment'></div>刻铭幽石，贻范后昆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1181155_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　在衡阳，常与范纯仁等为温益侵困。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年闰2月</a>　贬库部员外郎、分司。有谢表。作品：《谢责分司表》<div id='poem_1181006' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181006' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181006?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢责分司表<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣四年闰二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年闰2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181006")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181006_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181006'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181006'>人臣之过，莫大于不忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181006_comment'></div>王者之刑，必诛而无赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181006_comment'></div>仰赖好生之德，俾从分务之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181006_comment'></div>敬服宽恩，交流感涕<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181006_comment'></div>伏念臣禀生寒陋，涉世艰危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181006_comment'></div>不知事主之大方，徒惑近名之小智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181006_comment'></div>出辞妄乱，遇事狂迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181006_comment'></div>名教之所莫容，宪法之所不宥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181006_comment'></div>复何面目，尚缀班联？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181006_comment'></div>既假职于别都，仍即安于善地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181006_comment'></div>馀生甚幸，化力有归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181006_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下加意盈成，励精听断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181006_comment'></div>继志述事，以光大前烈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181006_comment'></div>显忠遂良，以固安永图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181006_comment'></div>察万物之殊源，无容纷纠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181006_comment'></div>悯一夫之垂尽，未即诛锄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181006_comment'></div>正其罪以示劝惩，锡之禄以养衰病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181006_comment'></div>臣敢不追讼前眚，切防后愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181006_comment'></div>革行险之非心，持保身之深戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181006_comment'></div>生而无补，仅逃萧斧之常刑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181006_comment'></div>死或有知，犹冀敝帷之终惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181006_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1181006_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年12月</a>　撰黎淳墓志铭。作品：《朝议大夫黎公墓志》<div id='poem_1181129' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181129' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181129?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝议大夫黎君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣四年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181129")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181129_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181129'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181129'>《春秋》事出于史，而法与义生于笔削，虽游夏不敢措辞其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181129_comment'></div>及夫微言寂绝，大旨畔散，传注解诂之家坌并而起，各持其说，以誇异骋高于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181129_comment'></div>盖自左丘明而下，五传殊归，历汉、晋及唐之盛，而秘府所藏至六十馀家、千馀卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181129_comment'></div>嗟乎，《春秋》之难知，而学者之难论亦已甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181129_comment'></div>渠江黎希声，专经而信道，常谓《春秋》缘旧史之文，假圣师之笔，行王者之事，其文坦易，其法简严，思之不必太深，求之不必太过，则有得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181129_comment'></div>乃探索蕴奥，敷畅厥旨，著《春秋经解》十卷，大率以经为主，不汩于异家曲说之纷纭，传诸士林，信之深，从之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181129_comment'></div>熙宁初，丞相韩魏公上其书于朝，谓可置文馆，翰林王禹玉辈援之甚力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181129_comment'></div>会贡举更制，《春秋》不为科，议乃寝，公亦浩然有归意，遂老于蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181129_comment'></div>今天子向儒重道，谓一经不可辄废，为置博士，用以取人，则公之亡久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181129_comment'></div>呜呼，道之难明也有至是乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181129_comment'></div>徇一时之好恶，而经术用舍系焉，亦儒者之不幸矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181129_comment'></div>此所以古之人著书立说，或藏之山岩屋壁，或投之煨炉，而不欲传于后世，盖有谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181129_comment'></div>按黎氏之先出北正，其后子孙散处四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181129_comment'></div>建隆中，有曰嵩者，初自云安徙居潼洄，今为广安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181129_comment'></div>嵩生元祐，元祐生德颖，乃公考也，累赠金紫光禄大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181129_comment'></div>妣王氏，赠太原郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181129_comment'></div>公讳錞，字希声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181129_comment'></div>幼务学，既冠，与仲兄洵游京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181129_comment'></div>当时儒宗石守道、孙明复皆美其才，韩忠献公召置门下，誉望益显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181129_comment'></div>第庆历六年进士，调利州节度推官，以父忧罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181129_comment'></div>终制，除成德军观察推官，监延州折博务，转大理寺丞，改殿中丞，知阆州南部县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181129_comment'></div>以母丧去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181129_comment'></div>服除，监在京铸䥱务，迁太常博士、屯田员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181129_comment'></div>欧阳文忠公、吴长文荐为学官，得国子监直讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181129_comment'></div>是时太学生凡千数，诸博士讲解，先日撰口义，升座徐读而退，无复辨析旨要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181129_comment'></div>公独不然，置经于前，按文释义，听者乐闻其说，咸宗向之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181129_comment'></div>公凡守雅、蜀、眉、简四郡，皆先德后刑，务存治体，不汲汲簿书期会，君子喜其劝，小人畏其惩，有古循吏之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181129_comment'></div>在唐安，乘岁饥，募民完堤堰，两得其利，不殍而稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1181129_comment'></div>此治状尤炳然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1181129_comment'></div>元丰七年，以朝请大夫致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1181129_comment'></div>哲宗即位，加朝议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1181129_comment'></div>元祐八年五月二十九日卒，享年七十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1181129_comment'></div>绍圣四年十二月十日，葬于渠江县敦义乡书台里书台山下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1181129_comment'></div>公娶安氏，再娶周氏，封仙居、寿安，皆县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1181129_comment'></div>一男傃，太庙斋郎，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1181129_comment'></div>女四人：长适朝议大夫蒲宗闵，次适朝奉大夫杨𧫎，次早夭，次又适宗闵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1181129_comment'></div>孙男二人：暹、昪，皆郊社斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1181129_comment'></div>公善学，知原本，穷经立言，虽皓首不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1181129_comment'></div>六卿荐于朝，将用，已而弃不录，然能以教于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1181129_comment'></div>其临政必重民，所至有可纪，舒而廓之，岂特沾渗四郡乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1181129_comment'></div>世所谓乡先生、良二千石，公无愧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1181129_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1181129'>言可以垂世，屈伸存乎时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1181129_comment'></div>或布于廊庙雍泮，震发斯文之光辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1181129_comment'></div>或委之重岩馀烬，来者莫得而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1181129_comment'></div>志可以泽物，广狭系乎用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1181129_comment'></div>或弥塞海宇，鼓舞万灵之动；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1181129_comment'></div>或踧踖遐陋，敝󶼌米盐之冗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1181129_comment'></div>名在彼孰先，义在我孰重？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1181129_comment'></div>欲识公怀，铭于高冢<span class='inlineComment2'>（《净德集》卷二二。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1181129_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1181129'>潼洄：文渊阁本作「潼川」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1181129_comment'></div>按徽宗重和元年始升梓州为潼川府，此时尚未有「潼川」之名，且梓州<span class='inlineComment2'>（治今四川三台）</span>亦与广安<span class='inlineComment2'>（今四川广安）</span>无涉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1181129_comment'></div>考《元丰九域志》卷七广安军下原注云：「开宝二年以合州浓洄、渠州新明二镇置军，治渠江县」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1181129_comment'></div>《宋史》卷八九《地理志》五宁西军<span class='inlineComment2'>（即广安军）</span>说同，唯「浓洄」作「侬洄」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1181129_comment'></div>疑此处「潼洄」乃「浓洄」之误。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1181129_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1099')">1098-1099年</a>　库部员外郎、分司。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年3月26日</a>　提举成都玉局观、鼎州团练副使、均州安置。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年4月</a>　落分司、差提举成都玉局观。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
邛崃（临邛）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='abbca37df64e43aba9e7aa422a457658_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("abbca37df64e43aba9e7aa422a457658");'><span id='abbca37df64e43aba9e7aa422a457658_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>，73岁</div><div id='abbca37df64e43aba9e7aa422a457658' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年5月20日</a>　差知邛州。有谢表。作品：《谢知邛州表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（表云“臣五月二十日，准进奏院递到敕一道至衡州”云云，知此前一直在衡州。）</span><div id='poem_1181008' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181008' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181008?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知邛州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年5月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181008")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181008_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181008'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181008'>臣陶言：五月二十日准进奏院递到敕一道至衡州，伏蒙圣恩，就差臣知邛州军州，兼管内劝农事，臣即时祗受讫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181008_comment'></div>贬处遐方，无复全躯之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181008_comment'></div>生还旧里，乃叨守土之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181008_comment'></div>恩出非常，力同再造<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181008_comment'></div>伏念臣禀生寒陋，涉世迂疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181008_comment'></div>粗闻修己之方，窃有逢辰之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181008_comment'></div>熙宁拔士，早缘制策之采收；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181008_comment'></div>元祐择官，晚有禁涂之更践。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181008_comment'></div>乏深厚之文，以丹书典诰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181008_comment'></div>寡周密之虑，以出纳枢机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181008_comment'></div>责任太隆，施为奚称？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181008_comment'></div>方朝廷之政举，尝励翼以赴功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181008_comment'></div>逮朋党之论兴，亦沦胥而被谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181008_comment'></div>天高莫诉，罪大胡言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181008_comment'></div>羽翼伤摧，尤畏鹰鹯之搏逐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181008_comment'></div>梦魂惊悸，深忧斧钺之诛锄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181008_comment'></div>敢期废放之馀，遽玷宠光之异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181008_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下运乘天造，道并日升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181008_comment'></div>圣继圣以储休，光昭大庆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181008_comment'></div>新又新而作德，覃及群伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181008_comment'></div>尽成汤解网之心，广夏禹泣辜之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181008_comment'></div>哀怜谪籍，付畀郡章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181008_comment'></div>肉白骨以觊充盈，燃死灰而求炎焰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181008_comment'></div>生成至此，报效云何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1181008_comment'></div>臣敢不欣戴至仁，推明初政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1181008_comment'></div>承流以治，少希循吏之所先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1181008_comment'></div>击壤以歌，愿与齐民而共乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1181008_comment'></div>庶几晚节，无累洪钧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1181008_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　到邛州，有回启。作品：《回邛州知郡陈大夫启》<div id='poem_1181058' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181058' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181058?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回邛州知郡陈大夫启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181058")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181058_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181058'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181058'>比者祗命易麾，深惭异数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181058_comment'></div>及兹受代，愧继前良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181058_comment'></div>空传父老之谣，难奉子孙之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181058_comment'></div>重加礼意，曲示笺修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181058_comment'></div>拜惠何堪，瞻风愈切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181058_comment'></div>永以为好，言莫能胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181058_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1181058_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　上表乞守本官致仕。作品：《乞致仕表》<div id='poem_1181011' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181011' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181011?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞致仕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181011")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181011_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181011'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181011'>臣生长远方，逢值圣世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181011_comment'></div>擢皇祐进士，登熙宁制举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181011_comment'></div>元祐中尘冒侍从，绍圣初谪放江湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181011_comment'></div>伏遇皇帝陛下光绍宝图，诞敷鸿泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181011_comment'></div>昭洗过恶，叙复班联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181011_comment'></div>臣深欲勉竭疲驽，仰答造化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181011_comment'></div>而齿发衰暮，疾恙侵凌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181011_comment'></div>窃虑职事旷废，重取罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181011_comment'></div>伏望圣慈念臣今已七十四岁，旧感瘴疠，间或病作，心力昏耗，难以釐务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181011_comment'></div>伏乞特降指挥，许臣守本官致仕，庶几安养羸疢，遂其馀生。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1181011_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
三台（郪县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3f1f8f739f97453f8902c8045793303a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3f1f8f739f97453f8902c8045793303a");'><span id='3f1f8f739f97453f8902c8045793303a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，74岁</div><div id='3f1f8f739f97453f8902c8045793303a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年2月7日</a>　充集贤殿修撰、改差知梓州。有谢表。作品：《谢授再知梓州表》<div id='poem_1181009' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181009' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181009?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授再知梓州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年2月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181009")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181009_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181009'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181009'>臣陶言：先以罪分司南京、衡州居住，于元符三年四月准告落分司，差提举成都府玉局观；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181009_comment'></div>至五月内，准敕就差知邛州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181009_comment'></div>臣逐次谢恩祗受，及奉表以闻去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181009_comment'></div>至今年二月七日到绵州罗江县，又准告充集贤殿修撰，改差知梓州，臣即时望阙谢恩拜受者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181009_comment'></div>九殒之馀，忽逢再造；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181009_comment'></div>一年之内，辄易三迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181009_comment'></div>初备位于祠官，旋领麾于乡郡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181009_comment'></div>继忝集贤之命，仍分左蜀之符，并出异恩，悉还旧物，幸非所望，感莫能胜<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181009_comment'></div>伏念臣学不能美身，志未可适道，动踰涯分，易速悔尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181009_comment'></div>奋飞于畎亩，而滥陪英俊之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181009_comment'></div>涉猎于缣缃，而与闻朝廷之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181009_comment'></div>谓之才则尝践更于台阁，加之罪则久废放于江湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181009_comment'></div>小人持附会之心，乘而下石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181009_comment'></div>骚客有哀怜之兴，惟欲招魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1181009_comment'></div>累年趋必死之乡，一旦履复生之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1181009_comment'></div>荐沾殊泽，增贲馀龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1181009_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下光绍宝图，勃兴治道，大判忠邪之势，深权用舍之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1181009_comment'></div>虽众正在朝，足跨商周之盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1181009_comment'></div>而一夫失职，尚撄尧舜之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1181009_comment'></div>恤及衰残，概从收叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1181009_comment'></div>臣敢不究观否泰，省念初终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1181009_comment'></div>如痛定而反思，若途穷而利往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1181009_comment'></div>枕丘适愿，既知于瞑目之前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1181009_comment'></div>结草酬恩，敢惮于没身之后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1181009_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年3月17日</a>　到梓州任，有谢表。作品：《谢知梓州到任表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　上《谢两府启》<div id='poem_1181048' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181048' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181048?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢两府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23614, "北宋", "吕陶", "poem_title_1181048")'>吕陶</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1181048_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1181048'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181048'>自梓易淮，引方车而就道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181048_comment'></div>由楚得蜀，遽委辔以涖官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181048_comment'></div>释万里奔走之劳，享一旦里闾之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181048_comment'></div>清朝信道，特重远民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181048_comment'></div>使者观风，许临故国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181048_comment'></div>以可否利害知之有素，故廉按职任付而不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181048_comment'></div>廪禄所沾，仅周<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1181048", 1181048, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>贫属</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181048_comment'></div>松楸在望，尤慰永怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181048_comment'></div>事非近比之常，力本误知之及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181048_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官橐籥万类，权衡百工，故曲从私欲之所安，乃可责公家之后效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181048_comment'></div>陶谨当清心任事，刻己致忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1181048_comment'></div>莫敢或遑，冀少行其素业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1181048_comment'></div>每怀靡及，庶无负于斯人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1181048_comment'></div>倘吏最之有闻，则化钧之可报。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1181048_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　有谢提举常平薛寺丞启。作品：《谢梓州路提举常平薛寺丞启》<div id='poem_1181059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1181059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1181059?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢梓州路提举常平薛寺丞启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1181059'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1181059'>起于谪放，贲以宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1181059_comment'></div>还书殿之美名，领潼川之优寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1181059_comment'></div>适父老之愿，愧无术以承宣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1181059_comment'></div>事大夫之贤，将有依于庇赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1181059_comment'></div>恭惟某官文而饬治，政必养源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1181059_comment'></div>袭训范于枢庭，振猷为于使部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1181059_comment'></div>渊澄流洁，馀波有以载沾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1181059_comment'></div>纲举网疏，众目从而不紊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1181059_comment'></div>况有云霄之清议，岂惟堂构之高才？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1181059_comment'></div>即序禁涂，益敷远业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1181059_comment'></div>某息肩故里，引领下风，行遂参承，并伸感抃。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1181059_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
